# Normative Rule Traceability — Ade

> **Status:** Living architectural document. Regenerated by `/traceability`; not hand-edited.
> Per-project instance of `~/.claude/methodology/templates/traceability.md`.

> 206 rules in `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` at HEAD (`75f75da`).
> 54 CI scripts under `ci/ci_check_*.sh`.
> Source of truth: `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` (canonical, append-only).
> **Refresh note (HEAD `75f75da`, PHASE4-N-I full close — in-memory
> snapshot + replay-forward rollback; closes `DC-CONS-20` rollback-side
> `open_obligation`).**
> PHASE4-N-I (6 slices S1 → S6) closes the rollback-side half of
> `DC-CONS-20` (the receive-side header→body bridge's outstanding
> obligation from PHASE4-N-H) using the **Path A recursive scope split**:
> in-memory snapshot storage only; persistent on-disk `LedgerState`
> encoding is deliberately carved out to a follow-on cluster. The
> single BLUE driver `materialize_rolled_back_state`
> (`crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs`) materializes a
> rolled-back `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)` via one
> `SnapshotReader::nearest_le` lookup + `BlockSource::blocks_in_range`
> iteration + per-block `apply_block_with_verdicts` replay-forward
> fold; the BLUE `commit_rollback`
> (`crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/commit.rs`) atomically swaps the
> ChainDb tip + `LedgerState` + `PraosChainDepState` + pending-header
> cache with an irreversible-step-first staged shape (chain_write
> failure leaves state unchanged); the GREEN `InMemorySnapshotCache`
> + `ChainDbBlockSource` + `SnapshotCadence` provide the runtime
> infrastructure (`every_n_blocks` BLUE-structural cadence — no
> operator-tunable runtime input); the BLUE-edit receive reducer's
> `RollBackward` branch (S6) replaces the prior
> `Err(ReceiveError::RollbackOutOfScope)` with
> `materialize_rolled_back_state + commit_rollback`, producing a
> `RolledBack` effect when an in-memory snapshot is available and a
> structured `RollbackTooDeep` when not (no silent fallback). The
> registry moves **202 → 206 rules** (+4: `CN-STORE-07` from S2,
> `DC-CONS-22` from S2, `DC-STORE-07` from S4, `DC-CONS-21`
> declared-only at S1 carrying
> `open_obligation = "persistent_ledger_snapshot_encoding_follow_on_cluster"`);
> the CI count moves **52 → 54** (+2:
> `ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh` S2,
> `ci/ci_check_snapshot_cadence_purity.sh` S4). Family counts at HEAD
> `75f75da`: T: 29, DC: **85** (was 82, +3 — `DC-CONS-21`,
> `DC-CONS-22`, `DC-STORE-07`), CN: **75** (was 74, +1 —
> `CN-STORE-07`), OP: 9, RO: 8 — total **206**. **One existing rule
> is flipped enforced (the cluster's headline closure):** `DC-CONS-20`
> (ChainDb / ledger / chain_dep lockstep — admit + rollback) flips
> `declared → enforced`, removes its
> `open_obligation = "rollback_side_blocked_until_ledger_snapshot_cluster"`,
> gains `strengthened_in = ["PHASE4-N-I"]` (with
> `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-H"` preserved), gains the rollback-side
> code-locus (receive reducer roll_backward branch,
> `rollback/commit.rs::commit_rollback`,
> `rollback/materialize.rs::materialize_rolled_back_state`, plus the
> GREEN/RED runtime rollback infrastructure under
> `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/{cadence,in_memory_cache,chaindb_block_source,snapshot_writer}.rs`),
> gains 8 rollback-side tests (admit-side carry-forward + the new
> `commit_rollback_*`, `rollback_branch_*`, and the end-to-end
> `rollback_then_continue_admit_equals_straight_line_admit`), and
> gains `ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh` to its CI row
> alongside the existing `ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh`.
> **The cluster doc additionally CLAIMS strengthenings of `T-DET-01`,
> `DC-PROTO-09`, `CN-CONS-08` in its §"Replay obligations introduced
> by this cluster" — these are NOT yet reflected in those rules'
> `strengthened_in` arrays in the registry at HEAD `75f75da`. See
> §A0000000000000000 warning #1 below for the parent's review.**
> New BLUE authority surface: `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/` —
> 4 modules: `mod.rs`, `traits.rs` (`SnapshotReader` + `BlockSource`
> narrow read-only traits — production impls in `ade_runtime` go
> through the same single composition path); `error.rs` (closed
> `MaterializeError` + `CommitRollbackError` sums, total `class()`,
> exhaustive match — round-trip tested); `materialize.rs` (the sole
> `pub fn` returning `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)` in the
> rollback module tree, guarded by
> `ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh`); `commit.rs` (atomic
> state replacement with irreversible-step-first shape:
> `chain_write` first, then `ledger` + `chain_dep` swap, then
> pending-header cache reset — failure on the irreversible step leaves
> everything unchanged). New GREEN/RED runtime surface:
> `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/` — 5 modules: `mod.rs`,
> `cadence.rs` (`should_snapshot_after_block` pure decision +
> `SnapshotCadence { every_n_blocks: u32 }` BLUE-structural with no
> operator-tunable runtime field, guarded by
> `ci_check_snapshot_cadence_purity.sh`); `in_memory_cache.rs`
> (`InMemorySnapshotCache` `BTreeMap<SlotNo, (LedgerState,
> PraosChainDepState)>`-keyed impl of `SnapshotReader` — no `HashMap`,
> iteration is BTreeMap-ordered); `chaindb_block_source.rs`
> (`ChainDbBlockSource<'a, D: ChainDb>` impl of `BlockSource` — pure
> projection over an in-memory ChainDb); `snapshot_writer.rs` (S5
> snapshot-write orchestration hook called after each successful
> admission in the receive orchestrator; per-peer snapshot decisions
> are independent). New BLUE-edit: receive reducer's `RollBackward`
> branch (`crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs`) — the prior
> `Err(ReceiveError::RollbackOutOfScope)` placeholder is replaced
> with the materialize + commit composition (admit branch unchanged;
> the `RollbackOutOfScope` variant is retained in the closed
> `ReceiveError` sum for migration but is no longer constructed by
> any production path). `DC-CONS-21` (snapshot encode/decode
> round-trip equivalence) stays `status = "declared"` at cluster
> close with
> `open_obligation = "persistent_ledger_snapshot_encoding_follow_on_cluster"`:
> the persistent on-disk `LedgerState` encoder is ~1500-2000 LoC of
> field-walk code mirroring `ade_ledger::fingerprint`'s structure
> and is deliberately scoped to a follow-on cluster (Path A recursive
> scope decision, OQ-3 locked at sketch close). The in-memory scope
> still closes `CN-STORE-07`, `DC-CONS-22`, `DC-STORE-07`, and
> `DC-CONS-20` fully; persistence across restarts is the follow-on
> cluster's deliverable, NOT a regression. **Forbidden during this
> cluster (mechanically enforced):** any new `pub fn` returning
> `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)` outside
> `materialize_rolled_back_state` (CI:
> `ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh`); construction of
> `ReceiveError::RollbackOutOfScope` from the reducer's `RollBackward`
> arm (variant retained for migration but unused post-S6);
> `HashMap` / `HashSet` / wall-clock / `tokio` / `rand` in any BLUE
> rollback module; operator-tunable runtime cadence parameter in
> `SnapshotCadence`. All N-I registry entries carry full `code_locus`
> / `tests` / `ci_script` populated arrays (except `DC-CONS-21` which
> stays declared, with empty `code_locus`/`tests`/`ci_script` —
> permitted because the constitution-coverage gate does not require
> populated CI on `declared` entries). Bidirectional `cross_ref`s
> across the new rules: `CN-STORE-07` ↔ `DC-CONS-22` ↔ `DC-STORE-07`
> (within the cluster) and outward to `T-DET-01`, `DC-PROTO-09`,
> `CN-CONS-08`, `DC-CONS-20`. Constitution-coverage gate expected to
> PASS at 206 entries (no `status = "deprecated"` entries; one
> `declared` entry — `DC-CONS-21` — which is permitted). **Cluster
> directory:** `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-I/` (already
> archived at HEAD `75f75da` — 6 slice docs `N-I-S1.md` …
> `N-I-S6.md` + `cluster.md`).
> **Prior refresh note (HEAD `efe1fb9`, PHASE4-N-H full close — receive-side
> header→body bridge, admit-only Path A scope).**
> PHASE4-N-H (6 slices S1 → S6) closes the receive-side mirror of the
> producer-side server response paths shipped by PHASE4-N-G. Peer-supplied
> header+body bytes arriving via chain-sync `RollForward` (header cache)
> + block-fetch `BlockDelivered` (body) are admitted to `ChainDb` +
> `LedgerState` + `PraosChainDepState` **only** via Ade's own
> `block_validity` (B1) authority producing an `AdmittedBlock`
> private-constructor token. The receive bridge reducer
> (`ade_ledger::receive::reducer::receive_apply`) is a pure, total,
> deterministic transition over canonical `ReceiveEvent` inputs; a
> peer cannot switch headers between announcement and body delivery
> (header-body cross-check via `PendingHeaderCache`); a peer
> `RollBackward` returns `Err(ReceiveError::RollbackOutOfScope)` with
> receive state unchanged (Path A scope edge — full rollback authority
> is a follow-on cluster). The registry moves **196 → 202 rules** (+6:
> `CN-CONS-08` from S2, `DC-CONS-19` from S2, `DC-CONS-20` declared at
> S2 — admit-side enforced under `CN-CONS-08` + `DC-CONS-19` +
> `DC-PROTO-09`, rollback-side
> `open_obligation = "rollback_side_blocked_until_ledger_snapshot_cluster"`,
> `DC-PROTO-09` from S3, `CN-PROTO-07` from S1, `RO-LIVE-02` from S6);
> the CI count moves **47 → 52** (+5:
> `ci/ci_check_admitted_block_closure.sh` S1,
> `ci/ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh` S2,
> `ci/ci_check_receive_replay_purity.sh` S3,
> `ci/ci_check_receive_orchestrator_no_producer_dep.sh` S4,
> `ci/ci_check_receive_paths_corpus_present.sh` S6). Family counts at
> HEAD `efe1fb9`: T: 29, DC: **82** (was 79, +3 — `DC-CONS-19`,
> `DC-CONS-20`, `DC-PROTO-09`), CN: **74** (was 72, +2 — `CN-CONS-08`,
> `CN-PROTO-07`), OP: 9, RO: **8** (was 7, +1 — `RO-LIVE-02`) — total
> **202**. **One existing rule is strengthened in the registry**:
> `DC-PROTO-06.strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-H` (negotiated protocol
> version is threaded through the receive-role surface via per-peer
> `PerPeerReceiveState` carried on every reducer call site by the RED
> receive orchestrator — never read from RED ambient context). **The
> `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-H/cluster.md` Replay-obligations
> section additionally claims strengthenings of `T-DET-01`, `T-ENC-01`,
> `DC-CONS-13`, `DC-CONS-16`, `CN-CONS-07`; these claims are NOT yet
> reflected in those rules' `strengthened_in` arrays in the registry
> at HEAD `efe1fb9` — see §A000000000000000 warning #1.** The new
> BLUE authority surface introduced by this cluster:
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/admitted.rs` (`AdmittedBlock`
> private-constructor token + `admit_via_block_validity` — the single
> admission authority; the receive-side analog of the producer-side
> `AcceptedBlock`, deliberately a distinct type so producer/receive
> gates do not interfere),
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/events.rs` (closed `ReceiveEvent` /
> `ReceiveEffect` / `ReceiveError` sums — `ReceiveEvent` has exactly
> 3 variants `RollForward` / `RollBackward` / `BlockDelivered`, all
> peer-originated; no constructor for `RequestNext` / `RequestRange`
> / `ClientDone` / `FindIntersect` exists in the public API),
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/pending_header_cache.rs`
> (`PendingHeaderCache` — `BTreeMap<(SlotNo, Hash32), Vec<u8>>` —
> deterministic, no `HashMap`, no eviction at this layer; eviction
> is a deterministic RED concern injected as canonical input at the
> orchestrator side),
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/chain_write.rs` (`ChainDbWrite`
> narrow trait — `write_admitted` takes `AdmittedBlock` by value so
> no path can persist raw bytes),
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs` (`ReceiveState` +
> `receive_apply` — pure total deterministic transition;
> `RollForward` branch caches the header without mutating any
> sub-state; `BlockDelivered` branch decodes the body, looks up the
> cached header at `(slot, block_hash)`, errors `HeaderBodyMismatch`
> on absent / mismatched cache, then runs `admit_via_block_validity`
> and commits via the `ChainDbWrite` trait; `RollBackward` returns
> `Err(RollbackOutOfScope)` with state unchanged).
> New GREEN adapter surface:
> `crates/ade_runtime/src/receive/events_to_state.rs` (pure adapter
> lifting RED-decoded mini-protocol signals/events into `ReceiveEvent`
> values — no I/O), `crates/ade_runtime/src/receive/in_memory_chain_write.rs`
> (`ChainDbWrite` impl backed by `InMemoryChainDb` — pure projection
> over an in-memory ChainDb). New RED orchestrator surface:
> `crates/ade_runtime/src/receive/orchestrator.rs` (per-peer dispatch;
> the gate `ci_check_receive_orchestrator_no_producer_dep.sh` forbids
> any import of `crate::producer::signing` / `producer::broadcast` /
> `producer::scheduler`). New operator-action binary:
> `crates/ade_core_interop/src/bin/live_block_follow_session.rs`
> (`#[ignore]`-default in CI; `--hermetic` mode prints readiness;
> `--connect <addr>` mode requires a private cardano-node peer and
> captures CE-N-H-6 evidence). New mechanical adapter:
> `crates/ade_runtime/tests/receive_pipeline_corpus_drive.rs` (CE-N-H-5
> — every Conway-576 corpus block admits through the full receive
> pipeline; ChainDb tip matches expected `(slot, hash)`; stored bytes
> equal corpus bytes byte-identically; `LedgerState` fingerprint
> changes on admission; closes `RO-LIVE-02` mechanical pre-condition).
> **`RO-LIVE-02` (cardano-node peer follow → ChainDb tip equals peer
> tip) is `partial` WITH open_obligation for the live half**: the
> mechanical pre-condition (`receive_pipeline_corpus_drive`) is fully
> enforced via S5's mechanical adapter +
> `ci/ci_check_receive_paths_corpus_present.sh`; the live half (real
> cardano-node peer follow over N blocks) lives in CE-N-H-6's
> **operator-action live evidence**: an operator must run
> `live_block_follow_session --connect <addr>` against a private
> cardano-node and append the captured log path to
> `RO-LIVE-02.evidence_notes`. **Reopen criteria:** when an operator
> peer is available, run the binary per
> `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-H/CE-N-H-6_PROCEDURE.md` and
> commit the log. The procedure mirrors PHASE4-N-C/CE-N-C-8 and
> PHASE4-N-G/CE-N-G-8 — this is the **OP-OPS-04 / CN-CONS-06 /
> RO-LIVE-01 precedent** reused (enforced + `open_obligation` for a
> follow-on operator-action artifact). **`DC-CONS-20` (ChainDb /
> ledger / chain_dep lockstep) stays `status = "declared"` at
> cluster close** with
> `open_obligation = "rollback_side_blocked_until_ledger_snapshot_cluster"`:
> the admit-side half is enforced under `CN-CONS-08` + `DC-CONS-19` +
> `DC-PROTO-09`; the rollback-side half is OUT OF SCOPE for this
> cluster — ledger rollback infrastructure does not exist (no
> `LedgerState` encode/decode, no snapshot+replay-forward driver). A
> follow-on rollback cluster will close DC-CONS-20's rollback half;
> until then the receive bridge returns
> `Err(ReceiveError::RollbackOutOfScope)` on any peer `RollBackward`
> and receive state stays consistent. This is a deliberate Path A
> scope split (OQ-1 decision), NOT an enforcement gap to surprise the
> next reader. All N-H registry entries carry full `code_locus` /
> `tests` / `ci_script` populated arrays plus bidirectional
> `cross_ref`s. Constitution-coverage gate expected to PASS at 202
> entries (no `status = "deprecated"` entries). **Cluster
> directory:** `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-H/` (already
> archived at HEAD `efe1fb9` — 6 slice docs `N-H-S1.md` …
> `N-H-S6.md` + `cluster.md` + `CE-N-H-6_PROCEDURE.md`).
> **Prior refresh note (HEAD `a280954`, PHASE4-N-G full close — producer-side
> server response paths).**
> PHASE4-N-G (7 slices S1 → S7) closes the producer-side server
> response half of the bounty: the producer's chain-sync server
> announces headers and its block-fetch server hands the body bytes
> back when a Haskell peer issues `RequestRange`. Every byte that
> leaves BLUE via the server pump is sourced from an `AcceptedBlock`
> that already cleared the `CN-CONS-07` self-accept gate, threaded
> through a single `ServedChainSnapshot` keyed in `BTreeMap` order,
> projected via the single canonical `accepted_block_header_bytes`
> splitter (no parallel header recipe), and tagged Server-agency at
> the type level by closed `ServerReply<M>` wrappers (client-agency
> variants are unrepresentable in the public API). The registry moves
> **190 → 196 rules** (+6: `DC-CONS-17/18` from S4/S3, `DC-PROTO-07/08`
> from S6/S3, `CN-PROTO-06` from S1, `RO-LIVE-01` from S7); the CI
> count moves **40 → 47** (+7: `ci/ci_check_no_parallel_header_splitter.sh`
> S1, `ci/ci_check_served_chain_closure.sh` S2,
> `ci/ci_check_chain_sync_server_closure.sh` S3,
> `ci/ci_check_block_fetch_server_closure.sh` S4,
> `ci/ci_check_broadcast_to_served_purity.sh` S5,
> `ci/ci_check_n2n_server_no_signing_dep.sh` S6,
> `ci/ci_check_server_paths_corpus_present.sh` S7). Family counts at
> HEAD `a280954`: T: 29, DC: **79** (was 75, +4), CN: **72** (was 71,
> +1), OP: 9, RO: **7** (was 6, +1) — total **196**. **Five existing
> rules are strengthened**: `T-DET-01.strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`
> (the full producer-side session orchestrator — chain-sync server +
> block-fetch server + GREEN broadcast-to-served adapter + served-chain
> projection — is a deterministic surface over canonical inputs:
> `DC-PROTO-07` makes session-transcript replay byte-identical and
> `DC-CONS-17/18` close the served-bytes/header-recipe authority);
> `T-ENC-01.strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G` (the wire bytes a peer
> receives are byte-identical to `AcceptedBlock.as_bytes()` / its
> canonical header sub-slice — never re-encoded by the server pump;
> `DC-CONS-17` + `DC-CONS-18` make Cardano's canonical block-envelope
> bytes the only wire authority on the server-role surface);
> `DC-CONS-16.strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G` (the validator's existing
> header/body byte split is now the SINGLE canonical splitter —
> `ci_check_no_parallel_header_splitter.sh` enforces that the only
> `pub fn *_header_bytes` in the workspace is
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs::accepted_block_header_bytes`,
> shared with the producer's `ServedHeaderLookup::next_after`);
> `CN-CONS-07.strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G` (the broadcast gate is
> now preserved across the network seam via `ServedChainSnapshot`:
> only `AcceptedBlock` values may enter the served-chain index, and
> only served-chain entries can be projected onto the wire — the
> network seam can no longer be an end-run around the self-accept
> gate); `DC-PROTO-06.strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G` (selected
> protocol version is threaded through the producer-side server-role
> surface via per-peer `PerPeerN2nServerState` — never read from RED
> ambient context). **`RO-LIVE-01` (Haskell node fetches Ade-forged
> block bytes) is enforced WITH open_obligation for the live half**:
> the mechanical pre-condition (`cross_impl_server_pipeline` — every
> served `Block{bytes}` decodes via Ade's envelope+block decoder and
> the recomputed body-hash matches the announced header's body_hash
> field) is fully enforced via S7's mechanical adapter +
> `ci_check_server_paths_corpus_present.sh`; the live cross-impl
> claim (a real cardano-node `RequestRange` over a private TCP peer
> accepts the served bytes) is by-design out of reach of any CI gate
> against the synthetic corpus and lives in CE-N-G-8's
> **operator-action live evidence**: an operator must run
> `live_block_fetch_session --connect <addr>` against a private
> Haskell peer and append the captured log path to
> `RO-LIVE-01.evidence_notes`. **Reopen criteria:** when the operator
> peer is available, run the binary per
> `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-G/CE-N-G-8_PROCEDURE.md` and
> commit the log. The procedure mirrors PHASE4-N-C/CE-N-C-8 — this is
> the **OP-OPS-04 / CN-CONS-06 precedent** reused (enforced +
> `open_obligation` for a follow-on operator-action artifact), NOT a
> regression or unhonest closure. New BLUE authority surface
> introduced by this cluster:
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/served_chain.rs`
> (`ServedChainSnapshot` BTreeMap-ordered index keyed on
> `(slot, hash)`, `served_chain_admit` total/closed admission,
> `range_bytes` / `block_bytes` accessors returning
> `AcceptedBlock.as_bytes()` slices verbatim, `next_after_header_bytes`
> for chain-sync RollForward header projection),
> `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs`
> (`producer_chain_sync_serve` + `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip` —
> pure, total, deterministic; `ServerReply<ChainSyncMessage>`
> closed wrapper with private inner enum, exhaustive match prove the
> closure), `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs`
> (`producer_block_fetch_serve` — pure, total, deterministic;
> `ServerReply<BlockFetchMessage>` closed wrapper),
> `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs::accepted_block_header_bytes`
> (the single canonical header projection — promoted from a
> validator-private helper to a workspace-level single authority).
> New GREEN adapter surface:
> `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/broadcast_to_served.rs`
> (`drain_and_admit` — pure, deterministic, ordered admission from
> `BroadcastQueue` into `ServedChainSnapshot`; no I/O),
> `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_lookups.rs`
> (`ServedRangeLookup` + `ServedHeaderLookup` trait impls that
> forward to `ServedChainSnapshot` accessors). New RED orchestrator:
> `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/n2n_server.rs` (per-peer
> session pump under `PerPeerN2nServerState` carrying the negotiated
> version typed parameter; no signing-module dependency, enforced by
> `ci_check_n2n_server_no_signing_dep.sh`). New operator-action
> binary: `crates/ade_core_interop/src/bin/live_block_fetch_session.rs`
> (`#[ignore]`-default in CI; `--hermetic` mode prints readiness;
> `--connect <addr>` mode requires a private cardano-node peer and
> captures CE-N-G-8 evidence). New mechanical adapter:
> `crates/ade_runtime/tests/cross_impl_server_pipeline.rs` (CE-N-G-7
> — every served `Block{bytes}` decodes through Ade's envelope+block
> decoder and the recomputed body-hash matches the announced header's
> body_hash field; closes `RO-LIVE-01` mechanical pre-condition).
> All N-G registry entries carry full `code_locus` / `tests` /
> `ci_script` populated arrays plus bidirectional `cross_ref`s to
> `T-DET-01`, `T-ENC-01`, `DC-CONS-16`, `DC-PROTO-06`, `CN-CONS-07`.
> Constitution-coverage gate expected to PASS at 196 entries (no
> `status = "deprecated"` entries). **Cluster directory:**
> `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-G/` (already archived at HEAD
> `a280954` — 7 slice docs + `cluster.md` + `CE-N-G-8_PROCEDURE.md`).
> **Prior refresh note (HEAD `694dd74`, PHASE4-N-C full close — block production
> closure, Tier 1 producer half).**
> PHASE4-N-C (7 slices S1 → S7) closes the block-production half of the
> bounty: forge a Conway block deterministically over a canonical
> `ProducerTick` (BLUE), self-accept it through Ade's own N-B header
> validator + B1 body validator (BLUE bridge gate), and cross-impl-deliver
> it to cardano-node via N2N. Private-key custody stays in RED throughout;
> BLUE consumes signed artifacts (`VrfProof`, `KesSignature`, `OpCert`)
> only — replay never invokes RED signing, replay corpora never carry
> private keys. The registry moves **176 → 190 rules** (+14:
> `DC-CRYPTO-03/04/05` from S1, `DC-CONS-11/12` from S2, `DC-CONS-13/14/15`
> + `DC-LEDGER-12` from S3, `DC-CONS-16` from S4, `CN-CONS-07` from S5,
> `OP-OPS-04/05` from S6, `CN-CONS-06` from S7); the CI count moves **32 →
> 40** (+8: `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh` S1, `ci/ci_check_opcert_closed.sh`
> S2, `ci/ci_check_forge_purity.sh` + `ci/ci_check_no_private_keys_in_corpus.sh`

> total **176**. The new rule `DC-LEDGER-11` (`status = "enforced"`,
> `introduced_in = "PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE"`) records that
> `proposal_procedures` MUST NOT remain an opaque byte field in the
> authoritative Conway tx-body shape: `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` is
> typed `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>` (was `Option<Vec<u8>>`), decoded
> through the single closed entry point `decode_proposal_procedures` that
> rejects unknown `gov_action` tags, structural failures, empty sets, and
> trailing garbage deterministically; the typed form re-encodes byte-identically
> (`PreservedCbor`) for every well-formed Conway tx body. The decoder reuses
> the existing closed `GovAction` enum (preserving the `DC-LEDGER-10`
> `UpdateCommittee` discriminant — the structured `{removed, added, threshold}`
> with `StakeCredential` cold members survives this decode) and the existing

> tx-body-grammar rule. The new CI script

> **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK (committee enactment wired at the epoch
> boundary) close** *strengthens* **two** existing rules **AGAIN** — `DC-EPOCH-01`
> (Conway governance timing / enactment atomicity) and `DC-LEDGER-10` (credential
> key/script discriminant fidelity) — **NO new rule, NO new CI script**. The

> existing `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` was *extended* —
> sections 7 + a write-back-wiring check — not added). This is the cluster that
> makes the previously-dormant committee-enactment effect **live**: committee
> enactment is now wired at the epoch boundary
> (`ade_ledger::governance::apply_committee_enactment`, called from
> `ade_ledger::rules`). A ratified `NoConfidence` action **dissolves the
> committee**; a ratified `UpdateCommittee` action **removes/adds discriminated
> cold members and sets the new quorum** (previously the committee was cloned
> unchanged, silently dropping ratified committee changes). `DC-EPOCH-01`
> (`strengthened_in += ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK`) gains the wired
> `apply_committee_enactment` Code surface, the
> `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` CI gate, and **four** new tests
> (`enact_noconfidence_dissolves_committee`,
> `enact_update_committee_applies_changes`,
> `committee_enactment_replays_byte_identical`,
> `epoch_boundary_ratified_noconfidence_dissolves_committee`); it stays
> `status = "partial"` because the governance-Plutus oracle is still deferred to
> CE-88. `DC-LEDGER-10` (`strengthened_in += ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK`):
> the discriminated committee credential now **survives the live enactment
> write-back** — `GovAction::UpdateCommittee` is structured (`{removed:
> BTreeSet<StakeCredential>, added: BTreeMap<StakeCredential,u64>, threshold}`,
> replacing opaque raw bytes), the snapshot-loader decode is fail-closed on an
> unknown credential tag, and the write-back path itself preserves the tag — not
> just the dormant type. Its `tests` array grows from 14 to **19** with five
> tests (`update_committee_decodes_removed_added_threshold`,
> `update_committee_keyhash_scripthash_members_distinct`,
> `update_committee_decode_rejects_malformed`,
> `update_committee_structured_fields_change_fingerprint`,
> `enact_update_committee_keyhash_scripthash_distinct`), all confirmed to exist as
> functions in the codebase at HEAD `3180e27`. The gate
> `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` was extended (sections 7 +
> write-back-wiring check); `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` PASSES (173
> entries). This close **resolves the prior OQ5 follow-up (d) write-back risk** as
> a now-live, discriminant-preserving enactment; the remaining `DC-LEDGER-10`
> follow-ups are only (e) the GREEN loader `mk_credential` older-helper unknown-tag
> default (contained to `ade_testkit`) and (b) the `shelley/cert.rs` unknown-cert
> zero-hash `KeyHash` placeholder. **Surfaced enforcement gap (unchanged class):**

> `EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` (`ade_ledger::governance`) is re-typed
> `Option<(Vec<Hash28>, Vec<(Hash28, u64)>)>` →
> `Option<(Vec<StakeCredential>, Vec<(StakeCredential, u64)>)>`, so when committee
> enactment (`UpdateCommittee`) is eventually wired it **cannot re-collapse the
> discriminated committee map on write-back**. The field stays **dormant** (`None`

> (`EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` stays `StakeCredential`-typed);
> `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` PASSES (173 entries). This close
> **resolves OQ5 follow-up (d)**; the remaining `DC-LEDGER-10` follow-ups are now
> only (e) the GREEN loader `mk_credential` unknown-tag default to `KeyHash`

---

## Conventions

- **Source of rules.** The canonical, append-only source is the invariant
  registry at `.idd-config.json` `invariant_registry`
  (`docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml`). The registry was renamed from
  `constitution_registry.toml` in the post-Phase-4-N-D IDD-canonicalization
  delta (`ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` was repointed in `39865f6`).
  Every `[[rules]]` entry whose `status` is not explicitly retired appears
  below. None are deprecated at HEAD.
- **Rule IDs** are stable across regenerations and immutable per
  registry doctrine. They are reproduced exactly as the registry holds them.
- **Families.** The registry groups rules under five family-letter
  prefixes:

  | Prefix | Family |
  |---|---|
  | `T-` | True invariants (project constitution §2) |
  | `DC-` | Derived Cardano compatibility invariants (§3) |
  | `CN-` | Classification-table invariants (`classification_table.md`) |
  | `RO-` | Release obligations (§4a) |
  | `OP-` | Operational invariants (§4b) |

  Within each family, level-3 sub-headings hold one rule each. The
  sub-section ID *is* the rule ID. Within a family, ordering follows
  the registry file order. The `DC-CONS-*` sub-family (8 rules
  introduced by PHASE4-N-B) appears at the end of the `DC-` section in
  registry file order.
- **Four-cell contract.** Every rule carries the canonical four-row table:
  Source, Requirement, Code, Tests, CI. Where the registry has populated
  `code_locus`, `tests`, `ci_script`, those fields drive the row. A row
  marked `_(no enforcement found — gap)_` corresponds to a registry
  entry whose `status` is `declared` (no enforcement promised) or to a
  partial entry that has not yet pointed at a code/test/CI artifact.
- **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY close (credential key/script discriminant fidelity).**
  This cluster introduced **1 new `DC-LEDGER-10` rule** (`status = "enforced"`) and
  back-referenced it bidirectionally from `T-DET-01`, `T-ENC-03`, `DC-LEDGER-08`,
  `DC-LEDGER-09`, `DC-TXV-05`. `DC-LEDGER-10` *strengthens* `T-DET-01` (the
  discriminated `StakeCredential`/`ConwayGovState` representation is a deliberate,
  oracle-confirmable cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration) and `T-ENC-03`
  (the credential decoders round-trip the key/script discriminant rather than
  erasing it), and *relates* `DC-LEDGER-08`/`DC-LEDGER-09` (the cert-state and
  gov-state these rules accumulate are now keyed on the discriminated credential)
  and `DC-TXV-05` (required-signer / witness closure resolves credentials by
  discriminated identity). The new authority surface is
  `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (`StakeCredential` closed 2-variant enum
  `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}` + `hash()` accessor — replaces the tuple-struct
  `StakeCredential(Hash28)`), `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/cert.rs` +
  `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (`decode_stake_credential` preserves the
  tag, rejects unknown), `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`ConwayGovState`
  re-keyed to `StakeCredential`), `gov_cert.rs`/`governance.rs`/`cert_classify.rs`/
  `rules.rs` (`cred.hash()` boundary adapter for the `Hash28`-keyed stake
  snapshot), and `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`write_stake_credential`
  emits discriminant+hash; gov-map writers use it; the stake-snapshot writer stays
  `write_hash28` by design). The GREEN testkit
  `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` preserves the tag in its
  gov-map + DRep-reg parses. **One new CI script landed** —
  `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` (anchored on `DC-LEDGER-10`),
  bringing the total to **29**. OQ5 carries one environment-blocked open
  obligation (the real-chain discriminated-credential agreement vs cardano-node's
  `Credential`-keyed UMap/VState, reclassified per tier doctrine), declared
  non-goals (withdrawal/required-signer/address credential discriminant, the
  `Hash28`-keyed stake-distribution snapshot, the Byron credential surface), and
  two declared per-cluster-security-review follow-ups bounded to those non-goal
  surfaces (committee member/vote discrimination; the Shelley unknown-cert
  zero-hash placeholder). This close also **resolves the prior OQ-5 declared
  follow-up on `DC-LEDGER-09`** — OQ-5 graduates into the enforced `DC-LEDGER-10`.
  See §A000000 and §G #21, #23.
- **PHASE4-B5 close (Conway governance-certificate accumulation authority).**
  Cluster PHASE4-B5 introduced **1 new `DC-LEDGER-09` rule** (`status = "enforced"`)
  and **strengthened `DC-LEDGER-08`** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B5`): B5 makes the
  governance certs B4 owner-tagged to `ConwayGovState` **applied** rather than
  observed-and-dropped, retiring `DC-LEDGER-08`'s "routed out-of-mutation-scope"
  disposition for governance certs. The new authority surface is
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/gov_cert.rs` (`apply_conway_gov_cert`, native gov dispatch
  total over 18 tags), `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`GovCertEnv` +
  `LedgerState::gov_cert_env()` fail-fast constructor),
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` (`ConwayOnlyDepositParams.drep_activity`),
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (`ValidationEnvironmentError::{MissingDRepActivityParam,
  DRepActivityOverflow}`), `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs`
  (`accumulate_tx_certs` / `process_block_certificates` thread
  `Option<ConwayGovState>`, apply the gov half, carry `gov_state` forward through
  `apply_block` — replaces the B4 observe-and-drop), and
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (gov-state + `drep_activity` fingerprint
  surface — a deliberate, oracle-confirmable migration making `ConwayGovState` a
  deterministic function of boundary-base + replayed block-stream cert effects).
  **One new CI script landed** — `ci/ci_check_gov_cert_accumulation_closed.sh`
  (anchored on `DC-LEDGER-09`), bringing the total to **28**. The B5 close also
  **RESOLVES the prior §G #18 bidirectional-cross_ref defect** (the gate now PASSES
  at HEAD `651adc9`, 172 entries — verified during this refresh). B5 carries one
  environment-blocked open obligation (the real epoch-576 VState oracle, reclassified
  per tier doctrine) and two declared separable follow-ups (OQ-3 committee-membership
  tx-validity gate; OQ-5 credential key/script discriminant collapse). See §A00000
  and §G #18–#21.
- **PHASE4-B2 close (tx validity agreement).** Cluster PHASE4-B2
  (single-transaction validity; the body authority's per-tx half) introduced
  **5 new `DC-TXV-*` rules** (`DC-TXV-01..05`, all `enforced`), flipped
  **`DC-MEM-01` and `DC-MEM-02`** `declared -> enforced` (the mempool gained a
  real `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/` BLUE module), and strengthened **6
  pre-existing rules** by appending `PHASE4-B2` to `strengthened_in`:
  `DC-LEDGER-05` and `CN-LEDGER-09` (Conway vkey-witness binding — fail-closed
  Ed25519 coverage over the preserved body hash), `DC-VAL-06` (wrong-size
  vkey/sig now `MalformedWitnessField` on the tx path; unresolvable inputs
  fail-fast), `DC-LEDGER-02` (GREEN no-false-accept tx adversarial corpus),
  `T-ENC-01` (`tx_id` lifted byte-for-byte from the body slice, never
  re-encoded), and `T-DET-01` (tx verdict-surface replay over the Conway-576
  corpus). The new authority surface is `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/`
  (closed `TxValidityVerdict`/`TxRejectClass`/`TxValidityError`,
  `transition.rs` phase-1 ∧ phase-2 composition with phase-1-first fail-fast,
  `required_signers.rs` closed era-versioned `SignerSource` enumeration over
  every signer source, `witness.rs` fail-closed coverage over the preserved
  body hash, `phase1.rs` decode + state-backed checks) and the mempool BLUE
  module `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/{admit,policy}.rs` (closed `AdmitOutcome`
  / `OrderPolicy`; admission verdict equals `tx_validity` verdict; overload
  policy never changes a verdict). The GREEN corpus harnesses live at
  `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/`. **No new CI script landed in B2** —
  every `DC-TXV-*` / `DC-MEM-*` rule carries
  `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (extended in B2 to scan
  `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/` and `ade_ledger/src/mempool/` for closed
  structured verdicts/outcomes) plus its test surface. The same close
  **populated the previously-empty `ci_script`** on every enforced `DC-CONS-*`
  and `DC-VAL-*` rule with `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`, which is what
  flips `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` from FAIL to **PASS** at HEAD
  (the coverage gate requires a non-empty `ci_script` on every `enforced`
  entry). The earlier "documented deposit/refund value-conservation gap" — the
  Conway state-backed coin-conservation check conservatively skipping txs
  carrying certificates or withdrawals — was **CLOSED in PHASE4-B3-S4**. The
  cert/withdrawal early-out was removed from
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation` (the
  source comment at the function header explicitly records "PHASE4-B3-S4
  removed the deposit/withdrawal early-out that was the cluster's known
  false-accept path"); the full preservation-of-value equation
  (`Σ(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == Σ(outputs) + fee + donation + new_deposits`)
  now runs for cert/withdrawal-bearing Conway txs, with deposit amounts
  sourced canonically via `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-07`. See §H (kept for
  provenance) and `T-CONSERV-01` / `CN-LEDGER-07`.
- **PHASE4-B1 close (full block validity agreement).** Cluster PHASE4-B1
  (block validity agreement; dependency root for B2/B3) introduced **6 new
  `DC-VAL-*` rules** (`DC-VAL-01..06`, all `enforced`) and strengthened **6
  pre-existing rules** by appending `PHASE4-B1` to `strengthened_in` and wiring
  the new block-validity surface: `T-DET-01` (verdict-surface replay over the
  Conway-576 positive corpus), `DC-CRYPTO-01` (Praos single-VRF input +
  leader/nonce range extension, op-cert-signable fix), `DC-CONSENSUS-02`
  (`LedgerView` projection), `DC-LEDGER-02` (GREEN no-false-accept adversarial
  corpus), `CN-CONS-04` (recomputed body-hash binding + VRF-keyhash binding),
  and `CN-EPOCH-01` (`consensus_view` projection). The new authority surface is
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` (closed `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict +
  `FieldKind`/`FieldError` fail-closed field taxonomy, `transition.rs`
  header∧body composition, `header_input.rs` body-hash binding),
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/{consensus_input_extract,consensus_view}.rs` (pure
  canonical-input projection), `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs`
  (`expect_size` fail-closed header crypto-field guard), and the GREEN harnesses
  `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/{replay,adversarial,corpus,ledger_view}.rs`.
  **No new CI script landed in B1** — every `DC-VAL-*` rule carries an empty
  `ci_script` and is discharged by its test surface plus structural CI
  (`ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`, `ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`,
  `ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh`); see §A0 and §G for the surfaced CI gaps.
  The earlier "documented Conway body-witness verification gap" (recorded in
  `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` and the corresponding
  README) was **CLOSED in PHASE4-B2-S1 (CE-B2-1)**: per-tx Ed25519 vkey-witness
  verification over the preserved body hash is wired into the body path via
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs::verify_required_witnesses`
  (L78), called from `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs:258` and `:342` via
  `verify_conway_witness_closure`. The gap is no longer carried forward; see
  `DC-LEDGER-05` / `CN-LEDGER-09` / `DC-TXV-05` for the closed surface.
- **PHASE4-N-B close (consensus runtime).** Cluster N-B (Praos consensus
  runtime, 10 slices S-B1..S-B10) introduced **8 new DC-CONS-* rules**
  (`DC-CONS-03..10`) and strengthened **11 pre-existing rules** by
  populating `code_locus`/`tests`/`ci_scripts` arrays and appending
  `PHASE4-N-B` to `strengthened_in`. Four new CI scripts landed —
  `ci/ci_check_no_chaindb_in_consensus_blue.sh`,
  `ci/ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`,
  `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`,
  `ci/ci_check_no_density_in_fork_choice.sh` — each rule-ID-anchored
  via its header comment. The strengthened rules are: `DC-CONSENSUS-01`
  (partial → enforced), `DC-CONSENSUS-02` (declared → partial),
  `DC-CRYPTO-01` (enforced, augmented test surface), `CN-CRYPTO-02`
  (declared → partial), `CN-EPOCH-01` (declared → partial),
  `DC-EPOCH-02` (enforced, augmented for consensus-side HFC),
  `CN-CONS-01..05` (each `declared` with code_locus/tests/ci wired),
  `DC-CORE-01` (declared, strengthened over ade_runtime::consensus),
  `T-DET-01` (enforced, consensus subset closed via stream replay),
  `T-CORE-02` (enforced, augmented by `ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`).
  Two new crates accompanied the work — `ade_core::consensus` is the
  BLUE consensus surface (16 modules under
  `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/`) and `ade_core_interop` is a RED
  live-peer driver crate gated by `#[ignore]` in CI by default. The
  GREEN orchestrator that threads N-A inputs through BLUE transitions
  lives at `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/{chain_selector,candidate_fragment,genesis_parser}.rs`.
- **Phase 4 N-A CI closure (PHASE4-N-A close).** Cluster N-A (Ouroboros
  mini-protocols, 11 protocols across N2N+N2C) strengthened four
  pre-existing registry rules with new tests against real cardano-node
  11.0.1 captures and synthetic agency traces: `T-ENC-03`, `CN-WIRE-07`,
  `DC-PROTO-02`, `DC-PROTO-05`. One new CI script —
  `ci/ci_check_ce_n_a_5_proof.sh` — exercises all 5 conditions of the
  CE-N-A-5 proof obligation. Two new registry IDs (`DC-CORE-01`,
  `DC-PROTO-06`) were added by the cluster — see their entries below.
- **Phase 4 N-D CI closure (`78da6c9`).** Three CI scripts —
  `ci/ci_check_chaindb_contract.sh`, `ci/ci_check_recovery_contract.sh`,
  `ci/ci_check_chaindb_crash_safety.sh` — flipped nine
  recovery/storage rules `declared → enforced`: `T-REC-01`, `T-REC-02`,
  `DC-STORE-01`, `DC-STORE-02`, `DC-STORE-03`, `DC-STORE-05`,
  `CN-STORE-03`, `CN-STORE-04`, `CN-STORE-05`. `DC-STORE-04` remains
  `declared` by design — see §B for the Tier 5 divergence note.
- **CI script BLUE scope (closed at `5b70bee`).** All seven BLUE-scoped
  CI scripts hard-code the full six-crate BLUE list `{ade_codec,
  ade_types, ade_crypto, ade_core, ade_ledger, ade_plutus}` declared
  by `.idd-config.json` plus the 9 BLUE `ade_network` submodule paths.
  No `_(scope gap)_` markers remain.

## T — True Invariants (Project Constitution §2)

### `T-DET-01`: Same canonical inputs → same authoritative bytes

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2; `comparison_surface_contract.md` (Byte Authority Model §3). PHASE4-B5 adds `DC-LEDGER-09` to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): the `ConwayGovState` fingerprint migration — gov state as a deterministic function of boundary-base + replayed block-stream cert effects rather than a frozen snapshot — is a deliberate, oracle-confirmable `T-DET-01` surface. **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY adds `DC-LEDGER-10`** to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): the discriminated `StakeCredential` makes `CertState`/`ConwayGovState` key on the key/script discriminant and `fingerprint::write_stake_credential` serializes it, so two states differing only in a credential's tag fingerprint differently — a deliberate, oracle-confirmable cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration. **PHASE4-N-C adds `DC-CRYPTO-03`, `DC-CRYPTO-04`, `DC-CONS-13`, `DC-CONS-14`** to this rule's `cross_ref`: VRF/KES signing transcripts are byte-identical to cardano-node references (the RED-confined `vrf_prove` / `kes_sign` produce captured signed artifacts that BLUE consumes); the BLUE producer's `forge_block` is pure over `ProducerTick` (`DC-CONS-13`) and replays byte-identically across two replays of the same tick stream (`DC-CONS-14`), making the producer surface a deterministic function of canonical inputs. `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-C`. **PHASE4-N-G adds `DC-PROTO-07`, `DC-CONS-17`, `DC-CONS-18`** to this rule's `cross_ref`: the full producer-side session orchestrator (chain-sync server + block-fetch server + GREEN broadcast-to-served adapter + served-chain projection) is a deterministic surface over canonical inputs (`negotiated_version, peer_message_sequence, broadcast_arrival_sequence, session_event_sequence`); `DC-PROTO-07` makes session-transcript replay byte-identical and `DC-CONS-17/18` close the served-bytes/header-recipe authority. `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`. |
| **Requirement** | Replaying the same canonical inputs against the same prior state must yield byte-identical authoritative outputs. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`apply_block*` family), `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (canonical per-component state hash; PHASE4-B3 adds a Conway-gated deposit-param fold to `fingerprint_pparams` — non-Conway states fingerprint byte-identically, Conway states fold in the canonical deposit params, see `DC-TXV-07`); plus PHASE4-N-B consensus surface — `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/encoding.rs` (canonical state encoding with deterministic op-cert counter map iteration) and `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/chain_selector.rs` (GREEN orchestrator that drives BLUE transitions deterministically); plus PHASE4-B1 verdict-surface replay — `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/replay.rs` (GREEN harness replaying `block_validity` over the 14-block Conway-576 positive corpus); plus PHASE4-B2 tx verdict-surface replay — `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/` (GREEN harness `replay_tx_validity` driving the BLUE `tx_validity` over every extracted Conway-576 corpus tx twice, surfaces byte-identical); plus PHASE4-N-C producer-surface replay — `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` (BLUE `forge_block` pure over `ProducerTick`; no wall-clock, no rand, no `HashMap`, no I/O), `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/state.rs` (`ProducerTick` canonical input value carrying slot + ledger_state + mempool_snapshot + pparams + vrf_proof + kes_sig + opcert), `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/replay.rs` (GREEN harness `producer_replay_fixtures` — replays a `ProducerTick` stream twice using captured signed artifacts and asserts `Vec<ForgedBlockBytes>` byte-identical, never invoking RED signing).; plus PHASE4-N-G server-role transcript-determinism surface — `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` (`producer_chain_sync_serve` + `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip` — pure, total, deterministic), `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs` (`producer_block_fetch_serve` — pure, total, deterministic), `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/broadcast_to_served.rs` (GREEN `drain_and_admit` — pure, no I/O, deterministic over arrival-sequence), `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_lookups.rs` (pure trait-impl projections). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/ledger_determinism.rs::apply_block_deterministic`; per-era `byron_determinism`, `shelley_determinism`, `allegra_determinism`, `mary_determinism`, `alonzo_determinism`, `babbage_determinism`, `conway_determinism`; plus consensus subset closed via `crates/ade_testkit/tests/consensus_stream_replay.rs::{synthetic_session_replays_identically, synthetic_session_event_kinds_match_corpus, synthetic_session_final_state_matches_corpus, op_cert_regression_header_rejected_mid_stream}` (CE-N-B-5) and the canonical state-roundtrip battery `crates/ade_core/tests/praos_state_canonical_roundtrip.rs::{layout_is_stable, roundtrip_empty_state, roundtrip_genesis_state, roundtrip_populated_state, roundtrip_chain_event_all_variants, roundtrip_chain_selection_reject_all_variants, op_cert_counter_map_iteration_is_deterministic}`; plus PHASE4-B1 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_positive_corpus.rs::verdict_stream_replays_identically` (the block-validity verdict surface replays byte-identically over the Conway-576 corpus); plus PHASE4-B2 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_positive_corpus.rs::tx_verdict_stream_replays_identically` (the tx-validity verdict surface replays byte-identically over the Conway-576 corpus); plus PHASE4-B3 `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs::tests::{pparams_fingerprint_stable_for_non_conway, pparams_fingerprint_includes_conway_deposits_when_present}` (the Conway deposit-param fold is byte-identical for non-Conway states and stable when present); plus PHASE4-N-C `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/replay.rs::tests::{forge_block_pure_no_io, forge_block_replay_byte_identical}` (the producer surface replays byte-identically over a canonical `ProducerTick` stream without invoking RED signing — see `DC-CONS-13` / `DC-CONS-14`).; plus PHASE4-N-G `producer_chain_sync_serve_replays_byte_identical_over_corpus`, `producer_block_fetch_serve_replays_byte_identical_over_corpus`, `drain_and_admit_is_deterministic_over_arrival_sequence`, `session_transcript_replay_byte_identical` (the producer-side session transcript is byte-identical across two replays over the same canonical input sequence — see `DC-PROTO-07`). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` (BLUE forbidden patterns, all 6 BLUE crates), `ci/ci_check_ledger_determinism.sh` (replay equivalence), `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (PHASE4-N-B — no `#[non_exhaustive]`, no `Other`/`Unknown` open-tail variants, no owned `String` or `Box<dyn>` in `ade_core::consensus`). Strengthened for PHASE4-N-B, again for PHASE4-B1 (block-validity verdict-surface replay), again for PHASE4-B2 (tx-validity verdict-surface replay), and again for PHASE4-N-C (producer-surface replay — `ci/ci_check_forge_purity.sh` defends `forge_block` purity; `ci/ci_check_no_private_keys_in_corpus.sh` defends the replay-corpus property that no private-key material appears in fixtures). `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-C`. Strengthened again for PHASE4-N-G (server-role transcript determinism — `ci/ci_check_chain_sync_server_closure.sh`, `ci/ci_check_block_fetch_server_closure.sh`, and `ci/ci_check_broadcast_to_served_purity.sh` each defend the purity / no-async / no-HashMap / no-wall-clock posture of the producer-side server reducers + the GREEN adapter — see `DC-PROTO-07`). `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`. |

### `T-ENC-01`: Canonical encoding for persisted/hashed/transmitted data

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2. Strengthened by PHASE4-B1 (block body hash over preserved CBOR), PHASE4-B2 (`tx_id` over preserved body slice), and PHASE4-N-C (the producer's forged-header `body_hash` MUST equal `blake2b_256(forged_body_wire_bytes)` produced by the single Cardano-compatible canonical block-body encoder used by the validator hash path — `DC-CONS-16` makes producer and validator hash the same bytes through the same encoder; `T-ENC-01.cross_ref += DC-CONS-16`). `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-C`. |
| **Requirement** | All persisted, hashed, or transmitted authoritative bytes use a single canonical encoding; hash-critical bytes are taken from the preserved wire segment, never re-encoded. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/preserved.rs` (`PreservedCbor<T>`, `pub(crate)` constructor); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs` (PHASE4-B1 — block body hash computed over the preserved CBOR segment bytes, never re-encoded; PHASE4-N-C-S4 — `computed_body_hash` is now a consumer of the single canonical recipe in `block_body_hash.rs`, no validator-private body encoder); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/phase1.rs` (PHASE4-B2 — `decode_tx`: `tx_id = blake2b_256` of the body slice lifted byte-for-byte from the full tx CBOR, never a re-encode); plus PHASE4-N-C `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_body_hash.rs` (S4 unification — `block_body_hash` + `block_body_hash_from_buckets` are the single canonical authority used by both the producer's `forge_block` (consumer at `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs`) and the validator's body-hash recomputation (consumer at `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs`); see `DC-CONS-16`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/...::preserved_wire_bytes_returned_exactly`; `crates/ade_ledger/...::altered_body_rejected_by_hash_binding`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_compose.rs::tx_id_uses_preserved_bytes`; plus PHASE4-N-C `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_body_hash.rs::tests::{block_body_hash_pinned_recipe_byte_identical, block_body_hash_from_block_equals_from_buckets, block_body_hash_none_invalid_txs_equals_empty_bucket, forged_body_hash_matches_validator_recomputation, body_encoder_is_single_authority}` (the single canonical recipe is byte-identical across producer + validator consumers and the encoder authority is unique). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_hash_uses_wire_bytes.sh` — scans all 6 BLUE crates `{ade_codec, ade_types, ade_crypto, ade_core, ade_ledger, ade_plutus}` for `hash(canonical_*)` patterns; plus PHASE4-N-C `ci/ci_check_no_producer_body_encoder.sh` — FAILs CI if a producer-private body encoder reappears (i.e. if anything other than `block_body_hash`/`block_body_hash_from_buckets` is used to compute a body hash on the producer or validator path; `DC-CONS-16` single canonical authority). Status remains `partial` (canonical-encoding surface not yet fully covered; the `tx_id`-preserved-bytes property is proven by test only). `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-C`. Strengthened again for PHASE4-N-G: `ci/ci_check_no_parallel_header_splitter.sh` enforces that the only `pub fn *_header_bytes` in the workspace is `accepted_block_header_bytes`; `ci/ci_check_broadcast_to_served_purity.sh` enforces that the GREEN broadcast-to-served adapter sources header/body bytes only through `ServedChainSnapshot` (no re-encode site outside the canonical recipe); `ci/ci_check_block_fetch_server_closure.sh` enforces that `Block{bytes}` payloads come only from `served.range_bytes`. `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`. |

### `T-ENC-03`: Round-trip identity

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2, D-3. **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY adds `DC-LEDGER-10`** to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): both era credential decoders preserve the key/script discriminant rather than erasing it, so `decode_stake_credential` round-trips the tag — `encode(decode(bytes)) == bytes` extends to the credential-type discriminant. |
| **Requirement** | For all valid encodings, `encode(decode(bytes)) == bytes`. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/preserved.rs`; plus per-protocol codecs `crates/ade_network/src/codec/{handshake,n2c_handshake,chain_sync,block_fetch,tx_submission,keep_alive,peer_sharing,local_chain_sync,local_tx_submission,local_state_query,local_tx_monitor}.rs` (PHASE4-N-A S-A2). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/...::full_corpus_round_trip` — 10,500 contiguous blocks across 7 eras; per-protocol synthetic `codec::<proto>::tests::roundtrip_every_variant` across all 11 mini-protocols (S-A2); plus six real-capture corpora harvested from cardano-node 11.0.1 — `handshake_real_capture_corpus`, `chain_sync_real_capture_corpus`, `block_fetch_real_capture_corpus`, `keep_alive_real_capture_corpus`, `peer_sharing_real_capture_corpus` (preprod local), `n2c_handshake_real_capture_corpus::real_capture_round_trips_byte_identical`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_cbor_round_trip.sh` (block-corpus round-trip); `ci/ci_check_ce_n_a_5_proof.sh` (CE-N-A-5 condition 3 — real-capture round-trip across 6 captured mini-protocols). |

### `T-CORE-02`: Forbidden nondeterminism

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2, D-2 through D-5. |
| **Requirement** | No wall-clock, unseeded randomness, floats, `HashMap`/`HashSet`/`IndexMap`, `tokio`, `async fn`, or nondeterministic collections may appear in BLUE code. |
| **Code** | All six BLUE crates carry `#![deny(unsafe_code)]`, `#![deny(clippy::unwrap_used)]`, `#![deny(clippy::expect_used)]`, `#![deny(clippy::panic)]`, `#![deny(clippy::float_arithmetic)]` in `lib.rs`. PHASE4-N-B narrows further: `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/*` uses Rational arithmetic (e.g. `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/vrf_cert.rs`) and never f32/f64 — verified by `ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`. |
| **Tests** | _(structural — enforced by lint + CI text scans)_; consensus-scoped Rational evidence in `crates/ade_core/tests/vrf_cert_threshold.rs::{taylor_exp_cmp_le_zero_x_returns_false, taylor_exp_cmp_le_x_equals_one_returns_true, taylor_exp_cmp_le_monotone_in_x, is_leader_determinism, is_leader_known_vector_matches_reference}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` — scans `{ade_codec, ade_types, ade_crypto, ade_core, ade_ledger, ade_plutus}` for `HashMap`, `HashSet`, `IndexMap`, `SystemTime`, `Instant`, `std::fs`, `std::net`, `tokio`, `async fn`, `f32`/`f64`, `anyhow`, `rand::thread_rng`, `thread::spawn`, plus `unsafe` outside an allowlist. PHASE4-N-B added `ci/ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh` — narrowly scans `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/` for `f32`/`f64` tokens, redundant with `forbidden_patterns` for `ade_core` but pinned to the consensus tree to anchor `DC-CONS-{07,08,09}`. |

### `T-REC-01`: Recovery is replay-equivalent

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2. |
| **Requirement** | Restart must produce byte-identical authoritative state to a clean replay. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/recovery.rs` (snapshot + forward-replay, S-36); `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/crash_safety.rs` (kill-strategy framework, S-37). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/recovery.rs::recover_from_snapshot_and_replay_forward`, `recover_from_genesis_when_no_snapshot`, `apply_failure_surfaces_with_slot`, `snapshot_decode_failure_surfaces_as_error`, `snapshot_with_no_post_blocks_is_ok`; `crates/ade_runtime/tests/stress_kill_harness.rs::stress_kill_smoke`, `stress_kill_1000`, `snapshot_table_intact_after_kill_loop`; `crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/crash_safety.rs::persistent_passes_crash_safety_with_no_kill`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_recovery_contract.sh`, `ci/ci_check_chaindb_crash_safety.sh`. Flipped `declared → enforced` in `78da6c9`. |

The full-equation accept/reject property has no dedicated conservation-corpus CI gate — proven by the named tests; see §G. |

### `DC-CRYPTO-01`: Crypto matches Haskell node on KAT

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-CORE-01`, `T-DET-01`. |
| **Requirement** | Crypto verification is pure and matches the Haskell node on all test vectors. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_crypto/src/`; plus PHASE4-N-B consensus-side VRF wrapper `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/vrf_cert.rs` (typed 41-byte Praos VRF input + Rational threshold check). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_crypto/...::blake2b_256_rfc_test_vectors`, `ed25519_rfc_8032_test_1`, `vrf_ietf_draft03_section_a3`; plus PHASE4-N-B consensus integration tests `crates/ade_core/tests/vrf_cert_threshold.rs::{verify_vrf_cert_accepts_valid_proof, verify_vrf_cert_rejects_wrong_alpha, verify_vrf_cert_rejects_malformed_proof}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_crypto_vectors.sh`. Strengthened for PHASE4-N-B (S-B3 typed VRF input — 8-byte BE slot ‖ 32-byte epoch nonce ‖ 1-byte role tag, NONCE=0x4E / LEADER=0x4C — built by a single audited function so callers cannot accidentally cross domains). Strengthened again for PHASE4-B1 (Praos single-VRF input + op-cert-signable fix proven against 14 real Conway headers); `ci_check_crypto_vectors.sh` remains the gate. |

### `DC-CRYPTO-03`: VRF signing transcript equivalence and verification symmetry

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-VRF-1/2/3); IETF `draft-irtf-cfrg-vrf-03` (Praos VRF). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `T-KEY-01`, `DC-CRYPTO-04`, `OP-OPS-04`. |
| **Requirement** | For canonical inputs `(slot, epoch_nonce, vrf_signing_key, vrf_role)` the RED signer produces a `VrfProof` byte-identical to cardano-node's reference output, and the emitted `VrfProof` verifies under `ade_crypto::vrf::verify_praos_vrf` with the matching verification key. Private-key execution is RED-shell confined; BLUE consumes the `VrfProof` as a captured signed artifact. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs::vrf_prove` (RED-confined VRF prove primitive; BLUE never reaches this). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs::tests::{vrf_prove_matches_reference_vectors, vrf_prove_then_verify_round_trip}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S1, anchored on `DC-CRYPTO-03/04/05` + `OP-OPS-04`) — FAILs CI if signing primitives appear outside `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/` (RED scope) or if a `*::sign_*` / `*::prove` symbol is referenced from any BLUE crate. |

### `DC-CRYPTO-04`: KES signing transcript equivalence and verification symmetry

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-KES-1); Cardano `Sum6KES` specification (depth-6 sum composition over ed25519). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `T-KEY-01`, `DC-CRYPTO-03`, `DC-CRYPTO-05`, `DC-CONS-11`, `OP-OPS-04`. |
| **Requirement** | For canonical inputs `(kes_secret, period, msg)` the RED signer produces a `KesSignature` byte-identical to reference and verifying under `ade_crypto::kes::verify_kes`. Private-key execution is RED-shell confined; BLUE consumes the `KesSignature` as a captured signed artifact. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs::kes_sign` (RED-confined KES sign primitive); `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes.rs` (`KesSignature` BLUE wire type + `verify_kes_signature` verify-only). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs::tests::{kes_sign_matches_reference_vectors, kes_sign_then_verify_round_trip}`; `crates/ade_crypto/src/kes.rs::tests::{kes_signature_from_bytes_round_trips, verify_kes_signature_agrees_with_existing_verify_kes}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S1). |

### `DC-CRYPTO-05`: KES evolution discipline (one-way; no replay)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-KES-2); Cardano `Sum6KES` specification. PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `DC-CRYPTO-04`, `T-KEY-01`, `OP-OPS-04`. |
| **Requirement** | `evolve(k_i) -> k_{i+1}` is one-way. The evolved key signs period `i+1` and MUST NOT sign for period `i`. RED `kes_sign` is forbidden when the requested period `> current_period + evolutions_remaining`; `kes_evolve` is forbidden when `to < from` or `to > from + evolutions_remaining`. Forward secrecy is a RED-shell discipline; BLUE has no recovery path if RED violates it. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs::{kes_update, kes_sign}` (RED-confined evolution + sign with period guards). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs::tests::{kes_update_chain_matches_reference, kes_sign_rejects_period_past_evolutions_remaining, kes_update_rejects_backwards_evolution}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S1). |

### `DC-LEDGER-02`: Same inputs → byte-identical ledger state

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-DET-01`. Strengthened by PHASE4-B1 (block adversarial corpus) and PHASE4-B2 (tx adversarial corpus). |
| **Requirement** | Same genesis plus same blocks must yield byte-identical ledger state; no mutation of a real block or tx ever yields `Valid` (no false accept). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs`, `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs`; plus PHASE4-B1 `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (GREEN no-false-accept block adversarial corpus — deterministic mutators M1–M6 derive adversarial blocks from the real Conway-576 corpus; no mutation ever yields `Valid` through `block_validity`); plus PHASE4-B2 `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/adversarial.rs` (GREEN no-false-accept tx adversarial corpus — deterministic witness/value/input mutations replay byte-identically through `tx_validity`, no mutation ever yields `Valid`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/..::utxo_state_deterministic`, `all_eras_determinism_summary`, `boundary_fingerprint_matches_pins`; plus PHASE4-B1 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_adversarial_corpus.rs::{no_mutation_is_ever_valid, adversarial_replays_identically}`; plus PHASE4-B2 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_adversarial_corpus.rs::{no_mutation_is_ever_valid, each_mutation_maps_to_expected_class, adversarial_replays_identically}` (no false accept across the adversarial cases). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_ledger_determinism.sh`, `ci/ci_check_differential_divergence.sh`. Status = `partial` (boundary-snapshot precision; per-block live differential deferred to external harness). Strengthened for PHASE4-B1 (block no-false-accept corpus) and PHASE4-B2 (tx no-false-accept corpus) — no new CI script. |

### `DC-EPOCH-01`: Conway governance timing

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-CAUSAL-01`, `T-EPOCH-01`. **Strengthened by ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK** (`strengthened_in += ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK`): committee enactment is now wired at the epoch boundary (previously the committee was cloned unchanged, silently dropping ratified committee changes). Stays `status = "partial"` — the governance-Plutus oracle is still deferred to CE-88. |
| **Requirement** | Proposals accumulate during the epoch; ratification and enactment are atomic at the epoch boundary; pulsing distributes DRep stake computation across the epoch. ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK makes the committee half of enactment atomic-at-boundary: a ratified `NoConfidence` dissolves the committee, a ratified `UpdateCommittee` removes/adds discriminated cold members and sets the new quorum — applied as a pure transition at the boundary, never mid-epoch. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (`enact_proposals`; **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK** `apply_committee_enactment` — pure transition: `NoConfidence` dissolve + discriminated `UpdateCommittee` remove/add + quorum); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (epoch-boundary apply site — calls `apply_committee_enactment` on the ratified committee action, ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK-S2). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/..::conway_epoch_boundary_end_to_end`, `crates/ade_ledger/...::conway_governance_ratification_test`; plus **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK** (4 new) `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs::{enact_noconfidence_dissolves_committee, enact_update_committee_applies_changes, committee_enactment_replays_byte_identical}` (a ratified `NoConfidence` dissolves the committee; a ratified `UpdateCommittee` removes/adds the discriminated members and sets the quorum; committee enactment replays byte-identically) and `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::epoch_boundary_ratified_noconfidence_dissolves_committee` (the epoch-boundary apply site dissolves a committee on a ratified `NoConfidence`). All 4 confirmed to exist as functions in the codebase at HEAD `3180e27`. **+1 since `3d94c22` (commit `b9cfaf9`, real-chain oracle):** `crates/ade_testkit/tests/epoch_oracle_comparison.rs::committee_oracle_mainnet_575_576_noop_agreement` — drives the mainnet Conway 575/576 ledger-state snapshots (snapshot-gated; skips when corpus absent) through our ratification + enactment and asserts no-op write-back agreement: cardano-node enacted no committee change across the boundary, and `apply_committee_enactment` fabricates none. Reclassifies the prior environment-blocked no-op case to **reality-blocked** for the positive committee-CHANGE case (mainnet enacted no `UpdateCommittee`/`NoConfidence` in this range, so no snapshot pair has a committee delta to diff). Confirmed to exist as a function at HEAD `168ac02`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` (ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK — sections 7 + the write-back-wiring check defend the committee-enactment write-back surface; this is now `DC-EPOCH-01`'s `ci_script`). _(Surfaced enforcement gap, now narrower: the real-chain committee **no-op** agreement is now ORACLE-CONFIRMED at the mainnet Conway 575→576 boundary by `committee_oracle_mainnet_575_576_noop_agreement` (`crates/ade_testkit/tests/epoch_oracle_comparison.rs`, commit `b9cfaf9`) — our loader parses the 7-member `ScriptHash` interim committee exactly, and our ratification + enactment reproduces the epoch-576 committee with no spurious mutation. The positive committee-CHANGE case is **reality-blocked**, not environment-blocked (mainnet enacted no `UpdateCommittee`/`NoConfidence` in this range, so no snapshot pair exhibits a committee delta to diff). The governance-Plutus oracle (CE-88) is the other deferred half keeping the rule at `status = "partial"`. Recorded in the registry `authority_surface`; status stays `partial`. See §A0000000000 and §G #30.)_ |

### `DC-STORE-07`: Snapshot cadence determinism (BLUE-structural, no operator-tunable runtime input)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/ledger-snapshot-rollback-invariants.md` §1 (I-8). PHASE4-N-I new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `tier = "derived"`). Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `DC-PROTO-09`. |
| **Requirement** | The decision to take a snapshot at slot S is a pure function of `(slot, block_no, cadence_params, last_snapshot)`. Same canonical input chain history produces the same set of snapshot slot keys. Cadence is BLUE-structural; not operator-tunable in this cluster (operator-tunable cadence is out of scope until represented as anchored, replay-derivable runtime data). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/cadence.rs` (`should_snapshot_after_block` pure decision; `SnapshotCadence` has only the `every_n_blocks: u32` BLUE-structural field — no `Duration`, no operator-tunable runtime input); `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/in_memory_cache.rs` (`InMemorySnapshotCache` `BTreeMap`-keyed impl of `SnapshotReader` — no `HashMap`, iteration is BTreeMap-ordered); `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/chaindb_block_source.rs` (`ChainDbBlockSource<'a, D: ChainDb>` impl of `BlockSource` — pure projection). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/cadence.rs::tests::{should_snapshot_after_block_every_n_returns_true_at_cadence, should_snapshot_after_block_returns_false_off_cadence, should_snapshot_after_block_returns_false_when_already_at_or_after_slot, should_snapshot_after_block_is_pure, snapshot_cadence_default_is_100_blocks}`; `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/in_memory_cache.rs::tests::{in_memory_snapshot_cache_nearest_le_returns_largest_key, in_memory_snapshot_cache_iteration_is_btreemap_ordered}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_snapshot_cadence_purity.sh` (PHASE4-N-I-S4, anchored on `DC-STORE-07`) — FAILs CI if `SnapshotCadence` gains any field beyond `every_n_blocks` (no operator-tunable runtime input), if `cadence.rs` / `in_memory_cache.rs` / `chaindb_block_source.rs` introduce `HashMap` / `HashSet` / wall-clock / `tokio` / `rand`, or if the cadence decision becomes non-pure. |

### `DC-QUERY-01`: Version-gated era-aware N2C queries
