### `DC-LEDGER-08`: Closed/total Conway cert-state accumulation (fail-closed)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL certificate tags 0..18; delegation/pool state transitions); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B4 new rule (`status = "enforced"`); **strengthened by PHASE4-B5** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B5`). Cross-refs `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-06`, `DC-LEDGER-07`, `T-DET-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, **`DC-LEDGER-09`** (now bidirectional — `DC-LEDGER-09` lists `DC-LEDGER-08` back), and **`DC-LEDGER-10`** (OQ5 — added bidirectionally; the cert-state this rule accumulates is now keyed on the discriminated `StakeCredential`, `DC-LEDGER-10` lists `DC-LEDGER-08` back). |
| **Requirement** | Conway cert-state accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition: certificates decode through the era-correct closed grammar (Conway via `decode_conway_certs` retaining all owner payloads, tags 0..18) selected by explicit era dispatch — never the Shelley 6-variant decoder on Conway bytes, never reduced into the 7-variant Shelley `Certificate`, never with payload fields dropped. Every certificate resolves to an owner-tagged disposition: it mutates B4-owned `CertState` (delegation/pool), or it is owner-tagged to `ConwayGovState` and routed out-of-mutation-scope (observed, not swallowed), or it is a structured reject (`NotValidInEra` for removed tags 5/6, `Malformed` for bad CBOR, `UnsupportedUntilStateOwner` only for genuinely-ownerless cases). Composite certs (tags 10/12/13) carry both a B4-owned mutation and an owner-tagged governance effect; both are represented. No certificate is flattened to neutral, decode-dropped, or apply-swallowed; a decode or apply error propagates as a structured `LedgerError` and halts the block transition. Incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. (Wiring the owner-tagged `ConwayGovState` effects into applied governance state is PHASE4-B5, not B4. **As of PHASE4-B5 this disposition is strengthened: governance certs are no longer observed-and-dropped but applied to `ConwayGovState` — see `DC-LEDGER-09`.**) |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` (owner-complete `ConwayCert` — every variant retains its owner payloads); `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (`PoolRegistrationCert.owners`); `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (`decode_conway_certs` payload retention + `decode_drep`, total over tags 0..18); `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/cert.rs` (shared `read_pool_registration_cert`) — PHASE4-B4-S1 decoder-completeness clause; `crates/ade_ledger/src/delegation.rs` (`apply_conway_cert` + the owner-tagged `ConwayCertAction` / `ConwayCertOutcome` apply model, total over the 18 tags) — PHASE4-B4-S2 apply-totality clause; `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`accumulate_tx_certs`, era-dispatched fail-closed — the Conway path runs the Conway decoder + apply model, the Shelley path the Shelley decoder; a decode or apply `Err` propagates and halts, never swallowed) — PHASE4-B4-S3/S4. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_decode_complete.rs::{each_tag_retains_owner_payloads, drep_grammar_total}` (decoder completeness — every tag retains its owner payloads, DRep grammar total); `crates/ade_ledger/src/delegation.rs::tests::{conway_cert_action_total, apply_outcome_agrees_with_action, removed_tag_rejects_as_era_invalid, drep_registration_is_owner_tagged_not_applied}` (apply model total + owner-tagged routing); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::tests::{era_dispatch_conway_accumulates_via_conway_path, era_dispatch_shelley_accumulates_via_shelley_path, conway_decode_error_is_fail_closed, conway_unknown_tag_is_fail_closed, conway_removed_tag_is_fail_closed, conway_apply_error_is_fail_closed, conway_governance_cert_routed_out_of_scope}` (era dispatch + fail-closed propagation + governance routing); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/cert_state_corpus.rs::{positive_synthetic_cert_state_accumulates, cert_state_replay_byte_identical, adversarial_no_false_accept}` (synthetic positive accumulation, byte-identical replay, adversarial no-false-accept — the B4 cert-state corpus, distinct from the same-named conservation-adversarial test). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` — extended in PHASE4-B4-S3/S4 to guard the cert-state fail-open swallow: it FAILs CI if the `"non-fatal during replay"` rationale string reappears anywhere under `crates/`, and if `accumulate_tx_certs` in `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` contains an `Err(_)` swallow arm. Gate PASSES at HEAD `ee35493` (verified during this refresh, exit 0). _(Enforcement gap, surfaced honestly — see §A0000: the real epoch-576 cert-state-vs-cardano-node oracle is **environment-blocked** (the epoch-576 UMap snapshot is absent post-extraction; see `corpus/cert_state/README.md`). Reclassified environment-blocked per tier doctrine — identical to the documented open obligation on `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-03`. Mechanical closure IS shipped — owner-complete decode + total owner-tagged apply + era-dispatched fail-closed accumulation + synthetic positive / replay / adversarial corpus; real-chain agreement remains the open obligation.)_ |

### `DC-LEDGER-09`: Closed/total Conway governance-certificate accumulation (fail-closed)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL governance cert tags 9..18; `CONWAY` CERTS/GOVCERT/COMMITTEE transitions; CIP-1694); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B5 new rule (`status = "enforced"`). Cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-08`, `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-06`, `T-DET-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, and (OQ5) **`DC-LEDGER-10`** — all bidirectional at HEAD `a3ee2da` (the six target rules list `DC-LEDGER-09` back). OQ5 graduates `DC-LEDGER-09`'s prior OQ-5 `open_obligation` declared follow-up into the enforced `DC-LEDGER-10`: the `ConwayGovState` keys this rule accumulates are now the discriminated `StakeCredential`, not bare `Hash28`. |
| **Requirement** | Conway governance-certificate accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition into `ConwayGovState`: every governance-affecting Conway cert that B4 owner-tagged to `ConwayGovState` (vote-delegation tags 9/10/12/13 → `vote_delegations`; committee tags 14/15 → `committee_hot_keys`; DRep tags 16/17/18 → `drep_expiry`) resolves to exactly one explicit `ConwayGovState` mutation or a structured reject — never observed-and-dropped, never flattened, never with payload fields lost. B5 mutates only governance-owned fields; it does not touch B4-owned `CertState` and does not double-apply the delegation/pool half of composite certs (10/12/13). DRep expiry is computed only from an explicit gov-env (current epoch + `drepActivity`); a missing required env input is a structured fail-fast (`MissingDRepActivityParam`), never a defaulted expiry; expiry arithmetic is checked (`DRepActivityOverflow`). A cert that cannot be applied propagates a structured `LedgerError` and halts the block transition; incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. `ConwayGovState` becomes a deterministic function of (boundary-loaded base then replayed block-stream cert effects) rather than a frozen snapshot — a deliberate, oracle-confirmable fingerprint migration (`T-DET-01`). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/gov_cert.rs` (`apply_conway_gov_cert` — native gov dispatch over `ConwayCert`, total over the 18 tags, no `_ =>` wildcard) — PHASE4-B5-S2; `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`GovCertEnv` + `LedgerState::gov_cert_env()`, the sole fail-fast `GovCertEnv` constructor) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` (`ConwayOnlyDepositParams.drep_activity`) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (`ValidationEnvironmentError::MissingDRepActivityParam`, `DRepActivityOverflow`) — PHASE4-B5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`accumulate_tx_certs` / `process_block_certificates` thread `Option<ConwayGovState>`, apply the gov half, carry `gov_state` forward through `apply_block` — replaces the B4 observe-and-drop) — PHASE4-B5-S3; `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (gov-state + `drep_activity` fingerprint surface). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/gov_cert.rs::tests::{gov_apply_total_over_18_tags, composite_gov_half_applied_once_certstate_untouched_by_b5, drep_expiry_uses_epoch_plus_activity, env_free_gov_certs_need_no_env, drep_register_missing_env_is_fail_fast, drep_expiry_overflow_is_fail_closed, gov_apply_is_deterministic}` (total gov dispatch, composite single-apply, DRep-expiry from env, env-free certs need no env, env fail-fast, overflow fail-closed, determinism); `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs::tests::{gov_cert_env_present_ok, gov_cert_env_missing_drep_activity_is_fail_fast}` (env constructor present + fail-fast); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::tests::{gov_accumulation_applies_drep_registration_into_gov_state, gov_apply_error_halts_accumulation}` (block-path accumulation applies into gov state + halts on error); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/gov_state_corpus.rs::{positive_synthetic_gov_state_accumulates, gov_state_accumulation_replays_byte_identical, adversarial_drep_register_update_missing_env_rejected, adversarial_drep_expiry_overflow_rejected, adversarial_decode_layer_rejects_guard_gov_path, adversarial_double_resign_is_deterministic}` (synthetic positive accumulation, byte-identical replay, and the four adversarial no-false-accept / fail-fast / determinism corpus tests). All 17 confirmed to exist as functions at HEAD `651adc9`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_gov_cert_accumulation_closed.sh` — **new in PHASE4-B5**, anchored on `DC-LEDGER-09` in its header comment. It FAILs CI if (1) `apply_conway_gov_cert`'s match over `ConwayCert` gains a `_ =>` wildcard arm (adding a `ConwayCert` variant must break the build, never silently drop a governance effect); (2) the B4 observe-and-drop returns — the "routed out of B4 mutation scope" comment must not reappear and `accumulate_tx_certs` must call `apply_conway_gov_cert`; (3) the DRep-expiry env fail-fast is removed — `MissingDRepActivityParam` must exist and `gov_cert_env()` must be the only `GovCertEnv` constructor. Gate PASSES at HEAD `651adc9` (verified during this refresh, exit 0). Plus `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` (bidirectional `cross_ref` enforcement — now PASSES with `DC-LEDGER-09`/`DC-LEDGER-08` bidirectional). _(Enforcement gap, surfaced honestly — see §A00000 and §G #19: the real epoch-576 governance-state (VState)-vs-cardano-node oracle is **environment-blocked** (the epoch-576 UMap/ledger snapshot is absent post-extraction; see `corpus/gov_state/README.md`, `corpus/cert_state/README.md`, `corpus/validity/conway_epoch576/README.md`). Reclassified environment-blocked per tier doctrine — identical to the documented open obligations on `DC-LEDGER-08` / `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-03`. Mechanical closure IS shipped — native total gov dispatch + env fail-fast + checked DRep-expiry arithmetic + block-path accumulation + synthetic positive/replay/adversarial corpus; real-chain agreement remains the open obligation. **Two declared separable follow-ups (NOT part of this closure):** OQ-3 — the GOVCERT committee-membership tx-validity gate (§G #20); OQ-5 — `ConwayGovState` keys gov state on bare `Hash28` and the codec collapses the key/script credential discriminant (`ade_codec` `decode_stake_credential` drops the type tag), so a key-hash and script-hash credential sharing 28 bytes are indistinguishable in `vote_delegations`/`committee_hot_keys`/`drep_expiry`; cardano-node keys on the full discriminated `Credential`. Pre-existing decoder behaviour newly promoted to authority by B5, tracked per the per-cluster security review (§G #21).)_ |

### `DC-LEDGER-10`: Credential key/script discriminant fidelity

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (`Credential = key|script` across UTXOW/DELEG/GOVCERT; CIP-1694); IDD illegal-states-unrepresentable + determinism doctrine. OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY new rule (`status = "enforced"`); **strengthened by COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY, AGAIN by DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY, AGAIN by ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY** (`strengthened_in = ["COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY", "DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY", "ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY", "ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK"]` — the committee-credential, DRep-voter, dormant committee-enactment-effect, and now the **live committee-enactment write-back** halves of the same discriminant-fidelity work; still one rule, still `enforced`, no new rule added by any strengthening). Origin: the PHASE4-B5 per-cluster security review (WARN/MEDIUM) + `DC-LEDGER-09`'s `open_obligation` (the prior §G #21 OQ-5 declared follow-up — now graduated into this enforced rule). Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `T-ENC-03`, `DC-LEDGER-08`, `DC-LEDGER-09`, `DC-TXV-05`, **and `DC-LEDGER-11` (PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE, added bidirectionally — the new typed Conway `proposal_procedures` decode preserves the `UpdateCommittee` discriminant this rule defines; `DC-LEDGER-11` lists `DC-LEDGER-10` back)** — all bidirectional (the six target rules list `DC-LEDGER-10` back). `DC-LEDGER-10` *strengthens* `T-DET-01` / `T-ENC-03` and *relates* `DC-LEDGER-08` / `DC-LEDGER-09` / `DC-TXV-05`. |
| **Requirement** | Credential identity is faithful end-to-end: a stake/committee/DRep credential is a closed sum over `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}` of a 28-byte hash, never a tag-erased `Hash28`. Both era certificate decoders preserve the key/script discriminant (an unknown tag is a deterministic reject); the credential type makes a discriminant-less credential unrepresentable on the BLUE authority path (no `Hash28`→credential coercion); `CertState` (registrations/delegations/rewards) and `ConwayGovState` (vote_delegations/committee_hot_keys/drep_expiry) key on the discriminated credential, so a key-hash and a script-hash credential sharing 28 bytes are distinct authoritative-state keys (matching cardano-node's `Credential`-keyed UMap/VState); and the canonical fingerprint serializes the discriminant so two states differing only in a credential's key/script tag fingerprint differently. The discriminated representation is a deliberate cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration (`T-DET-01`). Default scope is Shelley+; Byron is included only if proven to have an affected credential surface. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (`StakeCredential` closed `enum {KeyHash(Hash28), ScriptHash(Hash28)}` + `hash()` accessor — replaces the tuple-struct `StakeCredential(Hash28)`) — OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/cert.rs` + `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (`decode_stake_credential` reads the credential type tag, maps `0 → KeyHash` / `1 → ScriptHash`, rejects any other tag with `CodecError::InvalidCborStructure { detail: "unknown stake credential type" }` — the prior tag-discarding `let (_cred_type|_tag, _)` form is gone) — OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`ConwayGovState` re-keyed to `StakeCredential` on `vote_delegations`/`committee_hot_keys`/`drep_expiry`), `gov_cert.rs`, `governance.rs`, `cert_classify.rs`, `rules.rs` (the `cred.hash()` boundary adapter retained only for the `Hash28`-keyed stake-distribution snapshot — a declared non-goal surface) — OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`write_stake_credential` emits discriminant+hash; gov-map writers call it; the stake-snapshot writer stays `write_hash28` by design) — OQ5-S1; `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (GREEN — the gov-map + DRep-reg parses preserve the tag) — OQ5-S1. **COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY-S1 (committee surface):** `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (`evaluate_ratification` / `check_ratification` re-typed to `committee_members: &BTreeMap<StakeCredential, u64>` + `committee_hot_keys: &BTreeMap<StakeCredential, StakeCredential>`; committee ratification resolves a vote by **full-credential equality** — no `cred.hash()` on the committee path); `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`ConwayGovState.committee` re-keyed `Hash28` → `StakeCredential`); `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` (`GovActionState.committee_votes` re-typed `Vec<(Hash28, Vote)>` → `Vec<(StakeCredential, Vote)>`; the `drep_votes` / `spo_votes` lists stay `Hash28`-keyed by design — see follow-up (c)); `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (new `write_committee_vote_list` emits the committee-vote credential discriminant; the committee map writer now calls `write_stake_credential`); `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (GREEN — `parse_committee_state` + `parse_committee_vote_map` preserve the committee tag). **DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY-S1 (DRep-voter surface):** `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` (`GovActionState.drep_votes` re-typed `Vec<(Hash28, Vote)>` → `Vec<(StakeCredential, Vote)>` — the DRep-voter surface is now discriminated; `spo_votes` stays `Vec<(Hash28, Vote)>` by design, pools are always key-hash); `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (the `lookup_stake` closure resolves DRep stake by **exact variant** — `vote_delegations.get(cred)` keyed on the full `StakeCredential`, no key/script OR-fallback over identical bytes, so a key-hash DRep and a script-hash DRep sharing 28 bytes do not cross-resolve); `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`write_credential_vote_list`, renamed from `write_committee_vote_list`, now serves committee + DRep vote lists — emits the credential discriminant for both); `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (GREEN — `parse_credential_vote_map`, renamed from `parse_committee_vote_map`, serves committee + DRep and preserves the tag). **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY-S1 (committee-enactment write-back surface):** `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (`EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` re-typed `Option<(Vec<Hash28>, Vec<(Hash28, u64)>)>` → `Option<(Vec<StakeCredential>, Vec<(StakeCredential, u64)>)>` — `StakeCredential`-typed so committee enactment cannot re-collapse the discriminated committee map on write-back; the field is **dormant** (`None`), as `UpdateCommittee` enactment is still a no-op — a preventive structural guard-rail). **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK-S1/S2 (live committee-enactment write-back surface):** `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` (`GovAction::UpdateCommittee` re-shaped from opaque raw bytes to a structured `{removed: BTreeSet<StakeCredential>, added: BTreeMap<StakeCredential, u64>, threshold}` — the discriminated cold credentials survive decode); `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`write_gov_action` emits the structured 5-field shape via `write_stake_credential`, so two `UpdateCommittee` actions differing only in a cold member's key/script tag fingerprint differently); `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` (GREEN — `parse_cold_credential` / `parse_cold_credential_set` / `parse_cold_credential_epoch_map` + `parse_unit_interval`, **fail-closed on an unknown credential tag**); `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (`apply_committee_enactment` pure transition: `NoConfidence` dissolve + discriminated `UpdateCommittee` remove/add + quorum — the write-back preserves the key/script tag, never re-collapsing to `Hash28`) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (epoch-boundary apply site calls it). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/tests/shelley_credential_discriminant.rs::shelley_credential_preserves_discriminant` (Shelley decoder preserves the key/script tag); `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_decode_complete.rs::{conway_credential_preserves_discriminant, unknown_credential_tag_rejects}` (Conway decoder preserves the tag; an unknown discriminant rejects deterministically); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/credential_fidelity_corpus.rs::{discriminant_changes_fingerprint, keyhash_scripthash_same_bytes_are_distinct_certstate, keyhash_scripthash_same_bytes_are_distinct_govstate, discriminant_changes_fingerprint_corpus, credential_accumulation_replays_byte_identical}` (a credential's tag change changes the fingerprint; a key-hash and a script-hash sharing 28 bytes are distinct `CertState` keys and distinct `ConwayGovState` keys; the corpus-level discriminant/fingerprint property; discriminated-credential accumulation replays byte-identically). **+3 in COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY (committee surface):** `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs::committee_keyhash_scripthash_do_not_cross_resolve` (a `KeyHash(0xCC)` cold credential must NOT cross-resolve to a `ScriptHash(0xCC)` committee member of equal bytes — the vote does not count, quorum fails, ratification is denied; with a positive control that a matching-variant member ratifies); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/credential_fidelity_corpus.rs::{committee_keyhash_scripthash_same_bytes_distinct, committee_discriminant_changes_fingerprint}` (a key-hash and a script-hash committee member over identical 28 bytes are distinct `ConwayGovState.committee` members; two gov-states differing only in a committee member's discriminant fingerprint differently). **+2 in DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY (DRep-voter surface):** `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs::drep_keyhash_scripthash_do_not_cross_resolve` (a `KeyHash(b)` DRep vote must NOT cross-resolve to a `ScriptHash(b)` delegation of equal bytes — `lookup_stake` returns the exact-variant stake only, the cross-variant lookup yields zero, with a positive control that a matching-variant DRep resolves its stake); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/credential_fidelity_corpus.rs::drep_vote_discriminant_changes_fingerprint` (two gov-states differing only in a `drep_votes` entry's key/script tag fingerprint differently). **+1 in ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY (committee-enactment write-back surface):** `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs::enactment_committee_changes_keyhash_scripthash_distinct` (an `EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` carrying a `KeyHash(b)` removal and a `ScriptHash(b)` addition of equal 28 bytes keeps the two distinct — they do not collapse on the write-back-typed field; with the default `committee_changes == None` dormancy asserted). **+5 in ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK (live committee-enactment write-back surface):** `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs::{update_committee_decodes_removed_added_threshold, update_committee_keyhash_scripthash_members_distinct, update_committee_decode_rejects_malformed}` (the structured `UpdateCommittee` decodes its removed-set / added-map / threshold; a key-hash and a script-hash cold member of equal 28 bytes stay distinct; a malformed `UpdateCommittee` payload — including an unknown credential tag — rejects deterministically); `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs::update_committee_structured_fields_change_fingerprint` (two `UpdateCommittee` actions differing only in a structured field fingerprint differently); All **19** confirmed to exist as functions in the codebase at HEAD `3180e27`. **+1 since `3d94c22` (commit `b9cfaf9`, real-chain oracle, registry `tests` array now ends with this entry):** `crates/ade_testkit/tests/epoch_oracle_comparison.rs::committee_oracle_mainnet_575_576_noop_agreement` — the discriminated committee credentials are now ORACLE-CONFIRMED against cardano-node's own state at the mainnet Conway 575/576 boundary: the interim Constitutional Committee is exactly 7 `ScriptHash` members (term-expiry epoch 580, quorum 2/3), and our loader parses every member as `ScriptHash` — never a defaulted `KeyHash`. Confirmed to exist as a function at HEAD `168ac02`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` — **introduced in OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY, EXTENDED (not re-added) in COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY, EXTENDED AGAIN in DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY, EXTENDED AGAIN in ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY** (CI count stays 29 — no new file in any strengthening), anchored on `DC-LEDGER-10` in its header comment. Gate PASSES at HEAD `3180e27` (extended in ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK with sections 7 + the write-back-wiring check; no new file — count stays 29). All recorded in `DC-LEDGER-10`'s `open_obligation`.)_ |

### `DC-LEDGER-11`: Conway proposal_procedures is a closed typed grammar (no opaque bytes)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | CIP-1694 (`proposal_procedure = [coin, reward_account, gov_action, anchor]`); Project constitution §3 (closed semantic surfaces, `T-CORE-01`); `DC-LEDGER-10` (downstream credential discriminant must not be re-collapsed). PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE new rule (`status = "enforced"`, `introduced_in = "PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE"`, `strengthened_in = []`). Cross-ref `["DC-LEDGER-10"]` — bidirectional (`DC-LEDGER-10.cross_ref` lists `DC-LEDGER-11` back). The pairing is structural: PP-S1 reuses the existing closed `GovAction` enum (the `UpdateCommittee` arm carries the structured `{removed, added, threshold}` with `StakeCredential` cold members from ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK), so the new typed `proposal_procedures` decode cannot re-collapse the committee credential discriminant `DC-LEDGER-10` defends. |
| **Requirement** | `proposal_procedures` MUST NOT remain an opaque byte field in the authoritative Conway tx-body shape. `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` is `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>`, decoded through a single closed entry point (`decode_proposal_procedures`) that rejects unknown `gov_action` tags, structural failures, empty sets, and trailing garbage deterministically; the typed form re-encodes byte-identically (`PreservedCbor`) for every well-formed Conway tx body. The decoder reuses the existing closed `GovAction` enum (preserving `DC-LEDGER-10` `UpdateCommittee` discriminant) and the existing opaque `Anchor` struct. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs` — PP-S1: `decode_proposal_procedures` (the single sanctioned entry point: array-of-procedures with rejected empty set + rejected trailing bytes), `decode_proposal_procedure` (the per-procedure 4-tuple `[deposit, return_addr, gov_action, anchor]`), `decode_gov_action` (closed dispatch over every CIP-1694 tag — `ParameterChange`, `HardForkInitiation`, `TreasuryWithdrawals`, `NoConfidence`, `UpdateCommittee`, `NewConstitution`, `InfoAction` — unknown tag rejects deterministically), `encode_proposal_procedures` (byte-identical round-trip). `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` — PP-S1: `ProposalProcedure` closed struct `{ deposit: Coin, return_addr: RewardAccount-as-bytes, gov_action: GovAction, anchor: Anchor }`. `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/tx.rs` — PP-S1: the typed key 20 path on `ConwayTxBody` calls `decode_proposal_procedures` / `encode_proposal_procedures` (no `data[start..end].to_vec()` opaque pass-through anywhere on key 20). `crates/ade_testkit/src/governance/proposal_procedures_replay.rs` — PP-S2: the canonical synthetic corpus (covers every `GovAction` variant + a deliberate `UpdateCommittee` `KeyHash`/`ScriptHash` discriminant case + multi-procedure containers) plus the replay harness driving the closed decoder + body-codec round-trips byte-identically. |
| **Tests** | PP-S1 inline in `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs` `#[cfg(test)] mod tests` (14 unit tests): `roundtrip_info_action_proposal`, `roundtrip_hard_fork_initiation`, `roundtrip_no_confidence`, `roundtrip_treasury_withdrawals`, `roundtrip_parameter_change`, `roundtrip_new_constitution`, `roundtrip_update_committee`, `roundtrip_multi_procedure` (every `GovAction` variant + multi-procedure containers re-encode byte-identically), `rejects_unknown_gov_action_tag`, `rejects_empty_proposal_procedures_set`, `rejects_trailing_garbage`, `rejects_truncated_proposal_procedure`, `rejects_invalid_stake_credential_in_update_committee` (adversarial guarantees: unknown tag / empty set / trailing bytes / truncated payload / malformed nested credential all reject deterministically), `update_committee_keeps_stake_credential_discriminant` (the `DC-LEDGER-10` `UpdateCommittee` discriminant survives the new decode). PP-S1 integration in `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_tx_body_proposal_procedures.rs` (3 tests): `body_with_proposal_procedures_round_trips_through_typed_field` (the typed key-20 path round-trips on a full `ConwayTxBody`), `body_none_skips_proposal_procedures_key_20` (`None` does not emit key 20 at all — the negative shape), `body_and_sub_decoder_agree_on_proposal_procedures` (the body-level decode and the sub-decoder agree byte-for-byte on the same input). PP-S2 corpus tests in `crates/ade_testkit/tests/proposal_procedures_corpus_replay.rs` (4 tests): `canonical_corpus_decodes_to_expected_shape` (every canonical-corpus entry decodes into the expected typed shape), `canonical_corpus_round_trips_byte_identical` (encode-after-decode is byte-identical on every entry), `canonical_corpus_covers_all_gov_action_variants` (the corpus exercises every `GovAction` variant — the coverage gate the harness was built around), `canonical_corpus_includes_update_committee_discriminant_case` (the corpus contains the `UpdateCommittee` `KeyHash` + `ScriptHash` cold-member case that pins the `DC-LEDGER-10` pairing). All **21** confirmed to exist as functions in the codebase at HEAD `928c2be` (grep-verified during this refresh). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh` — **new in PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE PP-S1**, anchored on `DC-LEDGER-11` in its header comment. Five mechanical guards: (1) `ade_types::conway::governance` defines the closed `ProposalProcedure` struct with all four fields (`pub deposit`, `pub return_addr`, `pub gov_action`, `pub anchor`); (2) `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` is declared `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>` — NOT `Option<Vec<u8>>` (the prior opaque form); (3) `ade_codec::conway::governance` exists and exports both `decode_proposal_procedures` and `encode_proposal_procedures`; (4) the Conway tx-body codec at key 20 calls the typed decoder/encoder and does NOT use the prior `data[start..end].to_vec()` opaque pass-through for `proposal_procedures`; (5) no `ProposalProcedure {` struct-literal construction outside the sanctioned synthesis sites (`ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs`, `ade_testkit/`, `crates/*/tests/`, and `#[cfg(test)] mod tests` blocks — production callers MUST go through `decode_proposal_procedures`). Gate is expected to PASS at HEAD `928c2be` (PP-S1 + PP-S2 land the surface this gate defends). Plus `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` (bidirectional `cross_ref` enforcement — `DC-LEDGER-11.cross_ref = ["DC-LEDGER-10"]` is bidirectional with `DC-LEDGER-10.cross_ref` listing `DC-LEDGER-11` back; expected PASS at 176 entries). _(Open obligations recorded in `DC-LEDGER-11.open_obligation`, NOT enforcement gaps: OQ-1 — `voting_procedures` (tx body key 19) closure is the natural sibling cluster, same opaque-bytes shape, deliberately deferred and explicitly NOT covered by this rule. OQ-2 / OQ-3 — `ParameterChange.update` and `NewConstitution.raw` nested opacities are likewise deferred; they are future `strengthened_in` candidates if/when those sub-grammars are closed. OQ-4 — typed `RewardAccount` for `proposal_procedure.return_addr` is a separate fidelity decision. See §A000000000000 and §G #32.)_ |

### `DC-LEDGER-12`: Every tx in a forged block is admissible via mempool

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-FORGE-4); PHASE4-N-E mempool admit closure. PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `DC-MEM-03`, `DC-MEM-04`, `DC-CONS-13`. |
| **Requirement** | Every tx in a forged block is admissible via `ade_ledger::mempool::admit` against the base ledger state, in the snapshot's canonical accumulating order. No tx in a forged block bypasses mempool validation. Forge MUST NOT permute, fabricate, or skip the snapshot's canonical accumulating order. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` (tx-admissibility prefix gate inside `forge_block`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/admit.rs::admit` (reused — the producer's prefix check is exactly the closed admission predicate the mempool uses for inbound work, no producer-side fork of admission). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs::tests::{forge_block_rejects_tx_not_in_mempool_accepted_prefix, forge_block_rejects_tx_permuted_from_accumulating_order, forge_block_empty_mempool_produces_empty_body, admit_prefix_property_documented}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_purity.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S3, anchored on `DC-CONS-13/14/15` + `DC-LEDGER-12`) — discharges the admit-prefix property structurally by requiring the forge implementation to call `mempool::admit::admit` for prefix validation (the closed canonical predicate). |

### `DC-MEM-01`: Mempool rules subset of block/ledger rules

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-DET-01`, `T-CORE-01`. Flipped `declared -> enforced` by PHASE4-B2. **Strengthened AGAIN by PHASE4-N-E** (`strengthened_in = ["PHASE4-B2", "PHASE4-N-E"]`): admission is now reached only through the closed wire-level `mempool_ingress(IngressEvent)` chokepoint; the source variant (`N2N` / `N2C`) is evidence/policy/replay metadata and MUST NOT change the validity verdict. `cross_ref = ["DC-MEM-03", "DC-MEM-04"]` (bidirectional). |
| **Requirement** | Mempool acceptance rules must not contradict block/ledger acceptance rules — a tx admitted to the mempool is exactly a tx that `tx_validity` deems `Valid` against the accumulating view; admission never accepts what block/ledger validity would reject. PHASE4-N-E adds: admission is identical when reached through `mempool_ingress(IngressEvent { source, tx_bytes })` versus direct `admit(state, tx_bytes)` — the bridge is a thin source-erasing relabel that preserves verdicts byte-for-byte. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/admit.rs` (admission delegates to `tx_validity` against the accumulating `MempoolState`; closed `AdmitOutcome`); plus PHASE4-N-E — `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs` (`IngressEvent` / `IngressSource` closed types + the `mempool_ingress` single sanctioned production path into `admit`); `crates/ade_testkit/src/mempool/ingress_replay.rs` (GREEN harness `replay_ingress_trace`, `wrap_as_ingress`, `b_track_corpus_as_ingress` — exercises the bridge over the B-track corpus and asserts byte-identical verdicts vs direct admit). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/mempool_admission.rs::{valid_tx_admitted_and_accumulates, invalid_tx_rejected_no_false_accept, admission_equals_tx_validity_verdict, dependent_tx_admitted_against_accumulating_state}`; plus PHASE4-N-E `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_replay.rs::{ingress_admit_equals_direct_admit_on_b_track_corpus, b_track_adversarial_rejections_preserved_through_ingress, dependent_pair_through_ingress_admits_b_after_a}` (the bridge produces the same admit verdicts and the same accumulating state as direct admit on the entire B-track positive + adversarial corpus, including the load-bearing dependent-pair case where tx B depends on tx A and only the A→B order admits both). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (extended in B2 to scan `ade_ledger/src/mempool/` — `AdmitOutcome` must stay a closed structured value). Augmented in spirit by `ci/ci_check_mempool_ingress_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-E — forbids any production `admit` caller outside `mempool_ingress`, so the bridge is the only path into the BLUE admission verdict; the explicit anchor for that gate is `DC-MEM-03` but it structurally protects `DC-MEM-01`'s mempool-rules-equal-block-rules guarantee against future sideways-into-`admit` regressions). |

### `DC-MEM-02`: Deterministic overload shedding

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-DET-01`, `T-CORE-02`. Flipped `declared -> enforced` by PHASE4-B2. |
| **Requirement** | Overload shedding follows a deterministic ordering policy, not timing-dependent collapse — the policy may decide *which* txs are kept under pressure but may never change a tx's `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict (Tier-5 policy independence). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/policy.rs` (closed `OrderPolicy`; deterministic ordering independent of the validity verdict). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/mempool_admission.rs::{policy_does_not_change_validity, determinism}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (`OrderPolicy` must stay a closed structured value). |

### `DC-MEM-03`: Closed wire-level mempool ingress (source is metadata)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3, `T-CORE-01` (closed semantic surfaces), `DC-MEM-01`. Introduced by PHASE4-N-E (S1, commit `32c1ee6`). `cross_ref = ["DC-MEM-01"]` (bidirectional). |
| **Requirement** | Tx ingress reduces to a closed `IngressEvent` before BLUE mempool admission; the source variant is evidence/policy/replay metadata only and MUST NOT change the validity verdict. `IngressSource` is the closed two-variant sum `{N2N, N2C}` (no `#[non_exhaustive]`, no open tail). `mempool_ingress` is the only sanctioned production path into `admit` — every other production caller is a closure violation. `MempoolState.accumulating` is constructed or replaced only inside `admit.rs`. The `mempool_ingress` body MUST NOT branch on `event.source` — that field is metadata. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs` — `IngressEvent` (record carrying `source: IngressSource` + `tx_bytes: Vec<u8>`), `IngressSource` (closed `{N2N, N2C}`), `mempool_ingress(state, event) -> (MempoolState, AdmitOutcome)` (the single BLUE bridge — pure relabel onto `admit` with the source discarded for verdict purposes). |
| **Tests** | Inline in `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs`: `ingress_preserves_tx_bytes_verbatim` (the `tx_bytes` field is forwarded byte-for-byte into `admit`), `ingress_source_is_closed_two_variants` (the enum has exactly two variants and is closed — structural assertion). Integration in `crates/ade_ledger/tests/mempool_ingress.rs`: `ingress_admits_valid_tx_via_n2n`, `ingress_admits_valid_tx_via_n2c` (valid B-track tx admits through both source flavors), `ingress_rejects_invalid_tx_no_false_accept` (an invalid tx rejects through the bridge with the same `AdmitOutcome::Reject{...}` shape as direct admit — no false accept), `ingress_source_does_not_change_verdict_valid`, `ingress_source_does_not_change_verdict_adversarial` (the same `(state, tx_bytes)` produces byte-identical `(MempoolState, AdmitOutcome)` under `N2N` vs `N2C` on both the positive and the adversarial corpora), `ingress_equals_direct_admit_on_synthetic_corpus` (on the synthetic corpus, the bridge's output equals direct `admit` element-wise). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_mempool_ingress_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-E S1, anchored on `DC-MEM-03` in the script header). Five checks: (1) `ingress.rs` exists and defines `IngressSource` + `IngressEvent` + `mempool_ingress`; (2) `IngressSource` is a closed 2-variant enum (`N2N`, `N2C`), no `#[non_exhaustive]`; (3) `MempoolState.accumulating` is constructed/replaced only inside `admit.rs` (the only sanctioned production write site is the `accumulating: applied` field set in `admit()`); (4) `admit()` is called only from sanctioned production sites — `admit.rs` itself (definition + `#[cfg(test)]`) and `ingress.rs` (the bridge); any other `src/` caller is a closure violation, with `tests/` and `benches/` directories exempt; (5) `mempool_ingress`'s body does not branch on `event.source` — the source field is metadata only. |

### `DC-MEM-04`: Mempool ingress-trace replay is byte-identical

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3, `T-DET-01`, `DC-MEM-01`. Introduced by PHASE4-N-E (S2..S5, commits `2d0c918` → `509d714` → `ca3f23a` → `43fcc31`). `cross_ref = ["DC-MEM-01"]` (bidirectional). |
| **Requirement** | Replaying the same ordered ingress trace against the same base ledger state produces a byte-identical sequence of `(MempoolState, AdmitOutcome)` pairs. The replay is strictly single-step per OQ-6 (a fold over `mempool_ingress`, not a partition / batch). Multi-peer interleavings canonicalize to a deterministic round-robin order by sorted peer ID (S3/S4), so two interleavings of the same per-peer queues replay byte-identically. The GREEN harness goes through `mempool_ingress` (the BLUE bridge), never through `admit` directly — the replay is genuinely a fold over the BLUE chokepoint. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_testkit/src/mempool/ingress_replay.rs` (GREEN harness — `wrap_as_ingress`, `b_track_corpus_as_ingress`, `replay_ingress_trace`, `BTrackCase`, `ExpectedOutcome`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs` (the BLUE bridge the fold drives); `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/canonicalize.rs` (deterministic canonical-order canonicalizer that round-robins per-peer `PeerSubmissionQueue`s by sorted `PeerId`, preserving tx bytes verbatim and propagating the source from the queue — S3/S4). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_replay.rs::{ingress_admit_equals_direct_admit_on_b_track_corpus, b_track_adversarial_rejections_preserved_through_ingress, ingress_trace_replay_byte_identical, dependent_pair_through_ingress_admits_b_after_a, ingress_trace_source_invariant_n2n_vs_n2c}`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/canonicalize.rs` inline: `multi_peer_round_robin_by_sorted_peer_id` (multi-peer interleaving is canonicalized to a deterministic round-robin order by sorted peer ID — S4), `unsorted_input_canonicalizes_identically_to_sorted_input` (unsorted peer input canonicalizes to the same output as sorted input — S4); `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_canonicalize.rs::two_interleavings_replay_byte_identical` (two distinct interleavings of the same per-peer queues replay byte-identically through the canonical order — S5). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_mempool_ingress_replay.sh` (PHASE4-N-E S2, anchored on `DC-MEM-04` in the script header). Four checks: (1) the GREEN harness module exists and exports the four items (`wrap_as_ingress`, `b_track_corpus_as_ingress`, `replay_ingress_trace`, `BTrackCase` + `ExpectedOutcome`); (2) the harness's `replay_ingress_trace` body uses `mempool_ingress` — NOT direct `admit` calls — so the replay is genuinely a fold over the BLUE chokepoint; (3) the four load-bearing test names referenced by the registry's `DC-MEM-04.tests` array exist in the integration test file; (4) the harness contains no batching / out-of-order helpers — the replay is strictly single-step per OQ-6 (`fold`, not `partition`). |

### `DC-CORE-01`: BLUE crates are sync-only (no async); BLUE consensus ⇎ ChainDb

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2, `T-CORE-02`; PHASE4-N-A scope decisions §Decision 2 (`docs/active/PHASE4-N-A_scope_decisions.md`); strengthened by PHASE4-N-B over `ade_core::consensus` + `ade_runtime::consensus`. |
| **Requirement** | BLUE authoritative crates are sync-only: no `async fn`, `.await`, `tokio::`, `async_std::`, `Future`, `futures::`, task spawning, async channels, or timers. Async runtime concerns are confined to RED transport/runtime code. PHASE4-N-B narrows further: BLUE consensus (`ade_core::consensus`) may not reference `ChainDb`/`chain_db` — those belong to RED `ade_runtime::chaindb`. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/chain_selector.rs` (GREEN orchestrator that bridges BLUE consensus transitions to RED N-A network inputs; never receives sockets or tokio types); `crates/ade_core_interop/src/lib.rs` + `crates/ade_core_interop/src/bin/live_consensus_session.rs` (RED live-peer driver crate; depends on ade_core only via typed Orchestrator surface). |
| **Tests** | `consensus::chain_selector::tests::{header_arrival_updates_state_and_selector, rollback_walks_back_via_recent_snapshots, rollback_to_block_older_than_snapshots_rejected, epoch_boundary_emits_no_event}`; `crates/ade_core_interop/tests/live_consensus_session.rs::cardano_node_session_sustained_window` (`#[ignore]` by default). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_no_async_in_blue.sh` — bans `async fn`/`.await`/`tokio::`/`async_std::`/`Future`/`futures::`/spawn/timers anywhere in BLUE; scans all 6 BLUE crates plus the 9 `ade_network` submodule paths and `crates/ade_core/`. `ci/ci_check_no_chaindb_in_consensus_blue.sh` (PHASE4-N-B) — bans `ChainDb`/`chain_db` tokens anywhere under `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/`. Together they discharge the BLUE/RED partition for consensus. |

### `DC-PROTO-06`: BLUE protocol transitions are pure functions of explicit version

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2; PHASE4-N-A invariants §7 decision 1 (`docs/active/PHASE4-N-A_invariants.md`). **PHASE4-N-G strengthens this rule** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`): negotiated protocol version is threaded through the producer-side server-role surface via per-peer `PerPeerN2nServerState` carrying the version typed parameter — the server reducers `producer_chain_sync_serve` / `producer_block_fetch_serve` consume version as an explicit input, never read from RED ambient context. **PHASE4-N-H strengthens this rule again** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-H`): negotiated protocol version is threaded through the receive-role surface via per-peer `PerPeerReceiveState` carried on every reducer call site by the RED receive orchestrator (`crates/ade_runtime/src/receive/orchestrator.rs`) — the BLUE receive reducer `receive_apply` takes version as an explicit typed input alongside the canonical `ReceiveEvent`, never reads version from RED ambient context. |
| **Requirement** | BLUE mini-protocol transitions are pure functions of (canonical prior state, canonical input message, selected protocol version, deterministic configuration); no ambient session-glue state may alter authoritative behavior. Selected version is an explicit input, never read from RED context. |
| **Code** | Per-protocol pure transition modules under `crates/ade_network/src/{chain_sync,block_fetch,tx_submission,keep_alive,peer_sharing}/{state,agency,signal,event,transition}.rs` plus the four N2C state machines under `crates/ade_network/src/n2c/{local_chain_sync,local_tx_submission,local_state_query,local_tx_monitor}/{state,agency,event,transition}.rs`. All transition signatures take selected protocol version as an explicit typed parameter. PHASE4-N-G adds producer-side server reducers under the same discipline: `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs::producer_chain_sync_serve` + `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs::producer_block_fetch_serve` consume the negotiated version through `PerPeerN2nServerState` (`crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/n2n_server.rs`); no server reducer reads version from a runtime singleton or RED-ambient context. |
| **Tests** | Same large per-protocol transition battery as `DC-PROTO-01` — the `version_gating_rejects_out_of_version_message` test on every state machine is the explicit DC-PROTO-06 evidence anchor, plus the per-protocol `wrong_agency_returns_error` tests and the event-trace corpora. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_ce_n_a_5_proof.sh` (CE-N-A-5 condition 2 — version-gating rejection across all 11 protocols). Plus PHASE4-N-G `ci/ci_check_chain_sync_server_closure.sh` + `ci/ci_check_block_fetch_server_closure.sh` (defend the server reducers' purity / no-wall-clock / no-rand / no-async / no-HashMap posture) + `ci/ci_check_n2n_server_no_signing_dep.sh` (the RED N2N server orchestrator MUST NOT import `crate::producer::signing` — version-threaded server pump never touches the signing module). `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`. Plus PHASE4-N-H `ci/ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh` (defends the receive reducer's purity / no-wall-clock / no-rand / no-async / no-HashMap posture; the reducer is called with version threaded through `PerPeerReceiveState`) + `ci/ci_check_receive_orchestrator_no_producer_dep.sh` (the RED receive orchestrator MUST NOT import `crate::producer::signing` / `producer::broadcast` / `producer::scheduler` — version-threaded receive pump never touches the signing or broadcast modules). `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-H`. |

### `DC-PROTO-07`: Producer-side server-role session transcript is deterministic

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-a-successor-invariants.md` §3. PHASE4-N-G new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-G"`). Strengthens `T-DET-01` for the producer server-role surface. Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `DC-PROTO-06`. |
| **Requirement** | Given canonical inputs (`negotiated_version, peer_message_sequence, broadcast_arrival_sequence, session_event_sequence`), the producer-side chain-sync / block-fetch session orchestrator emits a byte-identical sequence of outgoing mini-protocol frames across replays. The per-session reducer is a pure deterministic transition. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` (`producer_chain_sync_serve` + `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip` — pure, total, deterministic); `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs` (`producer_block_fetch_serve` — pure, total, deterministic); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/broadcast_to_served.rs` (GREEN `drain_and_admit` — pure, no I/O); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_lookups.rs` (trait impls — pure projections). |
| **Tests** | `producer_chain_sync_serve_replays_byte_identical_over_corpus`; `producer_block_fetch_serve_replays_byte_identical_over_corpus`; `drain_and_admit_is_deterministic_over_arrival_sequence`; `session_transcript_replay_byte_identical` (end-to-end — drives the full pipeline over identical canonical inputs twice and asserts byte-equal outgoing frame sequences). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_chain_sync_server_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-G-S3, anchored on `DC-PROTO-07/08`), `ci/ci_check_block_fetch_server_closure.sh` (S4, anchored on `DC-CONS-17` + `DC-PROTO-07`), `ci/ci_check_broadcast_to_served_purity.sh` (S5) — each enforces purity / no-wall-clock / no-rand / no-async / no-HashMap on its respective reducer / adapter. |

### `DC-PROTO-08`: Producer-side chain-sync server reducer is total and deterministic-resolution

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-a-successor-invariants.md` §1 (I-8), §2 (¬P-4). PHASE4-N-G new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-G"`). Cross-refs `DC-PROTO-06`, `DC-PROTO-07`. |
| **Requirement** | Once chain-sync enters a state where the server holds agency, the pure per-session reducer must return exactly one of: a legal `RollForward`, a legal `RollBackward`, a legal `AwaitReply`, or a structured deterministic session-close/error. It must not return an ambiguous wait state unless the wait condition is an explicit replay input. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` (`producer_chain_sync_serve` + `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip` — total over server-agency states; exhaustive match returns `ServerStep::Reply` or `ServerStep::Done`; no silent wait). |
| **Tests** | `producer_chain_sync_serve_request_next_idle_yields_roll_forward_when_served_has_block`; `producer_chain_sync_serve_request_next_idle_yields_await_reply_when_served_empty`; `producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_known_point_yields_intersect_found`; `producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_unknown_point_yields_intersect_not_found`; `producer_chain_sync_serve_done_terminates_session`; `producer_chain_sync_serve_rejects_illegal_grammar_pair`; `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip_idle_yields_none`; `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip_can_await_yields_roll_forward_when_block_available`; `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip_must_reply_yields_roll_forward_when_block_available`; `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip_can_await_yields_none_when_cursor_at_head`; `producer_chain_sync_serve_roll_forward_header_equals_accepted_block_header_bytes`; `producer_chain_sync_serve_replays_byte_identical_over_corpus`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_chain_sync_server_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-G-S3, anchored on `DC-PROTO-08`) — defends totality (exhaustive match) and purity (no wall-clock / rand / async / HashMap) of `producer_chain_sync_serve` / `producer_chain_sync_advance_tip`. |


### `DC-CONS-03`: Praos chain selection ordering (no density)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; ouroboros-consensus (pinned reference: cardano-node 10.6.2 → ouroboros-consensus ~0.22.x); cross-refs `DC-CONSENSUS-01`, `CN-CONS-01`. |
| **Requirement** | Praos chain selection ordering: block number first, then Praos `TiebreakerView` (slot, issuer, op-cert issue number, VRF output). Density-based ordering is reserved for Genesis/catch-up and must not be used for caught-up Praos fork-choice. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/fork_choice.rs::select_best_chain`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/candidate.rs` (closed `CandidateFragment` + `TiebreakerView`); `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/candidate_fragment.rs` (GREEN candidate-fragment builder). |

| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_no_density_in_fork_choice.sh` (bans any case-insensitive `density` reference in `fork_choice.rs` / `candidate.rs` except a `// no-density:` audit-marker comment); `ci/ci_check_no_chaindb_in_consensus_blue.sh`; `ci/ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`; `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`. |

### `DC-CONS-04`: Praos chain-dep state authority (consensus-owned, not ledger)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; ouroboros-consensus `PraosChainDepState`; cross-refs `DC-CONSENSUS-02`, `DC-CONS-10`. |
| **Requirement** | Praos chain-dep state (`evolving`/`candidate`/`epoch`/`previous_epoch`/`lab`/`last_epoch_block` nonces, op-cert counters, `last_slot`) is owned by N-B consensus, not by the ledger, and evolves deterministically as a function of validated headers and epoch boundaries. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/praos_state.rs` (`PraosChainDepState` + op-cert counter `BTreeMap`); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/events.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/errors.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/encoding.rs` (canonical state encoding); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/nonce.rs` (`apply_nonce_input` + epoch-boundary rotation); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/op_cert.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/header_validate.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/header_summary.rs`. |
| **Tests** | `consensus::praos_state::tests::{op_cert_upsert_rejects_regression, op_cert_upsert_rejects_equal_counter, op_cert_upsert_accepts_strictly_increasing, genesis_state_is_well_formed, nonce_zero_constant_is_zero_bytes}`; `consensus::encoding::tests::op_cert_counter_map_iteration_is_deterministic`; canonical-roundtrip battery `crates/ade_core/tests/praos_state_canonical_roundtrip.rs::{layout_is_stable, roundtrip_empty_state, roundtrip_genesis_state, roundtrip_populated_state, roundtrip_chain_event_all_variants, roundtrip_chain_selection_reject_all_variants, decode_rejects_unknown_discriminant, decode_rejects_short_array, op_cert_counter_map_iteration_is_deterministic}`; nonce evolution `consensus::nonce::tests::*` (11 unit tests) + `crates/ade_core/tests/nonce_evolution_corpus.rs::{within_epoch_evolving_nonce_matches_corpus, epoch_boundary_freezes_and_rotates_correctly, nonce_evolution_replay_is_deterministic}`; op-cert `consensus::op_cert::tests::*` (8 unit tests) + `crates/ade_core/tests/op_cert_counter_corpus.rs::{normal_progression_records_highest_counter_per_window, regression_after_progression_rejected_with_typed_error, op_cert_replay_is_deterministic}`; header-validate `consensus::header_validate::tests::{pipeline_short_circuits_on_first_failure, nonce_contribution_uses_nonce_role_vrf_output_not_leader_role}` + `crates/ade_core/tests/header_validate_compose.rs::{valid_header_accepted_advances_state, header_with_slot_regression_rejected, header_with_block_no_regression_rejected, header_with_op_cert_regression_rejected, header_with_invalid_vrf_proof_rejected, header_beyond_forecast_horizon_rejected, validate_replay_is_deterministic}`. |

### `DC-CONS-05`: Rollback bounded by k blocks

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; ouroboros-consensus consensus report; cross-refs `DC-CONS-06`, `CN-CONS-01`. |
| **Requirement** | Authoritative rollback must never exceed the security parameter k measured in blocks (mainnet k = 2160). Rollback requests deeper than k return `ExceededRollback`. Forecast/stability windows may be slot-based but must accommodate at least k+1 blocks. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/rollback.rs::apply_rollback`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/events.rs` (`ChainEvent::RollBack`, `ChainSelectionReject::ExceededRollback` / `ForkBeforeImmutableTip`). |
| **Tests** | Unit-level `consensus::rollback::tests::{rollback_preserves_immutable_tip, rollback_preserves_security_param, rollback_with_zero_depth_is_noop, rollback_to_equal_block_no_as_immutable_succeeds, rollback_to_one_below_immutable_rejected}`; corpus tests `crates/ade_core/tests/rollback_corpus.rs::{rollback_within_k_succeeds, rollback_exceeding_k_rejected_with_typed_reason, rollback_before_immutable_tip_rejected, rollback_event_bytes_are_stable, rollback_is_deterministic, rollback_equivalent_to_truncated_replay}` (CE-N-B-2). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`, `ci/ci_check_no_chaindb_in_consensus_blue.sh`. |

### `DC-CONS-06`: Rollback = truncated replay; immutable tip final

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; `T-DET-01`; cross-refs `DC-CONS-05`, `T-DET-01`. |
| **Requirement** | `rollback(state, depth)` produces state byte-identical to truncated replay from the nearest checkpoint. Rollback that would cross the immutable tip (≥ k deep) returns `ForkBeforeImmutableTip` and never alters state. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/rollback.rs`. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_core/tests/rollback_corpus.rs::{rollback_equivalent_to_truncated_replay, rollback_is_deterministic, rollback_within_k_succeeds, rollback_before_immutable_tip_rejected, rollback_event_bytes_are_stable}`; `consensus::rollback::tests::{rollback_to_one_below_immutable_rejected, rollback_preserves_immutable_tip}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`. |

### `DC-CONS-10`: Op-cert counter monotonicity

|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; ouroboros-consensus `OperationalCertificate`; cross-refs `DC-CONS-04`. |
| **Requirement** | A header's op-cert issue counter must be ≥ the highest observed counter for the same (pool, kes_period). Regression yields `HeaderInvalid` with a typed `OpCertCounterError` reason; `ChainDepState` never accepts a regression. |
