| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface. Discharged structurally via `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` ensuring the `OpCertCounterError` variant stays closed and `ci_check_no_chaindb_in_consensus_blue.sh` enforcing the FC/IS boundary.)_ |


### `DC-CONS-11`: OpCert kes_period equals KES period at forged slot

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-KES-3/4); Praos / Shelley operational-certificate specification. PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `DC-CRYPTO-04`, `DC-CONS-12`. |
| **Requirement** | OpCert `kes_period` field equals the KES period at the forged slot under an operator-supplied anchor. `period_at_slot(slot, anchor) = (slot - anchor) / slots_per_kes_period` (integer floor). BLUE rejects header/opcert combinations with mismatched periods at forge time. BLUE MUST NOT infer the anchor from wall-clock or filesystem state; the anchor is a pure input on the canonical `ProducerTick`. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/opcert_validate.rs` (`opcert_validate` + closed `OpCertError`); `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/opcert.rs` (`encode_opcert` / `decode_opcert` + `OpCertCodecError` — closed grammar with byte-identical agreement to cardano-cli). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/opcert_validate.rs::tests::{opcert_validate_accepts_canonical_fixture, opcert_validate_rejects_period_mismatch, opcert_validate_rejects_short_hot_vkey, opcert_validate_first_opcert_no_prev_counter}`; `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/opcert.rs::tests::{opcert_encoder_matches_cardano_cli_byte_identical, opcert_round_trip_byte_identical}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_opcert_closed.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S2, anchored on `DC-CONS-11/12`) — FAILs CI if `OpCertError` / `OpCertCodecError` gains an open-tail variant, if the encoder gains a producer-private path, or if `opcert_validate` admits a header with a mismatched KES period. |

### `DC-CONS-12`: OpCert serial counter strictly monotonic per (cold-key, node)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-OC-2); Cardano operational-certificate counter discipline. PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `DC-CONS-11`, `OP-OPS-04`. |
| **Requirement** | OpCert serial counter is strictly monotonically increasing per `(cold-key, node)`. BLUE rejects regression or repetition at the RED→BLUE boundary: `opcert_validate` fails when `prev_counter` is `Some(c)` and `opcert.counter <= c`. RED feeds the value from durable per-node state; BLUE never trusts an in-memory-only counter. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/opcert_validate.rs` (`opcert_validate` + `OpCertError::{CounterRepeat, CounterRegression, BadColdSignature}`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/opcert_validate.rs::tests::{opcert_validate_rejects_counter_regression, opcert_validate_rejects_counter_repeat, opcert_validate_rejects_bad_signature_over_cold_key}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_opcert_closed.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S2). |

### `DC-CONS-13`: Forge is pure given a canonical `ProducerTick`

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-FORGE-1); Project constitution §2 (`T-DET-01`, Functional Core / Imperative Shell). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Strengthens `T-DET-01` for the producer authority surface. Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `DC-CONS-14`, `DC-CONS-15`, `DC-CONS-16`, `DC-LEDGER-12`, `CN-CONS-07`. |
| **Requirement** | `forge_block` has no wall-clock, no rand, no `HashMap` iteration, no I/O, no locale, and no ambient state. All inputs flow through the `ProducerTick` value (`slot, ledger_state, mempool_snapshot, pparams, vrf_proof, kes_sig, opcert`). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs::forge_block`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/state.rs::ProducerTick` (closed canonical-input value). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/replay.rs::tests::{forge_block_pure_no_io, forge_block_replay_byte_identical}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_purity.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S3, anchored on `DC-CONS-13/14/15` + `DC-LEDGER-12`) — FAILs CI if `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/` introduces wall-clock / rand / `HashMap` / `tokio` / `async fn` / I/O or if `forge_block` reads state outside the `ProducerTick` value. |

### `DC-CONS-14`: Forge byte-equality across replays (no RED signing on replay)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-FORGE-2), §4. PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `DC-CONS-13`. |
| **Requirement** | For two replays of an identical canonical `ProducerTick` stream over the same initial `LedgerState`, `forge_block` produces a byte-identical `Vec<ForgedBlockBytes>`. Replay uses captured signed artifacts (`vrf_proof`, `kes_sig`, `opcert`) and MUST NOT invoke RED signing; private-key material does not appear in replay corpora. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs`; `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/replay.rs::producer_replay_fixtures` (GREEN harness — captured signed artifacts only); `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/fixtures.rs` (canonical synthetic corpus with all-zero KES/VRF placeholders by design). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/replay.rs::tests::forge_block_replay_byte_identical`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_purity.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S3) + `ci/ci_check_no_private_keys_in_corpus.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S3) — the latter FAILs CI if any private-key material (KES skey, VRF skey, cold skey) appears in a producer replay corpus / fixture / test artifact. |

### `DC-CONS-15`: Forge invoked only on leader ticks

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-FORGE-3, NC-VRF-3); Praos / `ouroboros-consensus` leader-check. PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Cross-refs `CN-CONS-01`, `DC-CONS-03`, `DC-CONS-13`. |
| **Requirement** | `forge_block` is a forbidden transition for ticks where `is_leader(state, vrf_output, sigma, asc) == false` at `tick.slot`. The producer uses the same `is_leader` / `check_leader_claim` functions the validator uses; no producer-side fork of the leader-check formula is permitted. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` (leader-check gate before forge); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/leader_schedule.rs::is_leader_for_vrf_output` (shared with validator). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs::tests::{forge_block_rejects_non_leader_tick, forge_block_uses_validator_leader_check_function}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forge_purity.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S3) — defends both the purity property and the no-leader-check-fork property structurally (forge calls `leader_schedule::is_leader_for_vrf_output`, not a private duplicate). |

### `DC-CONS-16`: Forged header body_hash equals canonical blake2b_256 of body wire bytes (single encoder authority)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-FORGE-5); Project constitution §2 (`T-ENC-01`, Byte Authority Model). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`). Strengthens `T-ENC-01` for the producer surface; closes any potential producer/validator encoder bifurcation. Cross-refs `T-ENC-01`, `DC-CONS-13`, `CN-CONS-07`. **PHASE4-N-G strengthens this rule** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`): the validator's header/body split — the only `pub fn *_header_bytes` in the workspace — is now also the single canonical header projection on the network seam, consumed by the producer's `ServedHeaderLookup::next_after` and in turn by `producer_chain_sync_serve`'s `RollForward.header`. There is no parallel splitter, no server-side header re-projection. |
| **Requirement** | Forged `header.body_hash` MUST equal `blake2b_256(forged_body_wire_bytes)`, where `forged_body_wire_bytes` are produced by the **single** Cardano-compatible canonical block-body encoder used by the validator hash path. The producer and validator hash the same bytes through the same encoder. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_body_hash.rs` (`block_body_hash` + `block_body_hash_from_buckets` — the single canonical authority; S4 refactor unified the prior producer/validator drafts into this module); `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/forge.rs` (consumer); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs::computed_body_hash` (consumer).; plus PHASE4-N-G `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs::accepted_block_header_bytes` (the single canonical header byte projection — used by validator hash-check AND by `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_lookups.rs::ServedHeaderLookup::next_after`); `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs::producer_chain_sync_serve` (consumes the projection via the trait — single authority). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_body_hash.rs::tests::{block_body_hash_pinned_recipe_byte_identical, block_body_hash_from_block_equals_from_buckets, block_body_hash_none_invalid_txs_equals_empty_bucket, forged_body_hash_matches_validator_recomputation, body_encoder_is_single_authority}`.; plus PHASE4-N-G `accepted_block_header_bytes_equals_validator_split_on_corpus`, `accepted_block_header_bytes_is_subslice_of_as_bytes`, `accepted_block_header_bytes_rejects_malformed_envelope`, `session_transcript_announced_header_matches_served_body_recipe` (the header projection used on the network seam matches the validator's existing split and the announced header lines up with the served body recipe). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_no_producer_body_encoder.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S4, anchored on `DC-CONS-16`) — FAILs CI if a producer-private body encoder reappears (any blake2b over a non-`block_body_hash` recipe, any duplicate body-encoder definition outside `block_body_hash.rs`). Plus PHASE4-N-G `ci/ci_check_no_parallel_header_splitter.sh` (S1, anchored on `DC-CONS-16` strengthening + `DC-CONS-18` entry) — FAILs CI if any `pub fn *_header_bytes` exists in the workspace outside `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs`. `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`. |

### `DC-CONS-17`: Served block bytes equal AcceptedBlock bytes (block-fetch server never re-encodes)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-a-successor-invariants.md` §1 (I-1). PHASE4-N-G new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-G"`). Strengthens `T-ENC-01`. Cross-refs `T-ENC-01`, `DC-CONS-16`, `CN-CONS-07`. |
| **Requirement** | Block bytes delivered via the producer-side block-fetch `Block{bytes}` payload are byte-identical to `AcceptedBlock.as_bytes()` for the `AcceptedBlock` that cleared `self_accept`. The producer-side server never re-encodes. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs::producer_block_fetch_serve` (constructs `Block{bytes}` only from `served.range_bytes` outputs); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_lookups.rs::ServedRangeLookup` (impl forwards `ServedChainSnapshot::range_bytes` which yields `AcceptedBlock`-derived slices); `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/served_chain.rs::ServedChainSnapshot::block_bytes` (returns `AcceptedBlock.as_bytes()` verbatim). |
| **Tests** | `producer_block_fetch_serve_block_bytes_equal_accepted_block_as_bytes` (the reducer's `Block{bytes}` payload equals the admitted `AcceptedBlock` bytes for a corpus block); `session_transcript_served_block_bytes_equal_admitted_accepted_block_bytes` (end-to-end transcript test — every `Block{bytes}` payload in a corpus-driven transcript equals the admitted `AcceptedBlock.as_bytes()` at its `(slot, hash)` key). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_block_fetch_server_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-G-S4, anchored on `DC-CONS-17`) — enforces that `producer_block_fetch_serve` sources `Block{bytes}` only through `served.range_bytes` (positive grep), and that `block_fetch/server.rs` is pure (no wall-clock / rand / async / HashMap). `ci/ci_check_broadcast_to_served_purity.sh` (PHASE4-N-G-S5) — defends the GREEN broadcast-to-served adapter purity. |

### `DC-CONS-18`: Chain-sync RollForward header equals canonical AcceptedBlock header sub-slice

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-a-successor-invariants.md` §1 (I-2). PHASE4-N-G new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-G"`). Strengthens `DC-CONS-16` (the single canonical header splitter). Cross-refs `DC-CONS-16`, `DC-CONS-17`. |
| **Requirement** | Header bytes announced via chain-sync `RollForward{header, tip}` are the header sub-segment of the `AcceptedBlock` whose body bytes are subsequently servable via block-fetch. `block_body_hash` applied to the served body MUST equal the `body_hash` field of the announced header. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs::accepted_block_header_bytes` (the single canonical projection — promoted from validator-private to workspace-level single authority); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_lookups.rs::ServedHeaderLookup::next_after` (uses `accepted_block_header_bytes`); `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs::producer_chain_sync_serve` (sources `RollForward.header` from the trait lookup). |
| **Tests** | `producer_chain_sync_serve_roll_forward_header_equals_accepted_block_header_bytes` (the reducer's `RollForward.header` equals the canonical projection for a corpus block); `session_transcript_announced_header_matches_served_body_recipe` (end-to-end — the rolled header bytes equal `accepted_block_header_bytes` over the same `AcceptedBlock` the matching block-fetch range subsequently serves); `accepted_block_header_bytes_equals_validator_split_on_corpus` (the single canonical projection matches the validator's existing header split across the producer corpus). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_no_parallel_header_splitter.sh` (PHASE4-N-G-S1, anchored on `DC-CONS-18` entry + `DC-CONS-16` strengthening) — FAILs CI if any `pub fn *_header_bytes` exists in the workspace outside `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs`. `ci/ci_check_broadcast_to_served_purity.sh` (S5) — GREEN adapter imports `accepted_block_header_bytes` (positive grep). |

### `DC-CONS-19`: Receive-side header-body sourcing coherence

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/receive-side-bridge-invariants.md` §1 (I-2). PHASE4-N-H new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `tier = "derived"`). Cross-refs `DC-CONS-18`, `CN-CONS-08`. |
| **Requirement** | When `BlockDelivered{block_bytes}` arrives at the receive bridge, the decoded header bytes of `block_bytes` equal the `header_bytes` cached from the most recent `RollForward` at the same `(slot, hash)`. A peer cannot switch headers between announcement and body delivery. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs` (`block_delivered` helper: decodes the body, looks up `PendingHeaderCache` at `(slot, block_hash)`; absent or key-mismatched → `HeaderBodyMismatch`). `block_hash = blake2b_256(header_sub_slice)` binds header content to the key, so a cached entry at a matching key has bytes that hash to the same `block_hash` by construction. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs::tests::receive_apply_block_delivered_with_no_cached_header_rejects`; `receive_apply_block_delivered_with_mismatched_cached_header_rejects`; `receive_apply_block_delivered_with_matching_header_admits`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-H-S2, anchored on `DC-CONS-19` + `CN-CONS-08`) — defends the reducer's purity + closure properties; the helper's lookup-then-reject shape is structurally enforced by the closed `ReceiveError` taxonomy (no silent skip arm). |

### `DC-CONS-20`: ChainDb / ledger / chain_dep lockstep (admit + rollback)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/receive-side-bridge-invariants.md` §1 (I-3, I-4); `docs/planning/ledger-snapshot-rollback-invariants.md` §1 (I-6). `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-H"` (admit-side); `strengthened_in = ["PHASE4-N-I"]` (rollback-side close — PHASE4-N-I flips the rule `declared → enforced` and removes the `open_obligation = "rollback_side_blocked_until_ledger_snapshot_cluster"` shipped at N-H close). Cross-refs `CN-CONS-08`, `DC-CONS-13`, `CN-STORE-07`, `DC-CONS-22`. **Status: `enforced`** at HEAD `75f75da` (admit + rollback both shipped). |
| **Requirement** | A successful receive-side admission updates `ChainDb`, `LedgerState`, and `PraosChainDepState` as one structural transition. A successful `RollBackward` rolls back all three to the same slot. No path leaves them out of sync; no partial admission; no partial rollback. |
| **Code** | Admit-side (N-H): `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs` (the `BlockDelivered` branch runs `admit_via_block_validity`, persists through `ChainDbWrite`, and only then commits state; failure leaves state unchanged — see `CN-CONS-08`). Rollback-side (N-I): `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs` (the `RollBackward` branch atomically calls `materialize_rolled_back_state` + `commit_rollback` — replaces the prior `Err(ReceiveError::RollbackOutOfScope)` placeholder); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/commit.rs::commit_rollback` (irreversible-step-first staged commit — `chain_write` first, then ledger + chain_dep swap, then pending-header reset; chain_write failure leaves state unchanged); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs::materialize_rolled_back_state` (the single canonical driver via `SnapshotReader::nearest_le` + `BlockSource::blocks_in_range` + per-block `apply_block_with_verdicts` — see `CN-STORE-07` / `DC-CONS-22`); plus the GREEN/RED runtime rollback infrastructure under `crates/ade_runtime/src/rollback/{cadence,in_memory_cache,chaindb_block_source,snapshot_writer}.rs`. |
| **Tests** | Admit-side (carried forward from N-H): `receive_apply_block_delivered_with_matching_header_admits`, `receive_apply_block_delivered_validity_invalid_rejects`, `receive_apply_replay_byte_identical_over_corpus`. Rollback-side (N-I): `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/commit.rs::tests::{commit_rollback_advances_chaindb_and_ledger_atomically, commit_rollback_chain_write_failure_leaves_state_unchanged, commit_rollback_resets_pending_headers}` (S3 atomicity); `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs::tests::{rollback_branch_returns_rolled_back_on_in_memory_snapshot, rollback_branch_returns_rollback_too_deep_when_no_snapshot, rollback_branch_state_unchanged_on_materialize_failure}` (S6 receive-reducer wiring — closed `RolledBack` / `RollbackTooDeep` effects, no silent fallback); `crates/ade_runtime/tests/rollback_end_to_end.rs::rollback_then_continue_admit_equals_straight_line_admit` (S6 integration — snapshot+rollback yields the same ledger fingerprint as straight-line admit; snapshotting is a pure cache). |
| **CI** | Admit-side: `ci/ci_check_admitted_block_closure.sh`, `ci/ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh`. Rollback-side: `ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-I-S2, anchored on `CN-STORE-07` + `DC-CONS-22` — single-authority materialize + no HashMap / wall-clock / tokio) — extended in S6 to defend the receive reducer's `RollBackward` arm against re-introduction of the `RollbackOutOfScope` placeholder. `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-I`. |

### `DC-PROTO-09`: Receive-side transcript determinism

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/receive-side-bridge-invariants.md` §3, §4. PHASE4-N-H new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `tier = "derived"`). Strengthens `T-DET-01` for the receive-role surface. Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `DC-PROTO-07`. **The PHASE4-N-I cluster doc CLAIMS this rule is strengthened by PHASE4-N-I (receive transcript determinism now includes the rollback transition); this strengthening is NOT yet reflected in the registry's `strengthened_in` array at HEAD `75f75da` — surfaced in §A0000000000000000 warning #1 for parent review.** |
| **Requirement** | Given canonical inputs (`initial_ledger, initial_chain_dep, initial_chaindb, event_sequence`), the receive bridge reducer's output state (`ledger', chain_dep', chaindb'`) is byte-identical across replays. The reducer is a pure, total transition. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs` (`receive_apply` + `receive_apply_sequence` — pure transitions); `crates/ade_runtime/src/receive/events_to_state.rs` (GREEN adapter — pure, no I/O); `crates/ade_runtime/src/receive/in_memory_chain_write.rs` (GREEN `ChainDbWrite` adapter backed by `InMemoryChainDb` — pure projection over an in-memory ChainDb). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs::tests::receive_apply_replay_byte_identical_over_corpus` (reducer-level — the same `ReceiveEvent` sequence over the same initial state replays to a byte-identical final state); `crates/ade_runtime/tests/receive_session_transcript_replay.rs::receive_session_transcript_replay_byte_identical` (end-to-end integration — drives a synthetic `ForkChoiceSignal` + `BatchDeliveryEvent` stream through the GREEN adapter + BLUE reducer + `InMemoryChainDb` twice and asserts identical `(ledger fingerprint, ChainDb tip slot, ChainDb tip hash)`). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-H-S2, anchored on `DC-PROTO-09` + `CN-CONS-08` + `DC-CONS-19`) — defends `receive_apply` purity + totality (exhaustive match, no silent skip); `ci/ci_check_receive_replay_purity.sh` (PHASE4-N-H-S3, anchored on `DC-PROTO-09`) — defends the GREEN adapters' purity (no wall-clock / rand / async / HashMap / I/O). |

### `DC-CONS-21`: Snapshot encode/decode round-trip equivalence (declared; persistent encoder follow-on)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/ledger-snapshot-rollback-invariants.md` §1 (I-1, I-2, I-9). PHASE4-N-I new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `tier = "derived"`). **Status: `declared`** with `open_obligation = "persistent_ledger_snapshot_encoding_follow_on_cluster"` — Path A recursive scope split (OQ-3 locked at sketch close, 2026-05-26): N-I ships in-memory `SnapshotReader` only; persistent on-disk `LedgerState` encoding (the ~1500-2000 LoC field-walk encoder mirroring `ade_ledger::fingerprint`'s structure) is carved out to a follow-on cluster. Cross-refs `T-ENC-01`, `T-DET-01`, `DC-CONS-22`. |
| **Requirement** | For any reachable `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)`, `decode(encode(state))` yields a state whose `ade_ledger::fingerprint::fingerprint` matches the original's. Encoder is canonical (`BTreeMap` iteration, no `HashMap`, no floats, no wall-clock); encoded bytes start with a closed version tag and embed the source state's fingerprint for decode-side cross-check. |
| **Code** | _(no enforcement — by design; persistent encoder is the follow-on cluster's deliverable. In-memory snapshot storage at N-I uses `BTreeMap<SlotNo, (LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)>` value-clone rather than encode/decode, so the in-memory cache does not exercise this rule and is not a sufficient discharge.)_ |
| **Tests** | _(no tests — by design; will be the follow-on cluster's deliverable.)_ |
| **CI** | _(no CI enforcement — by design; `open_obligation = "persistent_ledger_snapshot_encoding_follow_on_cluster"`. Not a regression — Path A recursive scope split.)_ |

### `DC-CONS-22`: Replay-forward correctness (snapshot is a pure cache for direct-apply)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/ledger-snapshot-rollback-invariants.md` §1 (I-3, I-4). PHASE4-N-I new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `tier = "derived"`). Strengthens `T-DET-01` for the rollback-materialization replay-forward fold. Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `DC-CONS-21`, `CN-STORE-07`. |
| **Requirement** | Given `state_at_slot_S` and the ordered block sequence `blocks(S+1..=T)` from ChainDb, the replay-forward driver yields a state whose fingerprint matches the state that would result from applying those blocks via `apply_block_with_verdicts` in normal forward operation. Snapshot+replay-forward is a pure cache for direct-apply; never an authoritative side path. Replay-forward MUST honor the unique epoch-boundary authority for any range crossing one (¬P-9). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs::materialize_rolled_back_state` (pure replay-forward fold over `block_validity`; epoch boundaries handled implicitly by `apply_block_with_verdicts` per `rules.rs:244-250` calling `detect_epoch_transition` + `apply_epoch_boundary_full` before block application — no duplicate epoch-transition path in `materialize`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs::tests::{materialize_with_snapshot_at_target_returns_snapshot_state, materialize_with_snapshot_below_target_replays_forward, materialize_replay_forward_equals_direct_apply, materialize_fails_closed_on_invalid_block}`. The core proof is `materialize_replay_forward_equals_direct_apply` — direct-apply state at T and snapshot@S + replay-forward to T have byte-identical `ade_ledger` fingerprints; snapshotting is a pure cache. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-I-S2, anchored on `CN-STORE-07` + `DC-CONS-22`) — FAILs CI if the rollback module tree gains any other `pub fn` returning `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)`, if the driver introduces `HashMap` / `HashSet` / wall-clock / `tokio` / `rand`, or if it fails the positive grep for the `block_validity` call site (replay-forward MUST drive the single admission authority). |

### `DC-VAL-01`: Validity verdict is a pure function of canonical inputs

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec; Ouroboros Praos spec; IDD determinism doctrine (cross-refs `DC-CORE-01`, `T-DET-01`, `DC-CONSENSUS-01`). |
| **Requirement** | A block's validity verdict is a pure function of `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState, EraSchedule, LedgerView, block_cbor)`. No wall-clock, arrival order, `HashMap`/`HashSet` iteration, float, or ambient state may influence it. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/consensus_input_extract.rs` (canonical nonce/field projection), `crates/ade_ledger/src/consensus_view.rs` (pure ledger-side `LedgerView` impl), `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/ledger_view.rs` (`LedgerView` trait — extractive forecast surface). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/consensus_input_extract.rs::tests::{extract_nonces_field_order, extract_nonces_requires_exactly_five, extract_nonces_is_deterministic}`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/consensus_view.rs::{view_returns_corpus_pool_stake_and_vrf_keyhash, view_unknown_pool_returns_none, view_unknown_epoch_returns_none, view_is_pure}`; corpus self-consistency `corpus_loads_and_is_self_consistent`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. Discharged structurally over the BLUE tree by `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` (no `HashMap`/`HashSet`/float/wall-clock in BLUE) and, for the consensus inputs, `ci/ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`. No `ci/ci_check_block_validity.sh` exists — see §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-02`: Valid iff header AND body authority accept

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec; Ouroboros Praos spec (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`, `CN-CONS-04`, `DC-CONS-04`). |
| **Requirement** | A block is `Valid` iff both the consensus header authority (`validate_and_apply_header`) and the ledger body authority (`apply_block_with_verdicts`) accept it. No path may produce a `Valid` verdict while skipping either authority. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` (closed verdict/error taxonomy substrate); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` + `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs` (header ∧ body composition — header authority decided, then body authority applied). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_compose.rs::{valid_block_evolves_both_states, header_before_body_fail_fast}`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. Discharged structurally by `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` keeping the verdict/error taxonomy closed. See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-03`: Header-before-body fail-fast ordering

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Ouroboros Praos spec; IDD fail-fast doctrine (cross-refs `DC-VAL-02`). |
| **Requirement** | The header is validated before the body; body validation never runs on a header-invalid block. The first failing authority determines the reason. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` (header authority decided before body; body authority unreachable on header failure). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_compose.rs::header_before_body_fail_fast`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-04`: Verdict agrees with reference (positive + adversarial)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | cardano-node reference behavior; Cardano ledger spec (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`, `CN-LEDGER-02`). |
| **Requirement** | Ade's `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict for a block equals the reference cardano-node verdict, including the reason class where the reference exposes it — established over both a positive corpus (real valid blocks) and a mandatory adversarial corpus (blocks the reference rejects). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` (closed `Valid`/`Invalid` + reject-class comparison surface); `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/replay.rs` (GREEN positive-corpus replay over all 14 Conway-576 blocks); `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (GREEN deterministic mutators M1–M6 deriving adversarial blocks from the real corpus). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_positive_corpus.rs::{corpus_block_count_is_14, all_corpus_blocks_valid, verdict_stream_replays_identically}`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_adversarial_corpus.rs::{no_mutation_is_ever_valid, each_mutation_maps_to_expected_class, adversarial_replays_identically}`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via positive + adversarial corpus test surface. The CE-B1-4 no-false-accept property (`no_mutation_is_ever_valid`) and the 14/14 positive-corpus property (`all_corpus_blocks_valid`) have no CI gate. See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-05`: Total state evolution (invalid → unchanged)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | IDD explicit-total-transition doctrine; Cardano ledger spec (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`). |
| **Requirement** | A `Valid` block yields evolved `(LedgerState', PraosChainDepState')`; an `Invalid` block yields the unchanged input states plus a structured reason. No partial or in-place mutation occurs on the invalid path. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` (closed verdict taxonomy: `Valid` carries evolved-state stats, `Invalid` carries a structured reason); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` (`Valid` returns evolved `(ledger', chain_dep')`; `Invalid` returns input clones). |

| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. Discharged structurally by `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (closed verdict taxonomy). See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-06`: Fail-closed field checks (no silent skip)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (mandatory witness/field checks); IDD fail-fast doctrine (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`, `T-ENC-01`, `DC-CRYPTO-01`, `DC-TXV-06`). Strengthened by PHASE4-B1 (block fail-closed field checks), PHASE4-B2 (tx witness/input fail-closed checks), PHASE4-B3 (cert/withdrawal conservation early-out removed), PHASE4-B3F (decoder strictness), and PHASE4-B4 (cert-state silent-skip removal). |
| **Requirement** | Every crypto-input, field-size, and structural check on the authority path rejects (produces `Invalid`) on wrong size or shape and never silently skips. The pattern `if X.len() == K { check } else { skip }` is forbidden in BLUE validation; size checks go through a helper that returns an error. No defined-but-unwired check and no tautological (value-compared-to-itself) guard may stand in for a real check. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/verdict.rs` (`FieldKind`/`FieldError` closed fail-closed field taxonomy); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs` (`expect_size` fail-closed header crypto-field guard); `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (M1 truncated VRF proof, M3 flipped KES sig, M4 slot-beyond-horizon mutators); plus PHASE4-B2 tx-path fail-closed checks — `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs` (wrong-size vkey/sig -> `MalformedWitnessField` via `from_bytes`, never skipped) and `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs` (unresolvable input / collateral input is fail-fast, never a silent skip); plus PHASE4-B3 — `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation` no longer carries the cert/withdrawal early-out (the B2 `if certs.is_some() || withdrawals.is_some() { skip }` fail-open is **removed**), so a cert/withdrawal-bearing imbalanced tx is now rejected on value grounds rather than silently skipped; the §9.1 reject-precedence ordering is deterministic; plus PHASE4-B3F — `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs::decode_conway_certs` now rejects trailing bytes after the cert array (`CodecError::TrailingBytes`) and bounds preallocation against a hostile array count, closing two fail-open decoder paths; plus PHASE4-B4 — `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::accumulate_tx_certs` no longer swallows a cert-state decode/apply `Err` (the prior "non-fatal during replay" silent-skip is **removed**), so a Conway cert that fails to decode or apply now propagates a structured `LedgerError` and halts the block transition rather than being silently skipped (see `DC-LEDGER-08`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs::tests::expect_size_rejects_wrong_length`; `crates/ade_core/tests/praos_header_validate.rs::praos_malformed_kes_sig_rejected`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_adversarial_corpus.rs::{no_mutation_is_ever_valid, each_mutation_maps_to_expected_class}`; plus PHASE4-B2 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_witness_closure.rs::{wrong_size_signature_rejected, wrong_size_vkey_rejected, unresolvable_input_is_fail_fast, unresolvable_collateral_input_is_fail_fast}`; plus PHASE4-B3 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_full.rs::{conway_conservation_full, conservation_early_out_removed, reject_reason_precedence_is_deterministic, state_dependent_unaccountable_rejects}` and the adversarial suite `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_adversarial.rs::{adversarial_imbalanced_via_deposit, adversarial_imbalanced_via_withdrawal, adversarial_unknown_cert_tag_rejects_as_decode, adversarial_removed_tag_rejects_as_era_invalid, adversarial_truncated_withdrawals_rejects_as_decode, adversarial_state_dependent_unaccountable_rejects, adversarial_no_false_accept, adversarial_verdicts_replay_byte_identical}`; plus PHASE4-B3F decoder-strictness `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_classification.rs::{trailing_bytes_after_cert_array_rejected, huge_array_count_rejects_without_overallocating}` (the cert-array decoder rejects trailing bytes and bounds preallocation, never silently truncating or over-allocating on a hostile count). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (keeps the block-validity AND tx-validity reject/field/signer taxonomies closed over `ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` and `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/`). `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B1", "PHASE4-B2", "PHASE4-B3", "PHASE4-B3F", "PHASE4-B4"]`. PHASE4-B4 also wires `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` as a complementary fail-open guard (it FAILs if the cert-state `"non-fatal during replay"` swallow rationale or an `Err(_)` swallow arm in `accumulate_tx_certs` reappears — see `DC-LEDGER-08`). PHASE4-B5 adds `DC-LEDGER-09` to `DC-VAL-06`'s `cross_ref` (bidirectional): governance-cert accumulation extends the fail-closed/no-silent-skip discipline to the `ConwayGovState` mutation surface, defended by the new `ci/ci_check_gov_cert_accumulation_closed.sh`. The general fail-open-pattern ban (`if X.len()==K { } else { skip }`) is still **not** mechanically text-scanned — proven only by the adversarial corpora plus the B3 `conservation_early_out_removed` regression test. See §G — strong candidate for a new `ci/ci_check_no_fail_open_len_guard.sh`. |

### `DC-TXV-01`: Pure tx_validity

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec; IDD determinism doctrine (cross-refs `T-DET-01`). PHASE4-B2 new rule. |
| **Requirement** | `tx_validity` is a pure function of `(LedgerState, tx_cbor)`. No wall-clock, arrival order, `HashMap`/`HashSet` iteration, float, or ambient state may influence a transaction's `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/transition.rs` (`tx_validity`: pure composition over `(&LedgerState, &[u8])`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/phase1.rs` (`tx_phase_one` + `decode_tx`, no I/O / clock / rand). |

### `DC-TXV-02`: Phase-1 AND phase-2

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (UTXOW/UTXO/PPUP, Plutus phase-2). PHASE4-B2 new rule. |
| **Requirement** | A transaction is `Valid` iff both phase-1 (structural + UTxO rules + witnesses) and phase-2 (Plutus, when scripts are present) accept it. No path may produce a `Valid` verdict while skipping either phase. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/transition.rs` (`tx_validity`: fail-fast — phase-1 decided first; phase-2 dispatch via `plutus_eval::try_evaluate_tx` never runs when phase-1 fails or when no Plutus scripts are present); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/phase1.rs` (`tx_phase_one` composes the B2-S1 witness closure + `validate_conway_state_backed`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_compose.rs::{valid_tx_is_valid_and_applies, phase1_failure_short_circuits_phase2}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`. |

### `DC-TXV-03`: Verdict agreement (positive + adversarial)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | cardano-node reference behavior; Cardano ledger spec. PHASE4-B2 new rule. |

A false-accept is release-blocking. |

| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`. `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B2", "PHASE4-B3"]`. The no-false-accept property (`no_mutation_is_ever_valid`, `adversarial_no_false_accept`) and the positive-corpus property (`all_corpus_txs_valid`, `synthetic_balanced_cert_withdrawal_txs_are_valid`) have no dedicated corpus CI gate — proven by the test surface. See §G. |

### `DC-TXV-05`: Closed era-versioned required-signer enumeration

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (UTXOW required-signers per era); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B2 new rule. **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY adds `DC-LEDGER-10`** to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): the required-signer / witness closure resolves certificate and input credentials by discriminated `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}` identity, so the credential-fidelity rule and the signer-closure rule reference each other; `DC-LEDGER-10` lists `DC-TXV-05` back. |
| **Requirement** | For each era, `required_signers(state, tx_body)` is a closed, explicit, era-versioned function over every signer source (resolved input payment credentials, explicit required-signers, certificate key hashes, withdrawal key hashes, Conway governance/voting witnesses, collateral-input implications). A signer source not represented in the era's closed enumeration is impossible to silently omit; incomplete enumeration is a forbidden false-accept path. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs` (closed era-versioned `SignerSource` enum + `required_signers`/`tx_derived_required_signers` grounded in Conway `getConwayWitsVKeyNeeded` + `getVKeyWitnessConwayTxCert`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs` (fail-closed coverage over the preserved body hash); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`verify_conway_witness_closure` body-path wiring). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_witness_closure.rs::{all_required_covered_is_valid, missing_input_payment_witness_rejected, missing_explicit_required_signer_rejected, missing_withdrawal_witness_rejected, missing_certificate_witness_rejected, missing_governance_voter_witness_rejected, unresolvable_input_is_fail_fast, unresolvable_collateral_input_is_fail_fast, script_credential_input_not_a_vkey_signer, script_credential_certificate_not_a_vkey_signer, collateral_payment_key_is_required, non_conway_era_is_unsupported, closure_is_deterministic}` (within the 20-test `tx_witness_closure` suite covering the 6-source closure hard gates). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (`SignerSource` / `RequiredSignerError` / `WitnessClosureError` must stay closed). |

### `DC-TXV-06`: Closed/total Conway certificate-deposit classification

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL certificate tags 0..18; UTXO deposit/refund accounting); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B3 new rule; CI-enforced in PHASE4-B3F. Cross-refs `T-CONSERV-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-05`, `DC-TXV-07`. |
| **Requirement** | For each era, the certificate-deposit classification `map(state, cert)` is a closed, total, era-versioned function: every certificate variant resolves to exactly one of `new_deposit(coin)` / `refund(coin)` / `neutral` / `explicit_reject`, with the coin sourced from the cert (Conway explicit-deposit variants) or the protocol parameter (legacy variants). An unrecognized cert tag, malformed cert CBOR, or undecodable withdrawals field is a deterministic reject, never a silent neutral. State-dependent cases that cannot be accounted (e.g. pool re-registration charged as a new deposit) reject with a structured `UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting` error rather than guessing. Incomplete classification is a forbidden false-accept path feeding the value-conservation equation. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (`decode_conway_certs`, closed `ConwayCert` grammar — total decode over tags 0..18); `crates/ade_codec/src/error.rs` (`CodecError::UnknownCertTag`; `RemovedInConway` for tags 5/6); `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` (`ConwayCert`, `CertDisposition`, `DepositEffect`, `CoinSource` — closed sum types); `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs` (`classify`: compiler-exhaustive `match` mapping every variant to exactly one disposition); `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (`UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting`); `corpus/conway_certs/{classification_table.md,tags.json}`. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_classification.rs::{decode_total_over_tags_0_18, unknown_cert_tag_is_codec_error, removed_tag_5_6_is_not_valid_in_conway, malformed_cert_cbor_rejected, decode_is_replay_deterministic}`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs::tests::{class_mapping_is_total, legacy_unregistration_unresolved_is_unsupported_state_dependent, legacy_unregistration_resolves_recorded_deposit, pool_reregistration_is_neutral, pool_new_registration_charges_pool_deposit}`; plus PHASE4-B3F decoder-strictness regressions `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_classification.rs::{trailing_bytes_after_cert_array_rejected, huge_array_count_rejects_without_overallocating}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh` — dedicated grep-gate landed in PHASE4-B3F that flips `status = "partial" -> "enforced"`. It fails CI on: (1) `#[non_exhaustive]` or an open-tail `Other`/`Unknown` variant on `ConwayCert` / `CertDisposition` / `DepositEffect` / `CoinSource` in `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs`; (2) a missing `CodecError::UnknownCertTag` reject or a catch-all decoder arm (single-line `_ => …ConwayCert::` or block-form `_ => { … ConwayCert:: … }`) in `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (the reintroduced-Shelley-fallback anti-pattern); (3) any `_ =>` wildcard arm in `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs` (`classify` must stay compiler-exhaustive). Gate **PASSES** at HEAD `193d2fc` (`PASS: Conway cert classification is closed and total (DC-TXV-06)`, exit 0). The closure no longer rests on compiler-exhaustive `match` + tests alone — it is now CI-enforced. _(Residue: `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` is still outside `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` `TARGETS`, but the dedicated gate above covers the closure, so `DC-TXV-06` is genuinely `enforced`.)_ See §A000. |

### `DC-TXV-07`: Canonical deposit-parameter authority

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | IDD determinism doctrine (deposit params are canonical input); Conway protocol-parameter surface. PHASE4-B3 new rule. Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `T-CONSERV-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, `DC-TXV-06`. |
| **Requirement** | All deposit/refund amounts used by Conway transaction value-conservation accounting must be sourced from canonical ledger protocol parameters or explicit certificate fields, never from testkit defaults, shell configuration, ambient `ConwayGovParams`, or fallback constants. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` (`ConwayOnlyDepositParams`, `ConwayDepositParams` — the canonical deposit-param value); `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`LedgerState.conway_deposit_params` + the `conway_deposit_view` boundary view, which fails fast via `ValidationEnvironmentError::MissingConwayDepositParams` when a Conway state lacks deposit params — see `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`fingerprint_pparams`, Conway-gated deposit-param fold). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs::tests::{conway_deposit_params_canonical_source, non_conway_state_has_no_conway_deposit_params}`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs::tests::{pparams_fingerprint_stable_for_non_conway, pparams_fingerprint_includes_conway_deposits_when_present}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_deposit_param_authority.sh` (PHASE4-B3 — greps the 6 BLUE crates and FAILs on any non-canonical deposit-param source: testkit `ConwayGovParams` reference in a BLUE path, `ProtocolParameters::default()` feeding `drep_deposit`/`gov_action_deposit`/`key_deposit`/`pool_deposit`, an inline literal assigned to a Conway deposit field outside `conway_deposit_params`, or `env::var` feeding a deposit param). `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B3"]`. |

---

## CN — Classification Table Invariants (`classification_table.md`)

> Most `CN-*` rules remain `status = "declared"` in the registry at HEAD —
> three were flipped `declared → enforced` in `78da6c9` (CN-STORE-03/04/05).
> Five (`CN-CONS-01..05`) were strengthened in PHASE4-N-B by populating
> `code_locus`/`tests`/`ci_script` arrays while still carrying their
> declared/partial status. One (`CN-EPOCH-01`) was flipped
> `declared → partial`. One (`CN-CRYPTO-02`) was flipped
> `declared → partial`. The remaining classification-table entries are
> restatements of `T-*` invariants and inherit enforcement through their
> `cross_ref` targets, but the registry has not yet propagated the
> linkage. Each entry below records the canonical requirement, points
> at the cross-referenced `T-*` / `DC-*` rule where de-facto enforcement
> lives, and flags the registry gap.

### `CN-WIRE-01`: Hash-critical bytes preserved

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `classification_table.md` §A. |
| **Requirement** | Hash-critical original bytes must be preserved and used on all hash/signature-critical paths. |
| **Code** | De-facto via `T-ENC-01` / `DC-CBOR-02` — `crates/ade_codec/src/preserved.rs`. _(Registry direct linkage gap.)_ |
| **Tests** | De-facto via `T-ENC-03` / `DC-CBOR-01`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_hash_uses_wire_bytes.sh`. |

### `CN-WIRE-02`: One canonical internal encoding

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `classification_table.md` §A. |
| **Requirement** | Internal replay/state surfaces must use exactly one canonical project encoding. |
| **Code** | De-facto via `T-ENC-01`. _(Registry linkage gap.)_ |
| **Tests** | De-facto via `T-DET-01`. |
| **CI** | _(no CI enforcement — gap)_ |

### `CN-WIRE-03`: Deserialization equivalence across versions

| **Source** | `classification_table.md` §A (directly addresses Nov 2025 fork). |
| **Requirement** | Consensus-critical deserialization must be equivalent across all supported versions and code paths. |
| **Code** | _(no enforcement — gap)_ |
| **Tests** | _(no tests — gap)_ |
| **CI** | _(no CI enforcement — gap; release-tier obligation per `RO-REL-01`)_ |

### `CN-CONS-06`: Cross-impl acceptance — Ade-forged blocks accepted by cardano-node (mechanical half enforced; live half open_obligation)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-LIVE-1); bounty acceptance test (validation + block-production both required). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`, `tier = "release"`). Cross-refs `CN-CONS-07`, `CN-WIRE-01`, `OP-OPS-05`. |
| **Requirement** | Blocks forged by Ade are accepted by cardano-node when delivered via N2N block-fetch / chain-sync. Evidence is operator-action: a sustained-window `live_block_production_session` against a private cardano-node capturing `CE-N-C-LIVE_<date>.log`. Conditional on testnet stake / SPO registration; if unavailable at cluster close the live half is marked `blocked_until_operator_stake_available`, not deferred. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/cross_impl_adapter.rs` (mechanical half — structural cross-impl agreement: decode round-trip + body-hash binding + decoder/encoder structural field agreement against the synthetic S3 corpus); `crates/ade_core_interop/src/bin/live_block_production_session.rs` (live half — operator-action evidence binary, `#[ignore]`-gated; needs preprod SPO stake). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/src/producer/cross_impl_adapter.rs::tests::{cross_impl_adapter_forged_block_decodes_through_ade_codec, cross_impl_adapter_forged_block_structurally_agrees_with_decoder, cross_impl_adapter_corpus_round_trips_byte_identical}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_producer_corpus_present.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S7, anchored on `CN-CONS-06`) — FAILs CI if the synthetic S3 producer corpus is missing or if the cross-impl adapter cannot consume it. **Open obligation (live half):** the crypto-level cross-impl claim (real KES/VRF signatures accepted by cardano-node over N2N) is by-design out of reach of any CI gate against the synthetic corpus (fixtures carry all-zero KES/VRF artifacts so BLUE forge can be replayed without invoking RED signing). The crypto-level claim therefore lives in CE-N-C-8's operator-action live evidence: testnet (preview/preprod) SPO stake must be provisioned and the `live_block_production_session` binary run against a private cardano-node to capture `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-C/CE-N-C-LIVE_<date>.log`. **Reopen criteria:** when stake is registered, run the binary per `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-C/CE-N-C-8_PROCEDURE.md` and append the captured log path to this entry's `evidence_notes`. Follows the OP-OPS-04 precedent (enforced + `open_obligation` for a follow-on artifact). |

### `CN-CONS-07`: Self-acceptance bridge — RED broadcast gated on BLUE self-accept verdict

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §1 (NC-SELF-1). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`, `tier = "release"`). Cross-refs `CN-CONS-06`, `DC-CONS-13`, `DC-CONS-16`, `OP-OPS-05`. **PHASE4-N-G strengthens this rule** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`): the broadcast gate is preserved across the network seam via `ServedChainSnapshot` — only `AcceptedBlock` values may enter the served-chain index (`served_chain_admit` takes an `&AcceptedBlock`, not a `Vec<u8>`), and only served-chain entries can be projected onto the wire via the typed `ServedRangeLookup` / `ServedHeaderLookup` traits. Bytes that reach a peer trace through `AcceptedBlock → ServedChainSnapshot → ServerReply<M>`; the network seam can no longer be an end-run around the self-accept gate. |
| **Requirement** | A forged block is NOT eligible for RED broadcast unless Ade's own header validator (PHASE4-N-B path) and body validator (PHASE4-B1 path) accept it under the same slot, era, and context. Self-acceptance failure halts the producer deterministically. RED broadcast is gated on the BLUE self-accept verdict. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/self_accept.rs` (`self_accept`, `AcceptedBlock`, `SelfAcceptError` — the BLUE bridge); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs::block_validity` (the single closed validator authority `self_accept` wraps — no producer-side fork).; plus PHASE4-N-G `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/served_chain.rs` (`ServedChainSnapshot`, `served_chain_admit` — only `AcceptedBlock` values may enter the served-chain index; `BTreeMap`-ordered, no `HashMap`); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/broadcast_to_served.rs` (GREEN `drain_and_admit` — pure, no I/O, forwards `AcceptedBlock` from `BroadcastQueue` into the snapshot); `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` + `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs` (`ServerReply<M>` closed wrappers — client-agency variants unrepresentable in the public API). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/self_accept.rs::tests::{self_accept_accepts_freshly_forged_block, self_accept_rejects_corrupted_body_hash, self_accept_rejects_invalid_kes_signature, self_accept_rejects_unbalanced_tx_in_body, broadcast_callable_only_with_accept_verdict}`.; plus PHASE4-N-G `served_chain_admit_admits_corpus_block`, `served_chain_admit_idempotent_on_byte_identity`, `served_chain_admit_independent_of_order`, `served_chain_snapshot_iteration_is_btreemap_ordered`, `served_chain_block_bytes_accessor_returns_accepted_block_slice`, `served_chain_range_bytes_returns_inclusive_window`, `served_chain_fingerprint_replay_byte_identical` (the served-chain index is `AcceptedBlock`-only, deterministic, BTreeMap-ordered, and replay-stable). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_self_accept_gate.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S5, anchored on `CN-CONS-07`) — FAILs CI if RED broadcast code path can reach a `forge_block` output without going through `self_accept` (i.e. if a `Vec<u8>` flowing to RED broadcast is reachable without an `AcceptedBlock` proof type), or if `self_accept` is bypassed in any production caller. Plus PHASE4-N-G `ci/ci_check_served_chain_closure.sh` (S2, anchored on `CN-CONS-07` strengthening) — FAILs CI if `served_chain.rs` imports `HashMap`/`HashSet`, if `served_chain_admit` accepts non-`AcceptedBlock` values, or if the public accessors return anything other than `AcceptedBlock`-derived slices. `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-G`. |

### `CN-PROTO-06`: Producer-side server agency closure (typed Server-only reply wrappers)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-a-successor-invariants.md` §1 (I-4). PHASE4-N-G new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `tier = "derived"`). Cross-refs `DC-PROTO-06`, `CN-CONS-07`. |
| **Requirement** | The producer-side session orchestrator can only construct outgoing mini-protocol messages tagged with Server agency. Client-originated messages from the server-role pump are unrepresentable in the public API; misuse is a compile error (closed `ServerReply<M>` wrapper). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_network/src/chain_sync/server.rs` (`ServerReply` for chain-sync — private inner enum; no public constructor for client-agency variants `RequestNext`, `FindIntersect`, `Done`); `crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs` (`ServerReply` for block-fetch — same closure for `RequestRange`, `ClientDone`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs::accepted_block_header_bytes` (the single canonical header projection the chain-sync `ServerReply::roll_forward` consumes). |
| **Tests** | `chain_sync_server_reply_round_trips_through_codec`; `chain_sync_server_reply_into_message_only_yields_server_variants`; `block_fetch_server_reply_round_trips_through_codec`; `block_fetch_server_reply_into_message_only_yields_server_variants` (exhaustive match tests prove the closure: `into_message()` projects only to server-agency wire variants); `accepted_block_header_bytes_equals_validator_split_on_corpus`; `accepted_block_header_bytes_is_subslice_of_as_bytes`; `accepted_block_header_bytes_rejects_malformed_envelope`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_no_parallel_header_splitter.sh` (PHASE4-N-G-S1, anchored on `CN-PROTO-06`) — single-authority header projection: the only `pub fn *_header_bytes` in the workspace lives at `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs`. Type-level closure of `ServerReply<M>` is a compile-time property; adding a constructor for a client-agency variant would require explicit modification of the wrapper's public API and would surface in code review. |

### `CN-CONS-08`: Receive-side single admission authority — every block in ChainDb passed `block_validity::Valid`

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/receive-side-bridge-invariants.md` §1 (I-1, folds I-7). PHASE4-N-H new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `tier = "release"`). Cross-refs `CN-CONS-07` (broadcast-side analog), `DC-CONS-13`, `DC-CONS-19`, `DC-CONS-20`. |
| **Requirement** | Every block that lands in `ChainDb` via the receive path passed `block_validity` with `BlockValidityVerdict::Valid`. No bypass, no header-only fast path, no trusted-prefix mode. Invalid verdicts leave receive state unchanged and halt the peer pipeline with a structured error; no silent skip, no partial application. Receive-side analog of `CN-CONS-07` (broadcast gate). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/admitted.rs` (`AdmittedBlock` + `admit_via_block_validity` — the single admission authority; module-private struct constructor; `admit_via_block_validity` is the only public entry that can return an `AdmittedBlock`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs` (`block_delivered` helper composes `admit_via_block_validity` then commits state atomically via the `ChainDbWrite` trait; failure leaves state unchanged); `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/chain_write.rs` (`ChainDbWrite::write_admitted` takes `AdmittedBlock` by value — no path persists raw bytes). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/admitted.rs::tests::{admit_via_block_validity_accepts_corpus_block, admit_via_block_validity_rejects_corrupted_body}`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/reducer.rs::tests::{receive_apply_block_delivered_with_matching_header_admits, receive_apply_block_delivered_validity_invalid_rejects, receive_apply_rollback_returns_out_of_scope, receive_apply_replay_byte_identical_over_corpus}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_admitted_block_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-H-S1, anchored on `CN-CONS-08` + `CN-PROTO-07`) — FAILs CI if any `pub fn .*-> *AdmittedBlock` exists outside the canonical site `ade_ledger::receive::admitted::admit_via_block_validity`, or if the `ReceiveEvent` closed sum gains a locally-originated variant (`RequestNext`, `RequestRange`, `ClientDone`, `FindIntersect`); `ci/ci_check_receive_reducer_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-H-S2, anchored on `CN-CONS-08` + `DC-CONS-19` + `DC-PROTO-09`) — FAILs CI if `receive_apply` introduces wall-clock / rand / `HashMap` / `tokio` / `async fn` / I/O, if the `RollForward` branch mutates ledger/chain_dep/chaindb, or if the `RollBackward` branch returns `Ok`. |

### `CN-PROTO-07`: Receive-side agency closure (typed peer-only `ReceiveEvent` sum)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/receive-side-bridge-invariants.md` §1 (closure). PHASE4-N-H new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `tier = "derived"`). Cross-refs `CN-PROTO-06` (producer-side analog), `DC-PROTO-06`. |
| **Requirement** | The receive bridge consumes only peer-originated `ForkChoiceSignal` and `BatchDeliveryEvent` values valid for the client-role N2N receive surface. Constructing or admitting locally-originated / client-output events into the receive reducer is unrepresentable in the public API. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/events.rs` (closed `ReceiveEvent` sum with exactly 3 variants — `RollForward`, `RollBackward`, `BlockDelivered` — all peer-originated; no constructor for `RequestNext` / `RequestRange` / `ClientDone` / `FindIntersect` exists in the public API; exhaustive `match` over each enum variant compiles and no `_` arm is needed). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/events.rs::tests::{receive_event_round_trips_through_pattern_match, receive_effect_round_trips_through_pattern_match, receive_error_round_trips_through_pattern_match}` — exhaustive-match round-trip tests fail to compile if a fourth variant is added without explicit closure review. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_admitted_block_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-H-S1, also anchored on `CN-PROTO-07`) — forbids any locally-originated chain-sync / block-fetch variant name (`RequestNext`, `RequestRange`, `ClientDone`, `FindIntersect`) in `events.rs` production code, and any `pub fn .*-> *AdmittedBlock` outside the canonical site. |

### `CN-STORE-07`: Single materialize authority for rolled-back state

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/ledger-snapshot-rollback-invariants.md` §1 (I-5). PHASE4-N-I new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-I"`, `tier = "release"`). Mirror of `CN-CONS-08` (admission gate) for the rollback path. Cross-refs `CN-CONS-08`, `DC-CONS-20`, `DC-CONS-22`. |
| **Requirement** | The function that materializes `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)` at a target point uses ONLY one `SnapshotStore` lookup + `ChainDb::iter_from_slot` + `apply_block_with_verdicts` (+ `apply_epoch_boundary` when crossing). No bypass; no parallel rolled-back-state computation path. Single-public-function discipline; type-level + CI grep enforcement. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs::materialize_rolled_back_state` — the **sole** `pub fn` returning `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)` in the rollback module tree. The function takes narrow read-only traits (`SnapshotReader` + `BlockSource`), not concrete chain stores — production impls in `ade_runtime/src/rollback/{in_memory_cache,chaindb_block_source}.rs` (`InMemorySnapshotCache` + `ChainDbBlockSource<'a, D: ChainDb>`) go through the same single composition. `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/traits.rs` (`SnapshotReader` + `BlockSource` narrow read-only traits). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rollback/materialize.rs::tests::{materialize_returns_rollback_too_deep_when_no_snapshot, materialize_with_snapshot_at_target_returns_snapshot_state, materialize_with_snapshot_below_target_replays_forward, materialize_fails_closed_on_invalid_block, materialize_replay_forward_equals_direct_apply}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-I-S2, anchored on `CN-STORE-07` + `DC-CONS-22`) — enforces single-authority via grep: no other `pub fn` in `rollback/*` returns `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)`; positive grep for the `block_validity` call site (the driver composes one `SnapshotReader::nearest_le` + `BlockSource::blocks_in_range` + per-block `block_validity`); no `HashMap` / wall-clock / `tokio` / `rand` in the rollback BLUE tree. |

### `CN-CRYPTO-04`: No fallback after verification failure

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|

## RO — Release Obligations (Project Constitution §4a)

> All `RO-*` rules are release-tier obligations. None have `code_locus`,
> `tests`, or `ci_script` populated in the registry. They are
> release-gate criteria, not HEAD-time enforcement points; this is by
> design and is recorded here as the explicit "no CI at HEAD" state.

### `RO-LIVE-01`: Haskell node fetches Ade-forged block bytes (live cross-impl)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-a-successor-invariants.md` §8. PHASE4-N-G new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-G"`, `tier = "release"`). Cross-refs `DC-CONS-16`, `DC-CONS-17`, `DC-CONS-18`, `CN-PROTO-06`, `DC-PROTO-07`, `DC-PROTO-08`, `CN-CONS-06`. |
| **Requirement** | A Haskell cardano-node peer issuing `RequestRange` covering an Ade-forged block receives, via the producer-side block-fetch server, bytes that pass that peer's full header+body validation. Captured as an operator-action log against a private Haskell peer; the underlying semantic invariants are `DC-CONS-17`, `DC-CONS-18`, `CN-PROTO-06`, `DC-PROTO-07`, `DC-PROTO-08`, and the existing self-accept + body-hash recipe (`DC-CONS-16`). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/tests/cross_impl_server_pipeline.rs` (mechanical adapter — CE-N-G-7; pre-condition closure: every served `Block{bytes}` decodes via Ade's envelope+block decoder and the recomputed body-hash matches the announced header's `body_hash` field); `crates/ade_core_interop/src/bin/live_block_fetch_session.rs` (operator-action binary — CE-N-G-8; `#[ignore]`-default in CI; `--hermetic` mode prints readiness; `--connect <addr>` mode connects to a private cardano-node peer); `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-G/CE-N-G-8_PROCEDURE.md` (operator procedure). |
| **Tests** | `cross_impl_server_pipeline_request_range_returns_decodable_bytes`; `cross_impl_server_pipeline_request_range_byte_identical_to_self_accept_input`; `live_block_fetch_session_hermetic_default_prints_readiness`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_server_paths_corpus_present.sh` (PHASE4-N-G-S7, anchored on `RO-LIVE-01`) — FAILs CI if the mechanical cross-impl integration test source file is absent at the expected path with the expected test names, or if the `live_block_fetch_session` binary source file is absent. **Open obligation (live half):** `blocked_until_operator_peer_available` — the live cross-impl claim (a real cardano-node `RequestRange` over a private TCP peer accepts the served bytes) is by-design out of reach of any CI gate against the synthetic corpus and lives in CE-N-G-8's operator-action live evidence. **Reopen criteria:** operator runs `live_block_fetch_session --connect <addr>` against a private Haskell peer per `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-G/CE-N-G-8_PROCEDURE.md` and appends the captured log path to this entry's `evidence_notes`. Mirrors the OP-OPS-04 / CN-CONS-06 precedent (enforced + `open_obligation` for a follow-on operator-action artifact). Status: `partial`. |

### `RO-LIVE-02`: Cardano-node peer follow → ChainDb tip equals peer tip (live receive cross-impl)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/receive-side-bridge-invariants.md` §8. PHASE4-N-H new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `cluster = "PHASE4-N-H"`, `tier = "release"`). Cross-refs `RO-LIVE-01` (producer-side analog), `CN-CONS-08`, `DC-CONS-19`, `DC-CONS-20`, `DC-PROTO-09`. |
| **Requirement** | A cardano-node peer's `RollForward` + `BlockDelivered` stream, consumed by the receive bridge, produces a `ChainDb` tip equal to the peer's announced tip at every step over a captured follow window. Live evidence captured against a private cardano-node peer; underlying invariants are `CN-CONS-08`, `DC-CONS-19`, `DC-CONS-20`, `DC-PROTO-09`, and the existing `block_validity` (B1) authority. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/tests/receive_pipeline_corpus_drive.rs` (mechanical adapter — CE-N-H-5; pre-condition closure: every Conway-576 corpus block admits through the full receive pipeline; ChainDb tip matches expected `(slot, hash)`; stored bytes equal corpus bytes byte-identically; `LedgerState` fingerprint changes on admission); `crates/ade_core_interop/src/bin/live_block_follow_session.rs` (operator-action binary — CE-N-H-6; `#[ignore]`-default in CI; `--hermetic` mode prints readiness; `--connect <addr>` mode connects to a private cardano-node peer); `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-H/CE-N-H-6_PROCEDURE.md` (operator procedure). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/tests/receive_pipeline_corpus_drive.rs::{receive_pipeline_corpus_drive_admits_every_block, receive_pipeline_corpus_drive_chaindb_tip_matches_expected, receive_pipeline_corpus_drive_admitted_bytes_equal_corpus_bytes, receive_pipeline_corpus_drive_ledger_fingerprint_changes_on_admit}`; `crates/ade_core_interop/tests/live_block_follow_session.rs::live_block_follow_session_hermetic_default_prints_readiness`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_receive_paths_corpus_present.sh` (PHASE4-N-H-S6, anchored on `RO-LIVE-02`) — FAILs CI if the mechanical pipeline-drive test source file is absent at the expected path with the expected test names, or if the `live_block_follow_session` binary source file is absent. **Open obligation (live half):** `blocked_until_operator_peer_available` — the live receive cross-impl claim (a real cardano-node `RollForward` + `BlockDelivered` stream lands at a ChainDb tip equal to the peer's announced tip over a captured follow window) is by-design out of reach of any CI gate against the synthetic corpus and lives in CE-N-H-6's operator-action live evidence. **Reopen criteria:** operator runs `live_block_follow_session --connect <addr>` against a private cardano-node peer per `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-H/CE-N-H-6_PROCEDURE.md` and appends the captured log path to this entry's `evidence_notes`. Mirrors the OP-OPS-04 / CN-CONS-06 / RO-LIVE-01 precedent (enforced + `open_obligation` for a follow-on operator-action artifact). Status: `partial`. |

## OP — Operational Invariants (Project Constitution §4b)

> All `OP-*` rules are operational invariants. They constrain how the
> node is deployed and operated; they are not properties of the source
> tree. There is no HEAD-time CI enforcement for any of them by design.

### `OP-NET-01`: Trusted relay topology for BP

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §4b; cross-ref `CN-NET-01`. |
| **Requirement** | Block producer connects only through trusted relay topology. |
| **Code** | _(operational)_ |
| **Tests** | _(operational)_ |
| **CI** | _(operational — no in-repo enforcement)_ |

| **Tests** | _(operational)_ |
| **CI** | _(operational)_ |

| **Code** | _(operational)_ |
| **Tests** | _(operational)_ |

### `OP-OPS-04`: Operator-supplied keys; private-key material confined to RED

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §7 (OQ1). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`, `tier = "operational"`). Cross-refs `DC-CRYPTO-03`, `DC-CRYPTO-04`, `DC-CRYPTO-05`, `DC-CONS-12`. |
| **Requirement** | Ade does NOT generate cold / KES / VRF keys. Operator provides cardano-cli-format key files (`*.skey`, opcert) loaded by `ade_runtime::producer::keys`; private-key material never crosses into BLUE. Key generation remains a cardano-cli operator workflow. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/keys.rs` (`load_*_signing_key_skey`, `KeyLoadError`); `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs` (RED-confined signing custody). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/keys.rs::tests::{cardano_cli_skey_envelope_round_trips_through_keys_loader, keys_loader_rejects_wrong_envelope_type, keys_loader_rejects_malformed_cbor_hex, key_load_error_io_carries_no_path_bytes}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S1, mechanical enforcement of the RED-only custody invariant; closure proof for CE-N-C-1; cross-referenced by `DC-CRYPTO-03`/`DC-CRYPTO-04`/`DC-CRYPTO-05`). **Open obligation:** `cardano-crypto 1.0.8` exposes `gen_key_kes_from_seed_bytes` but no `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes` for `Sum6KES`; the keys loader currently round-trips synthetic seed-encoded skeys but does not yet load real cardano-cli's 612-byte expanded-tree `Sum6KES` serialization. Resolution: either upstream a `Sum6KES` deserializer, fork the parsing locally, or document the cardano-cli kes-skey conversion step in the operator workflow. CE-N-C-8 operator-action evidence must exercise whichever path closes. |

### `OP-OPS-05`: Slot-deadline forging SLA (operational, not hash-critical)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md` §7 (OQ9). PHASE4-N-C new rule (`introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-C"`, `tier = "operational"`). Cross-refs `CN-CONS-06`, `CN-CONS-07`. |
| **Requirement** | Forge + self-accept + N2N hand-off must complete within the slot's deadline (1s on mainnet, smaller on testnets). Operational, not constitutional: missing the deadline costs a slot but does not violate a hash-critical invariant. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/scheduler.rs::scheduler_step` (full pipeline timing); `crates/ade_runtime/tests/producer_pipeline_slot_deadline.rs` (wall-clock measurement). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_runtime/tests/producer_pipeline_slot_deadline.rs::producer_full_path_under_slot_deadline_on_reference_fixture`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_scheduler_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-C-S6, anchored on `OP-OPS-05`) — defends the scheduler's closed pipeline shape (forge → self-accept → handoff is a single ordered transition; no out-of-band shortcut). The wall-clock SLA itself is operational; the test runs in CI but the deadline is a soft target, not a CI fail. |

---

## Named ingress chokepoint registry (cross-cutting, T-INGRESS-01 / DC-INGRESS-01 / CN-WIRE-06)

The full named-chokepoint list at HEAD `b9ff041`. `ci/ci_check_ingress_chokepoints.sh` enforces that raw CBOR decoding outside `ade_codec` is forbidden except at these named sites; Check 3 currently allowlists exactly the one non-`ade_codec` entry. Adding a new chokepoint requires (a) listing it in the script's header comment, (b) adding the corresponding path to the allowlist if it lives outside `ade_codec`, and (c) updating this table.

| # | Chokepoint | Crate | Surface |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | `decode_block_envelope` | `ade_codec` | Era-tagged block envelope |
| 2 | `decode_byron_ebb_block` | `ade_codec` | Byron EBB block CBOR |
| 3 | `decode_byron_regular_block` | `ade_codec` | Byron regular block CBOR |
| 4 | `decode_shelley_block` | `ade_codec` | Shelley block CBOR |
| 5 | `decode_allegra_block` | `ade_codec` | Allegra block CBOR |
| 6 | `decode_mary_block` | `ade_codec` | Mary block CBOR |
| 7 | `decode_alonzo_block` | `ade_codec` | Alonzo block CBOR |
| 8 | `decode_babbage_block` | `ade_codec` | Babbage block CBOR |
| 9 | `decode_conway_block` | `ade_codec` | Conway block CBOR |
| 10 | `decode_address` | `ade_codec` | Address CBOR (Byron/Shelley legacy + Shelley) |
| 11 | `PlutusScript::from_cbor` | `ade_plutus` | Plutus script CBOR (distinct surface from block CBOR; uses aiken/pallas internally) |

The PHASE4-N-B consensus surface does *not* introduce a new named-chokepoint entry — `EraSchedule` enters BLUE consensus as a typed-value parameter built from genesis text in RED (`crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/genesis_parser.rs`), not as a CBOR-decoded chokepoint, so the chokepoint registry above is unchanged.

---

## Repo-wide CI scripts not yet pinned to a rule

Three CI scripts under `ci/` enforce repo hygiene rather than a single
invariant. They are run on every push but do not appear in any rule's
CI row above:

| Script | What it enforces | Why it is not pinned to a registry rule |
|---|---|---|
| `ci/ci_check_no_secrets.sh` | No credentials, IPs, hostnames, or keys committed to the tree. | Project hygiene rule (per `MEMORY.md::feedback_no_credential_leaks.md`); not an invariant in the project constitution. Candidate for an `OP-SEC-*` entry in a future registry pass. |
| `ci/ci_check_pallas_quarantine.sh` | `pallas-*` references confined to `ade_plutus`. | Phase 2C obligation `O-29.2` (CODEMAP §CI enforcement table) — confines aiken/pallas transitive types to the quarantine crate. Candidate for a `CN-WIRE-*` strengthening or a new `DC-PLUTUS-*` entry. |
| `ci/git-hooks/commit-msg` | Local commit-msg hook rejects commits without `Co-Authored-By: Claude` trailer. | Per-repo IDD scaffolding (HEAD_DELTAS §5 second table). Not a constitution rule. Not applicable to TRACEABILITY as currently scoped. |

---

## Cross-references and consistency warnings

These warnings are surfaced for the parent's downstream review; they do
not block doc generation.

### A0000000000000000. PHASE4-N-I close — 4 NEW rules (3 enforced + 1 declared with open_obligation) + 1 flipped enforced (`DC-CONS-20` rollback-side closed, with 3 strengthening claims NOT yet in registry) + 2 new CI scripts; in-memory snapshot + replay-forward rollback (Path A recursive scope) closed; persistent on-disk encoding deliberately deferred to follow-on cluster

Cluster PHASE4-N-I (in-memory snapshot + replay-forward rollback, 6 slices
S1 → S6) closes the rollback-side half of `DC-CONS-20` — the outstanding
open obligation shipped by PHASE4-N-H — at HEAD `75f75da`. The registry
total moves to **206 rules** (+4 from N-I); the CI count moves to **54
scripts** (+2 from N-I). The cluster ships the Path A recursive scope
split (in-memory only); the persistent on-disk `LedgerState` encoder is
deliberately carved out to a follow-on cluster (`DC-CONS-21` stays
declared with an explicit `open_obligation`). Every N-I enforced rule
carries full `code_locus` / `tests` / `ci_script` populated arrays plus
bidirectional `cross_ref`s.

End-to-end proof: `rollback_then_continue_admit_equals_straight_line_admit` (snapshot+rollback yields the same ledger fingerprint as straight-line admit — snapshotting is a pure cache). |

obligations introduced by this cluster" as design intent. They are NOT
regressions — each is a genuine rollback-side reuse of the cited
authority surface, captured by the new `DC-CONS-22` / `CN-STORE-07` /
`DC-STORE-07` rules' `cross_ref` arrays (which all point back at
`T-DET-01`, `DC-PROTO-09`, `CN-CONS-08`). Surfacing for parent review:
either update the registry's `strengthened_in` arrays to match the
cluster doc's claims, OR amend the cluster doc to drop the
strengthening language and rely on cross_ref alone. The registry is the

**Open obligations (NOT mechanical gaps; deferred by cluster scope decisions):**

- **`DC-CONS-21` persistent-encoder follow-on —
  `persistent_ledger_snapshot_encoding_follow_on_cluster`.** Path A
  recursive scope split decision (OQ-3, locked at sketch close
  2026-05-26). The full canonical `LedgerState` encoder is ~1500-2000
  LoC of field-walk code mirroring `ade_ledger::fingerprint`'s
  structure and is too large to ship in one slice without risking
  partial-implementation bugs. This cluster therefore ships in-memory
  only: `InMemorySnapshotCache` uses `BTreeMap<SlotNo, (LedgerState,
  PraosChainDepState)>` value-clone, never invoking encode/decode.
  Rollback works fully **within a session** (ChainDb rollback + ledger
  replacement + chain_dep replacement + pending-header reset all
  happen atomically); across restarts, snapshots are lost. The
  follow-on persistent-encoder cluster closes that gap. `DC-CONS-21`
  stays `declared` until then. This is a deliberate scope split, NOT
  a regression — the same Path A discipline N-H used for rollback-side
  itself, applied one level deeper (N-I rollback-side closes; N-I's
  own persistent encoder is the next recursion).
