archived at HEAD `75f75da` (6 slice docs `N-I-S1.md` … `N-I-S6.md` +
`cluster.md`).

**Status:** closed at HEAD `75f75da` (mechanical half — CE-N-I-1..CE-N-I-6
all green in CI: closed sums + materialize driver + commit_rollback
atomicity + cadence + InMemorySnapshotCache + snapshot-write orchestration
+ receive-reducer wiring + end-to-end snapshot-is-cache proof). The
`DC-CONS-21` declared-with-open_obligation entry is the explicit
follow-on; no other open obligations. Evidence reproducible via
`cargo test -p ade_ledger rollback::` (BLUE rollback driver + commit +
materialize) + `cargo test -p ade_runtime --test rollback_end_to_end`
(end-to-end snapshot-is-cache proof) + `cargo test -p ade_runtime
rollback::` (GREEN cadence + in-memory cache + chaindb-block-source) +
`bash ci/ci_check_rollback_materialize_closure.sh` +
`bash ci/ci_check_snapshot_cadence_purity.sh` + `bash
ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` (expected: PASS, 206 entries).

  on any peer `RollBackward` and receive state stays consistent.
  `DC-CONS-20.status = "declared"` at cluster close, NOT a regression.

**Open obligations (NOT mechanical gaps; deferred by cluster scope decisions or by-design operator-action):**

  `ci_check_producer_corpus_present.sh`). The crypto-level live claim is

  operator-action live evidence: testnet (preview/preprod) SPO stake must

  precedent** (enforced + `open_obligation` for a follow-on operator-action
  artifact).
- **`OP-OPS-04` Sum6KES real cardano-cli skey loader.** `cardano-crypto 1.0.8`
  exposes `gen_key_kes_from_seed_bytes` but no `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`
  for `Sum6KES`; the keys loader currently round-trips synthetic seed-encoded
  skeys but does not yet load real cardano-cli's 612-byte expanded-tree
  `Sum6KES` serialization. Resolution: either upstream a `Sum6KES` deserializer,
  fork the parsing locally, or document the cardano-cli kes-skey conversion
  step in the operator workflow. CE-N-C-8 operator-action evidence must
  exercise whichever path closes.

**New CI script (PP-S1, anchored on `DC-LEDGER-11`):**

`ci/ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh` defends the closure mechanically with
five checks (see the `DC-LEDGER-11` CI row above for the precise enumeration):
(1) closed `ProposalProcedure` struct + 4-field shape; (2) typed
`ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` field (not `Option<Vec<u8>>`); (3)
`ade_codec::conway::governance` exports the typed decoder + encoder; (4) the
key-20 path on `ConwayTxBody` uses the typed decoder/encoder, never the opaque
pass-through; (5) no production `ProposalProcedure {` struct-literal construction
outside the sanctioned synthesis sites (production callers MUST go through
`decode_proposal_procedures`). Test code (`crates/*/tests/`, `#[cfg(test)] mod
tests` blocks) and the GREEN harness under `ade_testkit/` are exempt by design.

**OPEN OBLIGATIONS (recorded on `DC-LEDGER-11.open_obligation`, NOT mechanical gaps;
deferred by cluster scope decisions, NOT regressions):**

- **OQ-1 — `voting_procedures` (tx body key 19) closure.** The natural sibling
  cluster: same opaque-bytes shape, same pressure, deliberately deferred. This
  rule does **NOT** cover key 19; a future cluster (`VOTING-PROCEDURES-DECODE` or
  similar) is the recommended next discriminant work.
- **OQ-2 — `ParameterChange.update` nested opacity.** `ParameterChange` is a
  closed `GovAction` arm at PP-S1, but its inner `update` payload remains opaque
  bytes (the protocol-parameter-update sub-grammar is its own future closure
  decision). A future `strengthened_in += <ppupdate-cluster>` candidate.
- **OQ-3 — `NewConstitution.raw` nested opacity.** Same shape as OQ-2: the arm
  is closed at PP-S1, the inner `raw` payload is opaque bytes; a future
  `strengthened_in` candidate when that sub-grammar is closed.
- **OQ-4 — Typed `RewardAccount` for `proposal_procedure.return_addr`.** A
  separate fidelity decision — `return_addr` is currently bytes (`RewardAccount`
  as encoded); typing it (`Network` + `StakeCredential`) is a separate cluster.

None of these are mechanical CI gaps in this cluster's scope — the gates discharge
exactly what `DC-LEDGER-11` was scoped to defend (the outer `proposal_procedures`
list + each procedure's 4-tuple + the closed `GovAction` dispatch). The nested
opacities are scoped to future siblings by explicit OQ resolution.

**Documented deposit/refund value-conservation gap (known gap; see §H):**
PHASE4-B2-S4 found and fixed a real fail-open — the Conway state-backed path never checked coin-level value conservation, so `outputs + fee != inputs` was accepted as `Valid` at `track_utxo=true`. The fix (`crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation`) enforces `sum(inputs) == sum(outputs) + fee + donation` for **cert/withdrawal-free** txs. Full preservation-of-value with deposit/refund/withdrawal accounting is **deferred**: the check conservatively skips txs carrying certificates or withdrawals (so it never false-rejects), which means a mis-accounted deposit/refund/withdrawal tx is not yet caught on value grounds. This is a tx-validity-completeness item against `T-CONSERV-01` / `CN-LEDGER-07`. Recorded in `MEMORY.md::project_value_conservation_deposits_deferred.md` and in `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs`. Surfaced in §G and §H.

**Status:** closed. CE-B2 evidence reproducible via
`cargo test -p ade_ledger --test tx_witness_closure`,
`--test tx_validity_compose`,
`--test tx_validity_positive_corpus`,
`--test tx_validity_adversarial_corpus`,
`--test mempool_admission`; `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` PASSES (168 entries).

| `DC-CRYPTO-01` | enforced (strengthened); `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B1"]` | Praos single-VRF input + leader/nonce range extension; op-cert-signable format fix; `kes_check.rs` wiring; 14/14 real Conway headers pass leader check |
| `DC-CONSENSUS-02` | partial (strengthened); `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-N-B", "PHASE4-B1"]` | added ledger-side `consensus_view.rs` `LedgerView` projection + `consensus_view` tests |
| `DC-LEDGER-02` | partial (strengthened); `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B1"]` | added GREEN no-false-accept adversarial corpus (`adversarial.rs`, `no_mutation_is_ever_valid`) |
| `CN-CONS-04` | declared (strengthened); `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-N-B", "PHASE4-B1"]` | recomputed segwit body-hash binding (`block_validity/{transition,header_input}.rs`) + VRF-keyhash binding + KES authentication (`kes_check.rs`) |
| `CN-EPOCH-01` | partial (strengthened); `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-N-B", "PHASE4-B1"]` | added ledger-side `consensus_view.rs` epoch-projection + `consensus_view` tests |

**Documented Conway body-witness verification gap (known gap, fenced; to close in B2):**
The adversarial corpus mutator M6 (forge a witness, then patch the header `body_hash`
to the mutated body) lands fail-closed at `HeaderInvalid` (KES) because the KES
signature signs the header body — which includes `body_hash` — and the header
pipeline runs before the body authority. So a forged spend cannot pass
`block_validity` by any byte mutation of a real block. **However**, when the inner
block is fed *directly* to `ade_ledger::rules::apply_block_with_verdicts` for a
Conway block (bypassing the header, which a real chain never does), the fabricated
vkey witness is **not** rejected — the Conway body authority runs structural +
Plutus dispatch without per-tx Ed25519 vkey-witness verification. This is **not
reachable through `block_validity`** (the header fences it), so it is not a CE-B1-4
false-accept, but it is a genuine pre-release finding against the witness-verification
invariant (`DC-LEDGER-05` / `CN-LEDGER-09`). Recorded in
`crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (M6 doc comment) and
`corpus/validity/adversarial/README.md` (§ "Separate, deeper note"). **Scheduled for
B2 (tx validity).** Not double-recorded as a registry gap because it lives outside the
`block_validity` authority surface B1 closed; surfaced here in §G.

**Discrepancy note (prompt vs registry):** the close summary listed `T-ENC-01` among
the PHASE4-B1 strengthenings, but the registry `T-ENC-01` entry carries no
`PHASE4-B1` in `strengthened_in` (it remains `status = "partial"` with no
`strengthened_in` field). No change was made to the `T-ENC-01` rule entry above. See §G #6.

**Status:** closed. CE-B1 evidence reproducible via
`cargo test -p ade_ledger --test block_validity_compose`,
`--test block_validity_positive_corpus`, `--test block_validity_adversarial_corpus`,
`cargo test -p ade_core --test praos_header_validate`,
`cargo test -p ade_ledger --test consensus_view`.

### B. `DC-STORE-04` Tier 5 divergence (documented, not a gap)

`DC-STORE-04` literally describes cardano-node's three-DB architecture
(ImmutableDB + VolatileDB + LedgerDB). Ade has deliberately diverged
per CE-79 Tier 5 (intentional-divergence on non-hash-critical
operator-facing surfaces, per `MEMORY.md::feedback_diverge_on_internal_surfaces.md`):
a single redb-backed store with logical separation via key prefixes
(`slots_by_hash`, `hashes_by_slot`, `snapshots_by_slot`) under
`crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/persistent.rs`.

The **semantic guarantees** that DC-STORE-04 was designed to deliver —
append-only finalized data and atomic snapshots — survive in Ade and
are now mechanically enforced under `DC-STORE-02` and `DC-STORE-03`
respectively, both flipped `declared → enforced` in `78da6c9`. The rule
remains `status = "declared"` in the registry rather than `enforced`
because Ade does not implement the literal three-DB topology DC-STORE-04
names; per IDD discipline, rules are append-only and may only be
strengthened, not weakened or repointed. A future `DC-STORE-04A`
strengthening (or a deprecation event paired with a major version bump)
is the legal way to reclassify.

This is recorded in the registry as a comment block above the
`DC-STORE-04` entry (commit `78da6c9`), in the `DC-STORE-04` row above,
and here in §B. **It does not read as an enforcement gap.** It is a
documented Tier 5 divergence with the semantic guarantee preserved
elsewhere and mechanically enforced.

  HEAD_DELTAS §5.

  PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE cluster directory was moved from
  `docs/clusters/PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE/` to

  `PP-S1.md`, `PP-S2.md`), joining the already-archived PHASE4-N-E (caa5ce8
  refresh), COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY, DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY,

  PHASE4-B3, ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK. The only in-flight cluster
  directory under `docs/clusters/` is `PHASE4-N-B/` (kept active as a
  cross-reference). The registry itself does not reference cluster paths (only
  cluster IDs via the `introduced_in` / `strengthened_in` fields), so no
  registry edit is required for the move. The new `DC-LEDGER-11` entry carries
  `introduced_in = "PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE"` (the cluster ID, not a path).

  using the archive path, no edit needed. The Generation Notes block above
  was updated to use the archive paths.

  in the tree, except where the field is empty (which is recorded
  above as a gap rather than a misreference).

(anchored on `DC-CONS-14`, S3), `ci/ci_check_no_producer_body_encoder.sh` (anchored
on `T-ENC-01` + `DC-CONS-16`, S4), `ci/ci_check_self_accept_gate.sh` (anchored on
`CN-CONS-07`, S5), `ci/ci_check_scheduler_closure.sh` (anchored on `OP-OPS-05`, S6),

§5 at its prior narrated HEAD (`928c2be`) lists none of these eight, narrates none of
the PHASE4-N-C cluster thread, and is being regenerated in parallel with this
TRACEABILITY refresh — §5 should grow from 32 → 40 scripts and the PHASE4-N-C cluster
narrative should be added (S1 RED signing primitives + cardano-cli skey loader, S2
opcert validate + closed encoder, S3 BLUE forge core + ProducerTick + tx-admissibility

open_obligation).

All 40 active CI scripts under `ci/ci_check_*.sh` at HEAD `694dd74` appear in at
least one rule's CI row above except the three repo-hygiene scripts listed in

`ci/ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh`, the rule is `enforced`, and

### F. SEAMS cross-check

`docs/ade-SEAMS.md` exists at HEAD (`5b70bee` baseline). No closed
registry referenced from rule Source fields above was found to be
missing from SEAMS §3 in the spot checks performed during this refresh.
A full SEAMS regeneration is recommended after the next
`/seams` invocation to pick up the PHASE4-N-B closed enums
(`ChainEvent`, `ChainSelectionReject`, `HeaderValidationError`,
`OpCertCounterError`, `NonceError`, the closed `NonceInput` /
`RollBackRequest` / `StreamInput` input enums, the typed
`EraSchedule` and `BootstrapAnchorHash` values) as closed registries, plus the
PHASE4-B1 closed taxonomies in `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/verdict.rs`
(the closed `Valid`/`Invalid` block verdict enum and the `FieldKind`/`FieldError`
fail-closed field taxonomy) — none of which appear in SEAMS §3 at the current baseline.
**PHASE4-B2 staleness:** SEAMS still lists the seam "B2 (tx validity)" and "N-E (mempool)"
as `candidate` / `proposed` future attach points — both are now *realized* in `ade_ledger`
(`tx_validity/` and `mempool/`), not deferred. SEAMS §3 also does not yet carry the new
PHASE4-B2 closed registries: `TxValidityVerdict` / `TxRejectClass` / `TxValidityError`,
the closed era-versioned `SignerSource` enum, `WitnessClosureError`, and the mempool
`AdmitOutcome` / `OrderPolicy`. A `/seams` regeneration is recommended to reclassify the
B2/N-E seams from candidate to closed and to register these enums.

### G. Open questions for the user

1. **`DC-CONS-09` and `DC-CONS-10` have no dedicated CI script.** Both
   are marked `status = "enforced"` via test surface only. Worth
   considering whether (a) the existing `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`
   already discharges them structurally (current implicit answer), or
   (b) a new narrow CI script — e.g. a corpus replay gate — should be
   added. No action taken in this refresh.
2. **`DC-CONSENSUS-02` registry status is `partial` with empty `ci_script`.**
   The leader-schedule corpus tests + structural CIs discharge it
   de-facto, but no dedicated `ci/ci_check_leader_schedule.sh` exists.
   Recommend adding one or accepting the de-facto discharge.
3. **`CN-CONS-04` (header/body binding) `code_locus` and `tests`
   populated but `ci_script` empty.** Same de-facto pattern as above —
   `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` keeps `HeaderValidationError`
   closed but no dedicated header-validate CI exists.
4. **CN-EPOCH-01 newly flipped to `partial`** with consensus-side
   evidence; ledger-side `epoch.rs`/`governance.rs` evidence also
   exists via `DC-LEDGER-04`. Consider unifying under a single CI gate
   or accepting the split.
5. **`ade_core` CODEMAP entry needs a substantial rewrite** — the
   "empty placeholder" classification is no longer accurate (16 BLUE
   consensus modules under `src/consensus/`, +`kes_check.rs` from B1). The
   next `/codemap` refresh will fix this, but the gap is worth flagging now.
6. **All six `DC-VAL-*` rules are `status = "enforced"` with empty
   `ci_script`.** They are proven by their test surface (positive +
   adversarial corpora, compose tests) and discharged structurally by
   `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` / `ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` /
   `ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`, but **no dedicated
   `ci/ci_check_block_validity.sh` exists**. The CE-B1-4 no-false-accept
   property (`no_mutation_is_ever_valid`) and the 14/14 positive-corpus
   property (`all_corpus_blocks_valid`) currently have no CI gate. Recommend
   a single block-validity corpus CI gate, or accept the de-facto discharge.
7. **`DC-VAL-06`'s fail-open-pattern ban is not text-scanned.** The rule
   forbids `if X.len() == K { check } else { skip }` in BLUE validation, but
   no CI script greps for that pattern — it is proven only by the adversarial
   corpus. Strong candidate for a new `ci/ci_check_no_fail_open_len_guard.sh`.
8. **Conway body-witness verification gap — CLOSED in PHASE4-B2-S1 (CE-B2-1).**
   Previously: the Conway body authority did not perform per-tx Ed25519
   vkey-witness verification when reached directly (bypassing the header). Now
   wired into the body path via
   `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs::verify_required_witnesses`
   (L78) — called from `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs:258` and `:342` through
   `verify_conway_witness_closure` — with the closed era-versioned `SignerSource`
   enumeration in `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs`
   covering every signer source (resolved inputs, explicit required-signers,
   cert/withdrawal/voter/collateral). Discharged by `DC-LEDGER-05` /
   `CN-LEDGER-09` / `DC-TXV-05` (all carry `strengthened_in += PHASE4-B2`),
   the 20-test `tx_witness_closure` suite, and `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`
   over `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/`. **CLOSED — no further action.**
9. **`T-ENC-01` strengthening discrepancy.** The PHASE4-B1 close summary
   named `T-ENC-01` as strengthened, but the registry entry shows no
   `PHASE4-B1` in `strengthened_in` and remains `partial`. Either the
   registry needs `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B1"]` (if B1 genuinely touched
   the canonical-encoding surface) or the close summary overstated. No edit
   was made to the `T-ENC-01` rule entry pending user judgment.

   ["PHASE4-B1", "PHASE4-B2"]` on `T-ENC-01` and a non-empty B1/B2 `code_locus`,
   so the discrepancy is closed — B1/B2 genuinely touched the canonical-encoding
   surface (block body hash; `tx_id` over preserved bytes). The rule remains
   `partial` (canonical-encoding coverage incomplete), not a regression.
10. **Deposit/refund value-conservation gap — CLOSED in PHASE4-B3-S4.**
    Previously: the Conway coin-conservation check
    (`crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation`)
    conservatively skipped txs carrying certificates or withdrawals, so a
    mis-accounted deposit/refund/withdrawal tx was not rejected on value
    grounds. The early-out is **gone**: the source comment at the function
    header (L164–166) records "PHASE4-B3-S4 removed the deposit/withdrawal
    early-out that was the cluster's known false-accept path", and the full
    Conway preservation-of-value equation
    (`Σ(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == Σ(outputs) + fee + donation + new_deposits`)
    now runs for cert/withdrawal-bearing Conway txs with deposit amounts
    sourced canonically via `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-07`. Proven by
    `conway_conservation_full`, `conservation_early_out_removed`, the
    adversarial conservation corpus, and the positive corpora (real + synthetic);
    discharged on `T-CONSERV-01` (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B3`),
    `CN-LEDGER-07`, `DC-VAL-06` (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B3, PHASE4-B3F`).
    See §H (kept for historical provenance). **CLOSED — no further action.**

21. **OQ-5 — credential key/script discriminant collapse — RESOLVED in OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY.**
    The B5-declared OQ-5 follow-up has graduated into the enforced rule `DC-LEDGER-10`:
    `StakeCredential` is now the closed sum `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}`, both era decoders
    preserve the tag (unknown rejects), `CertState`/`ConwayGovState` key on the
    discriminated credential, and `fingerprint::write_stake_credential` serializes the
    discriminant. CI-guarded by `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` (PASSES
    at HEAD `a3ee2da`). What remains is a real-chain oracle (environment-blocked, §G #23)
    plus declared non-goals (committee member/vote discrimination; the `Hash28`-keyed
    stake-distribution snapshot; the Byron credential surface) — bounded scope items,
    not the collapse itself. **CLOSED.** Original B5 framing follows for the record:
    **OQ-5 — credential key/script discriminant collapse in `ConwayGovState` keys
    (pre-existing decoder behaviour, newly promoted to authority by B5).** `ConwayGovState`
    keys gov state on bare `Hash28`; the codec `ade_codec` `decode_stake_credential` drops
    the credential type tag, so a key-hash and a script-hash credential sharing the same 28
    bytes are indistinguishable in `vote_delegations` / `committee_hot_keys` / `drep_expiry`.
    cardano-node keys on the full discriminated `Credential`. This is NOT introduced by B5
    — it is pre-existing decoder behaviour that B5 newly promotes into governance authority.
    The 28-byte collision is not cheaply forgeable; carrying the discriminant into
    `StakeCredential`/`DRep` is a separate cross-cutting follow-up touching the whole
    credential surface, tracked per the per-cluster security review. Confirm whether OQ-5
    is carried as a future cross-cutting credential-discriminant cluster.

    PHASE4-N-I ships in-memory snapshot storage only; `InMemorySnapshotCache` uses
    `BTreeMap<SlotNo, (LedgerState, PraosChainDepState)>` value-clone, never invoking

    field-walk code mirroring `ade_ledger::fingerprint`'s structure) is deliberately
    carved out to a follow-on cluster. Rollback works fully within a session
    (`DC-CONS-20` enforced); across restarts, snapshots are lost. The in-memory scope still
    closes `CN-STORE-07`, `DC-CONS-22`, `DC-STORE-07`, and `DC-CONS-20` fully; persistence
    across restarts is the follow-on cluster's deliverable, NOT a regression. This is the
    same Path A discipline N-H used for rollback-side itself, applied one level deeper.
    Confirm whether the persistent-encoder follow-on is carried as an entry-condition proof
    obligation on a future cluster (recommended: `LEDGER-SNAPSHOT-PERSISTENT` or similar)
    or accepted as `open_obligation` until further notice. Recorded in `DC-CONS-21`'s
    registry entry.

## H. Value-conservation completeness gap — CLOSED in PHASE4-B3 (tracked against T-CONSERV-01 / CN-LEDGER-07)

> **Status (HEAD `168ac02`, refresh):** **CLOSED** — kept as a historical
> provenance entry only. This refresh removes the gap's two carry-forward
> paragraphs from the PHASE4-B2 / PHASE4-B1 close summaries above (no
> back-reference from the live-code narrative); §G #10 is reclassified
> CLOSED with explicit code citation. The cert/withdrawal early-out was
> removed from `check_conway_coin_conservation` in PHASE4-B3-S4 (source
> comment at `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs:164-166` explicitly records
> "PHASE4-B3-S4 removed the deposit/withdrawal early-out that was the
> cluster's known false-accept path"); the **full** Conway preservation-of-
> value equation (`Σ(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == Σ(outputs) + fee +
> donation + new_deposits`) now runs for cert/withdrawal-bearing Conway txs,
> with deposit/refund amounts sourced canonically (`DC-TXV-06` closed/total
> cert-deposit classification + `DC-TXV-07` canonical deposit-param
> authority). Proven by `conway_conservation_full`,
> `conservation_early_out_removed`, the adversarial conservation corpus
> (`adversarial_imbalanced_via_{deposit,withdrawal}`,
> `adversarial_no_false_accept`), and the positive corpora (real + synthetic).
> The historical description below is retained for provenance only.

PHASE4-B2-S4 (`crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs`) fixed a real fail-open and
introduced `check_conway_coin_conservation`, which enforces
`sum(inputs) == sum(outputs) + fee + donation` for **certificate- and
withdrawal-free** Conway transactions. This closes the pure-spend
value-conservation hole the tx adversarial corpus surfaced (a tx with
`outputs + fee != inputs` was previously accepted as `Valid` at `track_utxo=true`).

**Still deferred:** full preservation-of-value accounting —
`sum(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == sum(outputs) + fee + deposits + donation`.
The current check **conservatively skips** txs that carry certificates or
withdrawals (so it can never false-*reject* them), which means a mis-accounted
deposit/refund/withdrawal tx is not yet caught on value grounds. Other checks
may still reject such a tx, but value conservation specifically would not.

This is the one **known, documented tx-validity-completeness gap** against the
value-preservation invariant (`T-CONSERV-01` — UTxO/asset conservation; mirrored
in the declared `CN-LEDGER-07`). It is **not** a silent gap: it is recorded in
`MEMORY.md::project_value_conservation_deposits_deferred.md` and in the
`conway.rs` source comment, and surfaced here and in §G #10. It does **not**
read as a `DC-TXV-*` enforcement gap (those rules close the verdict/witness/total-
evolution surface, all `enforced`) — it is a completeness boundary on the
value-conservation half of phase-1, scoped conservatively so it never
false-rejects.

---

## What does NOT belong here

- Implementation details (those live in CODEMAP).
- Extension-point rules (those live in SEAMS).
- Change history (lives in HEAD_DELTAS).
- Project-management state (slice status, owner).

This doc is purely **rule → enforcement**.

Every `_(no enforcement found — gap)_` line corresponds to a registry
`code_locus`/`tests`/`ci_script` field that is empty for an entry whose
`status` is `declared`, `partial`, or where a cross-referenced rule is
itself a gap. Closing a gap means populating the registry; the next
TRACEABILITY regeneration will lift the gap automatically.

`DC-STORE-04`'s rows are intentionally **not** marked gaps — see §B for
the documented Tier 5 divergence rationale.
